      <li>Izulu lixela ubulungisa bakhe, Ngokuba uThixo eza kugweba yena. (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Yivani, bantu bam, ndithethe; Sirayeli, ndiqononondise kuwe; NdinguThixo, uThixo wakho.</li>
      <li>Andikohlwayi ngenxa yemibingelelo yakho, Namadini akho anyukayo aphambi kwam amaxesha onke.</li>
      <li>Andiyi kuthabatha zinkunzi zankomo endlwini yakho,  Nazinkunzi zabhokhwe esibayeni sakho.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba zezam zonke iinyamakazi zehlathi, Neenkomo ezisezintabeni eziliwaka.</li>
      <li>Iintaka zonke zasezintabeni ndiyazazi, Nento edakasa endle inam.</li>
      <li>Ukuba bendilambile, ndibe ndingayi kukuxelela; Ngokuba lelam elimiweyo nenzaliseko yalo.</li>
      <li>Ndidle inyama yeenkunzi eziziimbalasane na? Ndisele igazi leenkunzi zeebhokhwe na?</li>
      <li>Bingelela kuYehova umbulelo, Uzizalise kOsenyangweni izibhambathiso zakho;</li>
      <li>Ubize mna ngemini yembandezelo, Ndikuhlangule, undizukise.</li>
      <li>Ke kongendawo uthi uThixo, Useke phi na wena ukuxela ummiselo wam, Uwuphathe ngomlomo wakho umnqophiso wam,</li>
      <li>Uyithiyile nje intethiso wena, Uwaphose nje amazwi am emva kwakho?</li>
      <li>Xa ubona isela, ukholana nalo, Wabelane nabakrexezi.</li>
      <li>Umlomo wakho uwuyekela ebubini; Ulwimi lwakho luthungela inkohliso;</li>
      <li>Uthi uhlale uthethe ngomzalwana wakho, Uhlaze umntwana kanyoko.</li>
      <li>Uzenzile ezo nto, ndathi tu, Waba ndinjengawe. Ndiya kukohlwaya ndizicwangcise emehlweni akho.</li>
      <li>Khaniqonde ke oko, nina bamlibalayo uThixo, Hleze ndiqwenge, kungabikho uhlangulayo.</li>
      <li>Obingelela umbulelo uyandizukisa, Alungise indlela,  Endombonisa kuyo usindiso lukaThixo.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide: ekuzeni kukaNatan umprofeti kuye, emveni kokuba ebengene uBhatshebha. Tarhu, Thixo,  ngokwenceba yakho! Ngokobuninzi benceba yakho, cima ukreqo lwam!</li>
      <li>Ndixovule kunene, busuke ubugwenxa bam, Undihlambulule esonweni sam.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba ndiyalwazi mna ukreqo lwam, Nesono sam siphambi kwam ngamaxesha onke.</li>
      <li>Ndonile kuwe, kuwe wedwa, Ndenza okubi emehlweni akho;  Ukuze ube lilungisa ekuthetheni kwakho, Ucace ekugwebeni kwakho.</li>
      <li>Uyabona, ndizalelwe ebugwenxeni, Ndakhawulwa nguma esonweni.</li>
      <li>Uyabona, ufuna inyaniso ezintsweni, Esitheni undazisa ubulumko.</li>
      <li>Ndihlambulule isono ngehisope, ndihlambuluke; Ndixovule,  ndibe mhlophe kunekhephu;</li>
      <li>Ndivise imihlali nemivuyo, Agcobe amathambo owacolileyo.</li>
      <li>Sithelisa ubuso bakho ezonweni zam, Ubucime bonke ubugwenxa bam.</li>
      <li>Dala phakathi kwam, Thixo, intliziyo ehlambulukileyo,  Uhlaziye umoya oqinisekileyo phakathi kwam.</li>
      <li>Musa ukundilahla ebusweni bakho, UMoya wakho oyiNgcwele ungamsusi kum.</li>
      <li>Buyisela kum imihlali yosindiso lwakho, Undixhase ngomoya wentumekelelo.</li>
      <li>Ndobafundisa abangendawo iindlela zakho, Babuyele kuwe aboni.</li>
      <li>Ndihlangule emagazini, Thixo, Thixo ondisindisayo;  Lomemelela ngobulungisa bakho ulwimi lwam.</li>
      <li>Nkosi yam, vula imilebe yomlomo wam, Uyixele indumiso yakho umlomo wam.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba akunanze mibingelelo, bendiya kukunika; Akalikholo kuwe amadini anyukayo.</li>
      <li>Imibingelelo kaThixo ngumoya owaphukileyo, Intliziyo eyaphukileyo, etyumkileyo, Thixo, akuyi kuyidela.</li>
      <li>Yenzele okulungileyo iZiyon ngokukholekileyo kuwe; Yakha iindonga zeYerusalem.</li>
      <li>Kuya kwandula ukuba mnandi kuwe imibingelelo yobulungisa,  amadini apheleleyo; Ziya kwandula ukunyuswa iinkunzi ezintsha zeenkomo esibingelelweni sakho.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli. Eyokuqiqa: ekaDavide: oko uDowegi umEdom waya waxelela uSawule, wathi kuye, UDavide ungene endlwini ka-Ahimeleki. Uqhayiselani na ngobubi, wena gorha? Inceba kaThixo ikho imihla yonke.</li>
      <li>Ulwimi lwakho lucinga ukweyelisela, Njengesitshetshe sokuguya iindevu esiloliweyo, wena mkhohlisi.</li>
      <li>Uthanda okubi kunokulungileyo; Ubuxoki, kunokuthetha ubulungisa. (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Uthanda onke amazwi aginyayo, Lulwimindini lukhohlisayo.</li>
      <li>Naye uThixo uya kukudiliza kuphele; Uva kukuxwila,  akuncothule ententeni, Akudonyule ezweni labaphilileyo.  (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Obona amalungisa, oyike, Amhleke, athi,</li>
      <li>Nanko umfo ongamenzanga igwiba lakhe uThixo, Owakholosa ngobuninzi bobutyebi bakhe, Waba nengcwangu ekweyeliseleni kwakhe.</li>
      <li>Ke mna ndinjengomnquma oluhlaza endlwini kaThixo;  Ndikholose ngenceba kaThixo ngonaphakade kanaphakade.</li>
      <li>Ndiya kubulela kuwe ngonaphakade, kuba ukwenzile oku; Ndiya kuthemba igama lakho, ngokuba lilungile, phambi kwabenceba bakho.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli: ngeyokhuzo. Eyokuqiqa; ekaDavide. Sithi isidenge entliziyweni yaso, Akukho Thixo. Bonakalisile,  balisikizi ngobugqwetha babo; Akukho wenza okulungileyo.</li>
      <li>UThixo esemazulwini uqondele koonyana babantu, Ukubona ukuba ukho na oqiqayo, Ofuna uThixo.</li>
      <li>Bonke babuye umva, bayimbozisa bephelele; Akukho wenza okulungileyo, Akukho nokuba abe mnye.</li>
      <li>Abanakwazi na abasebenzi bobutshinga, Abathi, bebadla abantu bam, bathi badla isonka, Bangamnquli uThixo?</li>
      <li>Apho bankwantya benkwantyile, phofu kungekho nto inkwantyisayo; Ngokuba uThixo wawathi saa amathambo omngqingi wakho; Wabadanisa, ngokuba uThixo ebebacekisile.</li>
      <li>Akwaba bekuvela eZiyon ukusindiswa kwamaSirayeli!  Ekubuyiseni kukaThixo abantu bakhe ekuthinjweni, Wogcoba uYakobi, avuye uSirayeli.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Eyokubethelwa ngezinto ezineentambo. Kumongameli.  Eyokuqiqa. EkaDavide: ekufikeni kwabaseZifi, bathi kuSawule,  UDavide akazimele phakathi kwethu na? Thixo, ndisindise ngegama lakho, Uligwebe ityala lam ngobugorha bakho.</li>
      <li>Thixo, yiva umthandazo wam; Wabekele indlebe amazwi omlomo wam.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba abasemzini basukela phezulu kum,  Nabanobungqwangangqwili bafuna umphefumlo wam; Abammisi uThixo phambi kwabo. (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Yabona, uThixo ngumncedi wam; INkosi yam ikwabasekela umphefumlo wam.</li>
      <li>Uya kubuyisela ububi kwabandilalelayo; Ngenyaniso yakho babhangise.</li>
      <li>Ndiya kubingelela kuwe ngokuqhutywa yintliziyo; Ndiya kubulela kwigama lakho, Yehova, kuba lilungile.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba lindihlangule embandezelweni yonke; Iliso lam libonela iintshaba zam.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli. Eyokubethelwa ngezinto ezineentambo.  Eyokuqiqa: ekaDavide. Wubekele indlebe umthandazo wam, Thixo,  Musa ukuzifihla esikhungweni sam.</li>
      <li>Ndibazele indlebe undiphendule. Ndiyaphaphatheka ekucamngceni kwam, ndincwine,</li>
      <li>Ngenxa yelizwi lotshaba, Ngenxa yokuxinzelelwa phantsi ngabangendawo; Ngokuba zindiqengqela ubutshinga, Ziyandisukela ngomsindo.</li>
      <li>Intliziyo yam iyazibhija-bhija phakathi kwam; Izothuso zokufa zindiwele.</li>
      <li>Ukoyika nokuthuthumela kundingene; Ndigutyungelwe kukududuzela.</li>
      <li>Ndathi, Andaba bendinamaphiko njengehobe! Bendiya kubaleka ndiye ndihlale!</li>
      <li>Nanko ndibalekela kude, Ndilalise entlango. (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Bendiya kukhawuleza, ndisinde Emoyeni ovuthuzayo naseluqhwitheleni.</li>
      <li>Tshabalalisa, Nkosi yam, yahlula ulwimi lwazo; Ngokuba ndibone ukugonyamela nokubambana phakathi komzi.</li>
      <li>Imini nobusuku bajikeleza ezindongeni zawo; Ubutshinga nokwaphula kuphakathi kwawo;</li>
      <li>Ukweyelisela kuphakathi kwawo; Endaweni yembutho yawo akusuki ukuxinezela nokukhohlisa.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba asilutshaba olu lundingcikivayo; Bendiya kukuthwala oko. Asingondithiyileyo lo uzikhulisayo kum; Bendiya kusithela kuye.</li>
      <li>Nguwe, mntu ubungumlingane wam, Ikholwane lam endazana nalo,</li>
      <li>Ebesicweya kamnandi, Siye endlwini kaThixo silihlokondiba eligcobayo.</li>
      <li>Ukufa makubaqubule, Mabehle baye kwelabafileyo besaphilile; Ngokuba ububi busemizini yabo phakathi kwabo.</li>
      <li>Mna ndinqula uThixo; UYehova uya kundisindisa.</li>
      <li>Ngokuhlwa, nakusasa, nasemini enkulu ndiya kucamngca,  ndincwine; Uya kuliva izwi lam.</li>
      <li>Uwukhulula umphefumlo wam unoxolo, ukuze bangasondeli kum,  Ngokuba baninzi abandichasayo.</li>
      <li>UThixo uya kuva, abaphendule, Uselokwamandulo ehleli,  (Phakamisani.) Abo bangenanguquko, Bangamoyikiyo uThixo.</li>
      <li>Babasa isandla abaxolelene nabo; Bahlambela umnqophiso wabo;</li>
      <li>Ubuthelezi njengamasi umlomo wabo, Ke yimfazwe intliziyo yabo. Athambile amazwi abongaphezu kweoli, Kanti aziintlangothi zekrele.</li>
      <li>Umthwalo wakho wulahlele kuYehova; yena wokuzimasa; Akayi kuliyekela ilungisa lishukunyiswe naphakade.</li>
      <li>Wena ke, Thixo, uya kubahlisela emngxunyeni wesihogo.  Abantu bamagazi nenkohliso abayi kuyiqingathisa imihla yabo; Ke mna ndikholose ngawe.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli; ngeyehobe elithe cwaka phakathi kwabakude.  EkaDavide. Eliligugu. Ukubanjwa kwakhe ngamaFilisti eGati.  Ndibabale, Thixo, ngokuba abantu bendizonda; Bandixinile,  besilwa yonke imini;</li>
      <li>Abandilalelayo bandizonda yonke imini, Ngokuba baninzi abalwa nam beziphakamisile.</li>
      <li>Mhlana ndinxunguphalayo mna, Ndokholosa ngawe.</li>
      <li>Ndiya kulidumisa ngoThixo ilizwi lakhe, Ndikholose ngoThixo, ndingoyiki; Inokundenza ntoni na inyama?</li>
      <li>Yonke imini bayawaphambanisa amazwi am; Zingam zonke iingcinga zabo zobubi.</li>
      <li>Baqukene, babonisele, Bona bagcine izithende zam, Ngokokuba belinde umphefumlo wam.</li>
      <li>Bengamatshinga nje, bosinda na? Zihlise ngomsindo izizwe,  Thixo.</li>
      <li>Ukuphalaphala kwam ukubhalile wena; Yitha iinyembezi zam entsubeni yakho; Azisencwadini yakho na?</li>
      <li>Ziya kubuya umva ke iintshaba zam, mhlana ndibizayo;  Ndiyakwazi oku, ukuba uThixo unam.</li>
      <li>Ndilidumisa ngoThixo ilizwi, Ndilidumisa ngoYehova ilizwi.</li>
      <li>Ndikholose ngoThixo, ndingoyiki; Unokundenza ntoni na umntu?</li>
      <li>Ziphezu kwam, Thixo, izibhambathiso zakho; Ndiya kuyizalisa kuwe imibingelelo yombulelo.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba uwuhlangule ekufeni umphefumlo wam, Iinyawo zam ekukhubekeni, Ukuba ndihambe phambi koThixo Ekukhanyeni kobomi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli; ngethi, Ungonakalisi. EkaDavide. Eliligugu:  ekumbalekeni kwakhe uSawule emqolombeni. Ndibabale, Thixo,  ndibabale; Ngokuba uzimela ngawe umphefumlo wam; Ndizimela esithunzini samaphiko akho, Kude kudlule inkxwaleko.</li>
      <li>Ndinqula uThixo Osenyangweni, UThixo ondifezelayo.</li>
      <li>Uya kuthuma esemazulwini andisindise, Emngcikiva nje ondizondayo; (Phakamisani.) UThixo uya kuthuma inceba yakhe nenyaniso yakhe.</li>
      <li>Umphefumlo wam uphakathi kweengonyama; Ndiya kulala phantsi nabafutha umlilo, Oonyana babantu abamazinyo aziintshuntshe neentolo, Ulwimi lwabo lulikrele elibukhali.</li>
      <li>Ziphakamisele ngaphezu kwamazulu, Thixo, Lube phezu kwehlabathi lonke uzuko lwakho.</li>
      <li>Isibatha basilungisele iinyawo zam; Bawugobile umphefumlo wam; Bandimbela isihogo, Beyela kuso ngokwabo. (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Izimasekile intliziyo yam, Thixo, izimasekile intliziyo yam; Ndiya kuvuma, ndiya kubetha uhadi.</li>
      <li>Vuka, luzuko lwam! Vukani, mrhubhe nohadi! Ndiya kusiphangela isifingo.</li>
      <li>Ndiya kubulela kuwe phakathi kwezizwe, Nkosi yam; Ndiya kukubethela uhadi phakathi kwezizwe.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba inkulu, yada yaya ezulwini, inceba yakho; Yada yesa esibhakabhakeni inyaniso yakho.</li>
      <li>Ziphakamisele ngaphezu kwezulu, Thixo, Lube phezu kwehlabathi lonke uzuko lwakho.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli; ngethi, Ungonakalisi. EkaDavide. Eliligugu.  Yinene na kodwa ukuba nithetha ubulungisa, nina bothixo?  Nigweba oonyana babantu ngokuthe tye?</li>
      <li>Hayi, entliziyweni nenza ngobugqwetha; Ezweni nilinganisela ukugonyamela kwezandla zenu.</li>
      <li>Abangendawo baphambukile kwasesizalweni; Bandwendwile kwasesiswini abathethi bamanga.</li>
      <li>Banobuhlungu obunjengobuhlungu benyoka, Njengephimpi elizenza isithulu, elivingca indlebe yalo;</li>
      <li>Ukuze lingaliva izwi labanyangi, Lababopha ngomabophe,  beziingcibi.</li>
      <li>Thixo, yaphula amazinyo abo emlonyeni wabo; Amabamba eengonyama ezintsha wavithe, Yehova.</li>
      <li>Mabaphalale njengamanzi equkuqela; Akuxuna iintolo zakhe,  mazinge zicutshiwe.</li>
      <li>Mababe njengenkumba ehamba inyibilika, Njengemva-mbilini yomfazi, engalibonanga ilanga.</li>
      <li>Zingekaziva iintsasa iimbiza zenu, Nokuba ikrwada inyama,  nokuba iza kuvuthwa, uyayiqweqwedisa.</li>
      <li>Liya kuvuya ilungisa, lakuyibona impindezelo; Liya kuzihlamba iinyawo zalo egazini longendawo,</li>
      <li>Athi umntu, Inene, ilungisa linesiqhamo; Inene, ukho uThixo ogwebayo ehlabathini.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli; ngethi, Ungonakalisi. EkaDavide. Eliligugu:  ekuthumeleni kukaSawule, bayilinda indlu ukuba bambulale.  Ndihlangule ezintshabeni zam, Thixo wam, Ndise engxondeni kwabasukela phezulu kum.</li>
      <li>Ndihlangule kubasebenzi bobutshinga; Ndisindise ebantwini abanamagazi.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba nabo bewulalela umphefumlo wam; Baqukana ngam abanamandla, Kungekho lukreqo kum, kungekho sono kum, Yehova.</li>
      <li>Ndingenabugwenxa nje, bagidime baxhoba. Vuka,  undikhawulele, ubone.</li>
      <li>Wena Yehova, Thixo wemikhosi, Thixo kaSirayeli, Phapha,  uzivelele zonke iintlanga; Musa ukubayeka bonke abanginizayo bengabagqithi. (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Bayabuya ngokuhlwa, bayavungama njengezinja,  Bawuhamba-hambe umzi.</li>
      <li>Nabo belephuza amagwebu ngomlomo; Ngamakrele emlonyeni wabo; Ngokuba bathi, Kuva bani na?</li>
      <li>Wena, Yehova, uyabahleka, Uyazigculela zonke iintlanga.</li>
      <li>Mandla am, ndiva kulindela kuwe; Ngokuba uThixo uyingxonde yam.</li>
      <li>UThixo wam uya kundikhawulela ngenceba yakhe; UThixo uya kundibonisa abandilaleleyo.</li>
      <li>Musa ukubabulala, hleze balibale abantu bakowethu;  Babhadulise ngamandla akho, ubawise, Ngweletshetshe yethu,  Nkosi yethu.</li>
      <li>Isono somlomo wabo lilizwi lemilebe yomlomo wabo;  Mababanjiswe likratshi labo, Nangenxa yokushwabula nokuhanahanisa abakuthethayo.</li>
      <li>Bagqibe ngobushushu; gqiba, bangabi sabakho; Baqonde ukuba uThixo ngumlawuli kwaYakobi, Wesa eziphelweni zehlabathi.  (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Bayabuya ngokuhlwa, bayavungama njengezinja,  Bawuhamba-hambe umzi.</li>
      <li>Bona babhadulela ukudla; Ukuba bathe abahlutha, balala apho.</li>
      <li>Ke mna, ndiya kuvuma ngamandla akho, Ndimemelele kwakusasa ngenceba yakho, Kuba ubuyingxonde kum, Nendawo endisabela kuyo ngemini yokubandezelwa kwam.</li>
      <li>Mandla am, ndiya kukubethela uhadi; Ngokuba uThixo yingxonde yam, nguThixo wam onenceba.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli; ngeyenyibiba yesingqino. Eliligugu.  EkaDavide. Eyokufundisa: ekulweni kwakhe nama-Aram phakathi kweMilambo nama-Aram aseTsobha; wabuya uYowabhi, wawabulala amaEdom emfuleni wetyuwa, amawaka alishumi elinamabini.  Thixo,  usihlambile, wasichitha, Waqumba; ngamana wasibuyisa.</li>
      <li>Ulinyikimisile ilizwe, ulikrazule; Philisa iintanda zalo ngokuba lishukuma.</li>
      <li>Ubabonisile abantu bakho into elukhuni, Usiseze iwayini ehexisayo.</li>
      <li>Ubanike ibhanile abakoyikayo, Ukuba bayiphakamise ngenxa yenyaniso. (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Ukuze zihlangulwe iintanda zakho, Sindisa ngesandla sakho sokunene, undiphendule.</li>
      <li>UThixo uthethe engcwele: mandivuyelele, Ndimabe uShekem,  ndiyilinganisele intili yaseSukoti.</li>
      <li>Ngowam uGiliyadi, ngowam uManase, UEfrayim sisigcina-ntloko sam, UYuda yintonga yam yommiselo;</li>
      <li>UMowabhi sisitya sam sokuhlambela, Ndiyiphosa kuEdom imbadada yam; Filisti, nkqangaza wena ngam.</li>
      <li>Ngubani na owondisa emzini wamandla? Ngubani na owondikhaphela kwaEdom?</li>
      <li>Asinguwe na, kwawena Thixo, osihlambileyo? Akwaphuma,  Thixo, nemikhosi yethu.</li>
      <li>Sincede kumbandezeli wethu; Alunto yanto usindiso lomntu.</li>
      <li>NgoThixo siya kweyisa, Wobagqusha yena ababandezeli bethu.</li>
    </ol>

  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli; eyokubethelwa ngezinto ezineentambo.  EkaDavide. Kuve, Thixo, ukuhlahlamba kwam; Wubazele indlebe umthandazo wam.</li>
      <li>Ndidanduluka kuwe ndisesiphelweni sehlabathi, ekutyhafeni kwentliziyo yam; Ndikhaphele eweni elisemalengalengeni kum.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba ulihlathi lam, Uyinqaba ende eliqele phambi kotshaba.</li>
      <li>Ndiya kuphambukela ententeni yakho ngonaphakade, Ndiya kuzimela ngesithe lamaphiko akho. (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Ngokuba wena, Thixo, uzivile izibhambathiso zam; Ubanike ilifa abaloyikayo igama lakho.</li>
      <li>Uya kongeza imihla emihleni yokumkani; Iminyaka yakhe iya kuba njengezizukulwana ngezizukulwana;</li>
      <li>Uya kuhlala ngonaphakade phambi koThixo; Mmisele inceba nenyaniso, ukuba zimlondoloze.</li>
      <li>Kukhona ndiya kulibethela uhadi igama lakho ngonaphakade,  Ndizizalise izibhambathiso zam imihla ngemihla.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli. KuYedutun. Umhobe kaDavide. Uthozamele kuThixo kwaphela umphefumlo wam; Kuvela kuye ukusindiswa kwam.</li>
      <li>Nguye kwaphela iliwa lam, umsindisi wam, Ingxonde yam;  andiyi kushukunyiswa kakhulu.</li>
      <li>Kunini na nisuka indulumbane emntwini? Kunini na nimncinitha nonke niphela, enjengodonga oluzimkayo,  enjengothango oluwayo?</li>
      <li>Bagqibe kwelokuba bamtyhale bamsuse ekuphakameni kwakhe kuphele; Bakholene namanga; Basikelela elowo ngomlomo,  embilinini yabo bayatshabhisa. (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Thozamela kuThixo yedwa, mphefumlo wam, Ngokuba livela kuye ithemba lam.</li>
      <li>Nguye kwaphela iliwa lam, umsindisi wam, Ingxonde yam;  andiyi kushukunyiswa.</li>
      <li>KunoThixo ukusindiswa kwam nozuko lwam; Iliwa lokunqaba kwam nehlathi lam likuThixo.</li>
      <li>Kholosani ngaye ngamaxesha onke, nina bantu; Phalazani intliziyo yenu phambi kwakhe. UThixo ulihlathi kuthi.  (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Bangumphunga kwaphela onyana boluntu, ngamanga oonyana bamadoda; Esikalini bangenyuka, Bangumphunga bephelele.</li>
      <li>Musani ukukholosa ngokudla abantu, Ningazenzi into engeyanto ngento exhakamfuliweyo. Yakwanda imfuyo, musani ukuyinyamekela.</li>
      <li>Uthethe nto-nye uThixo, Ezi zinto zimbini ndizivile: Ukuba amandla ngakaThixo,</li>
      <li>Nenceba yeyakho, Nkosi yam; Ngokuba uyababuyekeza, elowo ngokwezenzo zakhe.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Umhobe kaDavide: oko ebesentlango yakwaYuda. Thixo,  unguThixo wam, ndiya kukuquqela kwakusasa, Umphefumlo wam unxanele wena; inyama yam iyakulangazelela Ezweni elingumqwebedu, elibharhileyo, eligenamanzi.</li>
      <li>Ndenjenjalo ukukhangela kuwe engcweleni, Ukuba ndibone amandla akho nobuqaqawuli bakho.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba inceba yakho ilungile ngaphezu kobomi, Umlomo wam uya kukuncoma.</li>
      <li>Ndiya kwenjenjalo ukukubonga lo gama ndihleliyo,  Ndiphakamise izandla zam egameni lakho.</li>
      <li>Umphefumlo wam uhluthi umongo namanqatha; Ngemilebe yomlomo wam omemelelayo uya kukudumisa umlomo wam,</li>
      <li>Ndakukukhumbula emandlalweni wam, Emilindweni yobusuku ndicamanga ngawe.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba uluncedo kum, Ndinokumemelela esithunzini samaphiko akho.</li>
      <li>Umphefumlo wam uthene mbende nawe; Isandla sakho sokunene sindibambile.</li>
      <li>Ke bona bafuna umphefumlo wam ukuze batshabalale, Baya kutshona kwezisezantsi iindawo zehlabathi.</li>
      <li>Baphalazelwa emandleni ekrele; Baba sisabelo seempungutye.</li>
      <li>Ke yena ukumkani uya kuvuya ngoThixo; Baya kuqhayisa abo bonke bafunga yena; Ngokuba uya kuvingcwa umlomo wabathetha ubuxoki.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide. Live, Thixo, izwi lam ekukhalazeni kwam; Ekunkwantyiseni kotshaba bulondoloze ubomi bam.</li>
      <li>Ndisithelise egquguleni labanobubi, Ehlokondibeni labasebenzi bobutshinga;</li>
      <li>Abalulola njengekrele ulwimi lwabo, Abaxuna iintolo zabo,  amazwi akrakra,</li>
      <li>Bamtole ogqibeleleyo besentsithelweni; Bamtola ngesiquphe,  bangoyiki.</li>
      <li>Bazomelezela ilizwi elibi, Bagqiba kwelokuba bafihle izirhintyelo, Bathi, Singabonwa ngubani na?</li>
      <li>Baceba ubugqwetha; Baligqibile icebo abalicebileyo;  Imbilini yendoda nentliziyo yayo yinzulu.</li>
      <li>Ke uThixo uyabatola ngotolo; Amanxeba abo abakho ngesiquphe.</li>
      <li>Baya kukhutyekiswa, lufikele kwabona ulwimi lwabo;  Bayahlunguzela intloko bonke abababonayo.</li>
      <li>Basuka boyike bonke abantu, Bawuxele umsebenzi kaThixo,  Basiqiqe isenzo sakhe.</li>
      <li>Liya kuvuya ilungisa ngoYehova, lizimele ngaye, Baqhayise bonke abantliziyo zithe tye.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide. Ingoma. Ukuthozama kuyindumiso kuwe, Thixo, eZiyon; Sizaliswa kuwe isibhambathiso.</li>
      <li>Wena mphulaphuli wemithandazo, Iza kuwe inyama yonke.</li>
      <li>Zindoyisile nje iindawo zobugwenxa, Ukreqo lwethu uyaluxolela wena ngocamagushelo.</li>
      <li>Hayi, uyolo lomnyulayo, umsondeze Ukuba ahlale ezintendelezweni zakho! Siya kuzihluthisa ngokulunga kwendlu yakho, Kwetempile yakho engcwele.</li>
      <li>Usiphendula ngezenzo ezoyikekayo zobulungisa, Thixo osisindisayo; Nkoloseko yeziphelo zonke zehlabathi, neyolwandle olukude;</li>
      <li>Ulozinzisa iintaba ngamandla akhe, Ebhinqe ubugorha;</li>
      <li>Ulodambisa ukugquma kweelwandle, ukugquma kwamaza azo,  Nokuxokozela kwezizwe.</li>
      <li>Bayayoyika imiqondiso yakho abemi beziphelo zehlabathi.  Umemelelisa ukuvela kokusa nokuhlwa.</li>
      <li>Uwuvelele umhlaba, wawunyela, Wawutyebisa kakhulu. Umjelo kaThixo uzele ngamanzi: Walungisa ingqolowa yabo, ngokuba uwenjenje ukuwulungisa.</li>
      <li>Useza ihluthe imisele yawo; Unyakamisa imiqela yawo.  Uthambisa ngeziphango; Usikelela izilimo zawo.</li>
      <li>Uwuthwesile umnyaka wokulunga kwakho, Imikhondo yakho itsitsa ukutyeba.</li>
      <li>Ayatsitsa amakriwa entlango, Iinduli zizibhinqise umgcobo.</li>
      <li>Amadlelo anxibe imihlambi yeenkomo; Iintili zambethe ingqolowa. Yonke into iyaduma, yonke into iyavuma.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli. Ingoma. Umhobe. Dumani kuThixo, nonke hlabathi,</li>
      <li>Lubetheleni uhadi uzuko lwegama lakhe, Mzukiseni,  mdumiseni.</li>
      <li>Yithini kuThixo, Hayi, ukoyikeka kwemisebenzi yakho! Ngenxa yobuninzi bamandla akho ziya kuhanahanisa kuwe iintshaba zakho.</li>
      <li>Lonke ihlabathi liya kukunqula, Bakubethele uhadi;  Balibethele uhadi igama lakho. (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Yizani, nibone imisebenzi emikhulu kaThixo, Engowoyikekayo ekwenzeni kwakhe koonyana babantu.</li>
      <li>Waluguqula ulwandle lwayinto eyomileyo; Bawuwela umlambo ngeenyawo; Apho savuya ngaye.</li>
      <li>Ulolawula ngobugorha bakhe ngonaphakade; Amehlo akhe ayabonisela ezintlangeni; Abaziinjubaqa mabangaziphakamisi.  (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Mbongeni, zizwe, uThixo wethu, Nivakalise ilizwi lendumiso yakhe.</li>
      <li>Ulomisa umphefumlo wethu ebomini, Akalunikela unyawo lwethu ekutyibilikeni.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba usicikidile, Thixo; Usinyibilikisile njengokunyibilikiswa kwesilivere;</li>
      <li>Usingenise emboniselweni; Ubeke uxinzelelo esinqeni sethu;</li>
      <li>Ukhwelise abantu entlokweni yethu; Singene emlilweni nasemanzini; Waza wasikhuphela endaweni enendyebo.</li>
      <li>Ndiya kungena endlwini yakho ndinamadini anyukayo; Ndiya kuzizalisa kuwe izibhambathiso zam,</li>
      <li>Eyazivulelayo imilebe yomlomo wam, Owazithethayo umlomo wam ekubandezelweni kwam.</li>
      <li>Ndiya kunyusela kuwe amadini anyukayo eemvana ezityebileyo, Ndawonye nesiqhumiso seenkunzi zeegusha; Ndiya kwenza aweenkomo ndawonye naweenkunzi zeebhokhwe.  (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Yizani, nive, ndinixelele, nonke nina bamoyikayo uThixo,  Oko akwenzele umphefumlo wam.</li>
      <li>Ndadanduluka kuye ngomlomo wam; Kwaye ukubonga kuphantsi kolwimi lwam.</li>
      <li>Ukuba bendisekeleze ubutshinga ngentliziyo yam, INkosi yam ibingayi kuphulaphula.</li>
      <li>Hayi ke, uThixo uphulaphule, Ulibazele indlebe ilizwi lomthandazo wam.</li>
      <li>Makabongwe uThixo, Yena ungawugxothanga umthandazo wam,  Nobubele bakhe kum.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli; eyokubethelwa ngezinto ezineentambo. Umhobe.  Ingoma. Ngamana uThixo wasibabala, wasisikelela, Wabukhanyisa ubuso bakhe kuthi; (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Ukuze yaziwe ehlabathini indlela yakho, Usindiso lwakho ezintlangeni zonke.</li>
      <li>Ngamana zabulela izizwe kuwe, Thixo, Zabulela izizwe kuwe zonke ziphela;</li>
      <li>Zavuya zamemelela izizwe: Ngokuba uya kugweba phakathi kwezizwe ngokuthe tye, Uzikhaphe izizwe ehlabathini.  (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Ngamana zabulela izizwe kuwe, Thixo, Zabulela izizwe kuwe zonke ziphela.</li>
      <li>Umhlaba uyivelisile indyebo yawo; Uya kusisikelela uThixo,  uThixo wethu;</li>
      <li>Uya kusisikelela uThixo, Zimoyike zonke iziphelo zehlabathi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli; ekaDavide. Umhobe. Ingoma. Makasuk eme uThixo, zibe ziintsali iintshaba zakhe, Basabe ebusweni bakhe abamthiyayo.</li>
      <li>Njengokuphetshethwa komsi, baphephethe; Njengokunyibilika komthwebeba phambi komlilo, Mabadake ngokunjalo abangendawo ebusweni bukaThixo.</li>
      <li>Ke wona amalungisa makavuye, adlamke phambi koThixo, Abe nemihlali, enemivuyo.</li>
      <li>Vumani kuThixo, libetheleni uhadi igama lakhe; Menzeleni umendo ophakamileyo, ulokhwela ecanda ezinkqantosini, Ogama lakhe linguYehova; nidlamke phambi kwakhe.</li>
      <li>Uyise weenkedama, umthetheleli wabahlolokazi, NguThixo ekhayeni lakhe elingcwele.</li>
      <li>UThixo nguhlalisa endlwini ababebodwa, Ngukhuphela enywebeni ababanjiweyo; Ngabaziinjubaqa bodwa abahlala kwelibalelelweyo.</li>
      <li>Thixo, ekuphumeni kwakho uphambi kwabantu bakho,  Ekunyatheleni kwakho enkangala, (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Lanyikima ihlabathi, Lavuza izulu ebusweni bukaThixo,  ISinayi leya ebusweni bukaThixo, uThixo kaSirayeli.</li>
      <li>Walitshiza ngemvula eninzi yesisa sakho, Thixo, ilifa lakho; Lakubharha, walizimasa wena.</li>
      <li>Wahlala khona umhlambi wakho, Wamlungisela olusizana ngokulunga kwakho, Thixo.</li>
      <li>INkosi iya kukhupha izwi elinamandla, Ube mkhulu umkhosi weentokazi ezishumayela iindaba ezilungileyo.</li>
      <li>Ookumkani bemikhosi baya kusaba besabile; Intokazi esele ekhaya iya kuwaba amaxhoba.</li>
      <li>Nakulala phantsi phakathi kweentlanti, Noxelisa amaphiko evukuthu alekwe ngesilivere, Neentsiba zalo ezalekwe ngegolide ebengezelayo.</li>
      <li>Ekubadubadubeni kukaSomandla ookumkani kulo, Koba mhlophe ngowekhephu eTsalimon.</li>
      <li>Yintaba kaThixo intaba yaseBhashan, Yintaba encopho zininzi intaba yaseBhashan.</li>
      <li>Niyigxeleshelani na, zintaba zincopho zininzi, Intaba ayinqweneleyo uThixo ukuba ahlale kuyo? Ewe, uYehova uya kuhlala kuyo ngonaphakade.</li>
      <li>Iinqwelo zokulwa zikaThixo zizigidi, ngamawaka-waka;  INkosi ikuzo; yiSinayi ebungcweleni,</li>
      <li>Unyuke waya phezulu, uthimbe abathinjwa, Uthabathe izipho phakathi kwabantu, Naphakathi kwabaziinjubaqa, ukuba ahlale uYehova uThixo khona.</li>
      <li>Mayibongwe iNkosi; Ithwala imithwalo yethu imihla ngemihla; NguThixo umsindisi wethu. (Phakamisani.</li>
      <li>Yena uThixo kuthi nguThixo wosindiso, KokukaYehova, iNkosi yethu, ukukhupha ekufeni.</li>
      <li>Kodwa uThixo uya kuyiphalusa intloko yeentshaba zakhe,  Nentloko enesihlwitha yohambayo kwizigqitho zakhe.</li>
      <li>Yathi iNkosi, Ndiya kuzibuyisa eBhashan, Ndiya kuzibuyisa iintshaba zakho ezinzulwini zolwandle;</li>
      <li>Ukuze uziphaluse, unyawo lwakho lusegazini, Nolwimi lwezinja zakho lube nesabelo salo ezintshabeni.</li>
      <li>Bakubona ukunyathela kwakho, Thixo, Ukunyathela koThixo wam, koKumkani wam, esebungcweleni.</li>
      <li>Phambili ziimvumi, ngasemva ngababethi bohadi, Emacaleni ziintombi ezibetha iingqongqo.</li>
      <li>Emabandleni bongani uThixo, INkosi, nina basemthonjeni wakwaSirayeli.</li>
      <li>Balapho ooBhenjamin, inci yabo, umphathi wabo, Abathetheli bakwaYuda, ihlokondiba labo; Abathetheli bakwaZebhulon,  abathetheli bakwaNafetali.</li>
      <li>UThixo wakho wakuwisela umthetho wokuba uqine; Kuqinise,  Thixo, oko usenzeleyo.</li>
      <li>Bevela etempileni yakho eyongamele iYerusalem, Ookumkani mabeze nezithabathaba kuwe.</li>
      <li>Khalimela amarhamncwa asengcongolweni, Umhlambi weenkunzi eziziimbalasane, kunye namathole ezizwe, Ukuze baziwise benezijungqe zesilivere. Wazibhangisa izizwe eziyithandayo imfazwe.</li>
      <li>Kovela amanono eYiputa; UKushi wozolulela msinya izandla zakhe kuThixo.</li>
      <li>Zikumkani zehlabathi, vumani kuThixo, Niyibethele uhadi iNkosi; (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Ekhwela ecanda emazulwini awo amazulu amandulo; Nanko elikhupha ilizwi lakhe, ilizwi elinamandla.</li>
      <li>Mnikeni amandla uThixo; Buphezu koSirayeli ubungangamsha bakhe; Asesibhakabhakeni amandla akhe.</li>
      <li>UloThixo woyikekayo ezingcweleni zakho. UloThixo kaSirayeli, ubanikayo amandla nokomelela abantu. Makabongwe uThixo.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli; ngeyeenyibiba. EkaDavide. Ndisindise, Thixo;  Ngokuba amanzi andifikele, ada eza emphefumlweni.</li>
      <li>Nditshonile eludakeni olunzulu, akukho kuma; Ndingene emmbithini onamanzi, umsinga uyandintywilisela.</li>
      <li>Ndidiniwe kukudanduluka; womile umqala wam; Aphelile amehlo am; mna ndilindele kuThixo.</li>
      <li>Abandithiyayo ngelize baninzi ngaphezu kweenwele zentloko yam; Baninzi abandibangisayo, abaziintshaba zam bexoka; Into endingayiphanganga bathi mandiyibuyise.</li>
      <li>Thixo, wena uyakwazi ukumatha kwam; Namatyala am akanakugushwa kuwe.</li>
      <li>Mabangadani ngam abakuthembayo, Nkosi yam, Yehova wemikhosi; Mabangangcikivwa ngam abakufunayo, Thixo kaSirayeli.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba ndithwele ingcikivo ngenxa yakho; Ihlazo libugqubuthele ubuso bam;</li>
      <li>Ndingowasemzini kubazalwana bam; Ndingowolunye uhlanga kubantwana bakama:</li>
      <li>Ngokuba lindidlile ikhwele ngenxa yendlu yakho: Iingcikivo zabakungcikivayo ziwe phezu kwam.</li>
      <li>Mna, umphefumlo wam walila, uzila ukudla; Oko kwaba yingcikivo kum.</li>
      <li>Iingubo zam zaba zezirhwexayo, Ndaba yinto yokuzekelisa kubo.</li>
      <li>Bathetha ngam abahleli esangweni; Ndiyingoma yamanxila.</li>
      <li>Ke mna ndithandaza kuwe, Yehova, ngexesha elikholekileyo:  Thixo, ngobuninzi benceba yakho, Ndiphendule ngenyaniso yosindiso lwakho.</li>
      <li>Ndihlangule eludakeni, ndingatshoni; Mandihlangulwe kwabandithiyayo nasemimbithini enamanzi.</li>
      <li>Mawungandintywiliseli umsinga wamanzi; Ingandiginyi inzulu; Iqula malingandivingceli ngomlomo walo</li>
      <li>Ndiphendule, Yehova, ngokuba ilungile inceba yakho,  Ngangobuninzi bemfesane yakho ndibheke.</li>
      <li>Musa ukubusithelisa ubuso bakho kumkhonzi wakho, Ngokuba ndibandezelekile; khawuleza undiphendule.</li>
      <li>Sondela emphefumlweni wam, uwukhulule; Ngenxa yeentshaba zam ndikhulule.</li>
      <li>Wena uyakwazi ukungcikivwa kwam, nokudaniswa kwam,  nokuhlazwa kwam; Baphambi kwakho bonke abandibandezelayo.</li>
      <li>Ingcikivo yaphula intliziyo yam, ndaphantsa ukufa;  Ndathemba ukukhuzwa, akwabakho; Nokuthuthuzelwa, andakufumana.</li>
      <li>Ukudla bandinika inyongo; Ekunxanweni kwam bandiseza iviniga.</li>
      <li>Isithebe sabo phambi kwabo masibe ngumgibe; Sibe sisirhintyelo kwabanemasi.</li>
      <li>Makabe mnyama amehlo abo, bangaboni, Usigxadazelise isinqe sabo amaxesha onke.</li>
      <li>Baphalazele ngobhavumo lwakho, Kubafikele ukuvutha komsindo wakho.</li>
      <li>Ingqili yabo mayibe senkangala, Ezintenteni zabo kungahlali mntu;</li>
      <li>Ngokuba bayamsukela obethwe nguwe, Bancokole ngomvandedwa wobahlabileyo wena.</li>
      <li>Yongeza ubugwenxa ebugwenxeni babo, Bangangeni ebulungi senibakho.</li>
      <li>Mabacinywe encwadini yobomi, Bangabhalwa namalungisa.</li>
      <li>Ke mna ndilusizana, ndinomvandedwa; Usindiso lwakho,  Thixo, malundise engxondeni.</li>
      <li>Ndiya kulidumisa igama likaThixo ngokuvuma, Ndilenze likhulu ngokubulela.</li>
      <li>Oko kuya kukholeka kuYehova ngaphezu kweenkunzi ezintsha,  Ezineempondo neempuphu.</li>
      <li>Bebona abalulamileyo, bovuya; Nina bamquqelayo uThixo,  intliziyo yenu mayiphile.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba uYehova uyaweva amahlwempu, Akabadeli ababanjiweyo bakhe.</li>
      <li>Malimdumise izulu nomhlaba, Ulwandle nento yonke enambuzelayo kulo.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba uThixo uya kuyisindisa iZiyon, ayakhe imizi yakwaYuda, Bahlale khona, bayime;</li>
      <li>Ilidle ilifa imbewu yabakhonzi bakhe; Bahlale kuyo abalithandayo igama lakhe.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli; ekaDavide; eyokukhumbuza. Thixo, khawuleza undihlangule; Yehova, khawuleza undincede.</li>
      <li>Mabadane babe neentloni abawufunayo umphefumlo wam;  Mababuye umva bahlazeke abananze ukuba ndihlelwe bububi;</li>
      <li>Mababuye ngenxa yomvuzo wedano labo Abathi, Tshotsho!  Tshotsho!</li>
      <li>Mababe nemihlali bavuye ngawe bonke abakuquqelayo;  Abaluthandayo usindiso lwakho Mabahlale besithi, Makenziwe mkhulu uThixo.</li>
      <li>Ke mna ndilusizana, ndilihlwempu; Thixo, khawuleza uze kum.  Umncedi wam nomsindisi wam nguwe; Yehova, musa ukulibala.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ndizimela ngawe, Yehova, Mandingaze ndidane naphakade:</li>
      <li>Ngobulungisa bakho ndihlangule, ndisize; Ndithobele indlebe yakho, undisindise.</li>
      <li>Yiba liliwa elilikhaya kum, ndize kulo ngamaxesha onke.  Uwise umthetho wokuba ndisindiswe, Ngokuba ingxondorha yam nemboniselo yam nguwe.</li>
      <li>Thixo wam, ndisize esandleni songendawo, Esandleni sogqwethayo nosisibhovubhovu.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba ulithemba lam, Nkosi yam, Yehova, Inkoloseko yam kwasebuncinaneni bam.</li>
      <li>Ndixhaswe nguwe kwasesizalweni; Nguwe owandityhobozisayo ezibilinini zikama. Indumiso yam ingawe ngamaxesha onke.</li>
      <li>Ndinjengesimanga kwabaninzi; Ke wena ulihlathi lam elinqabileyo.</li>
      <li>Umlomo wam uya kuzala yindumiso yakho, Sisihombo sakho imini yonke.</li>
      <li>Musa ukundilahla ngexesha lobuxhego; Musa ukundishiya akuphela amandla am.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba zithetha ngam iintshaba zam; Abawulindayo umphefumlo wam bayacebisana,</li>
      <li>Besithi, UThixo umlahlile; Msukeleni nimbambe, ngokuba akukho mhlanguli.</li>
      <li>Thixo, musa ukuba kude kum; Thixo wam, khawuleza undincede.</li>
      <li>Mabadane, bagqitywe, abawuchasayo umphefumlo wam, Bathiwe wambu yingcikivo nehlazo abafuna ukuba ndihlelwe bububi.</li>
      <li>Ke mna ndiya kuhlala ndilindile, Ndongeze endumisweni yakho yonke.</li>
      <li>Umlomo wam uya kubalisa ngemisebenzi yobulungisa bakho,  Neyosindiso lwakho imini yonke, ngokuba ndingawazi amanani ayo.</li>
      <li>Ndiya kuza nemisebenzi yobugorha beNkosi uYehova; Ndiya kukhankanya ubulungisa bakho, bakho wedwa.</li>
      <li>Thixo, undifundisile kwasebuncinaneni bam; Unangoku ndiyayixela imisebenzi yakho ebalulekileyo.</li>
      <li>Thixo, musa ukundishiya kude kuye ebuxhegweni nasezimvini;  Ndide ndiyixele ingalo yakho kwisizukulwana esitsha, Nobugorha bakho kubo bonke abaya kuza.</li>
      <li>Thixo, ubulungisa bakho buye bafika phezulu; Wena uzenzayo izinto ezinkulu, Thixo, ngubani na onjengawe?</li>
      <li>Wena, usibonisileyo iimbandezelo ezininzi ezinobubi, Uya kubuya usiphilise, Ubuye usirhole ezinzonzobileni zamanzi ehlabathi;</li>
      <li>Uya kubandisa ubukhulu bam, Ubuye wena undithuthuzele.</li>
      <li>Ndiya kuyibulela nokuyibulela kuwe ngomrhubhe Inyaniso yakho, Thixo wam; Ndiya kukubethela uhadi, Ngcwele kaSirayeli.</li>
      <li>Uya kumemelela umlomo wam, ndakukubethela uhadi,  Nomphefumlo wam owukhululeyo;</li>
      <li>Nolwimi lwam luya kuxela ubulungisa bakho imini yonke,  Ngokuba bedanile beneentloni abafuna ukuba ndihlelwe bububi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>EkaSolomon. Thixo, mnike ukumkani imigwebo yakho, Mnike unyana wokumkani ubulungisa bakho.</li>
      <li>Makagwebe ebantwini bakho ngobulungisa, Nakwabaziintsizana zakho ngokwesiko.</li>
      <li>Iintaba mazibathwalele uxolo abantu, Kwaneenduli zibathwalele ebulungiseni.</li>
      <li>Makagwebe ityala labaziintsizana ebantwini, Asindise oonyana bamahlwempu, Abatyumze abacudisi.</li>
      <li>Mabakoyike, ukuhlala elihleliyo ilanga Kwanenyanga,  izizukulwana ngezizukulwana.</li>
      <li>Makehle njengemvula ehla phezu kotyani obusikwayo,  Njengeziphango, njengemvula emathontsi makhulu, emhlabeni.</li>
      <li>Malityatyambe ngemihla yakhe ilungisa, Nobuninzi boxolo,  ide ingabi sabakho inyanga.</li>
      <li>Makaphathe ubukhosi ethabathela elwandle ase elwandle,  Ethabathela kuwo uMlambo ase eziphelweni zehlabathi.</li>
      <li>Baya kuguqa phambi kwakhe abemi bomqwebedu, Zikhothe uthuli iintshaba zakhe.</li>
      <li>Ookumkani baseTarshishe nabeziqithi baya kunika iminikelo;  Ookumkani bakwaShebha nabakwaSebha baya kusondeza isithabathaba;</li>
      <li>Baqubude kuye bonke ookumkani, Zimkhonze sonke iintlanga.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba uya kulihlangula ihlwempu elizibikayo,  Nabaziintsizana abangenaluncedo;</li>
      <li>Abenzele inceba abasweleyo nabangamahlwempu; Asindise imiphefumlo yamahlwempu;</li>
      <li>Akhulule imiphefumlo yawo ekuxinezelweni nasekugonyamelweni; Linqabile emehlweni akhe igazi lawo.</li>
      <li>Uya kuphila anikwe igolide yakwaShebha, Bahlale bemthandazela, Bamsikelele imini yonke.</li>
      <li>Makubekho intabalala yengqolowa ezweni, ise encotsheni yeentaba; Ukuqhama kwayo makurhashaze njengeLebhanon;  Mabatyatyambe emizini yabo njengemifuno yomhlaba.</li>
      <li>Malibe ngunaphakade igama lakhe; Malivelise amagatya igama lakhe phambi kwelanga, Bazisikelele ngaye; Mazithi zonke iintlanga ungonoyolo.</li>
      <li>Makabongwe uYehova uThixo, uThixo kaSirayeli. Ulomenzi wemisebenzi ebalulekileyo yena yedwa.</li>
      <li>Malisikelelwe igama lakhe elizukileyo ngonaphakade, Lizale lonke ihlabathi luzuko lwakhe. Amen, amen.</li>
      <li>Iphelile imithandazo kaDavide unyana kaYese.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Umhobe ka-Asafu. Ulungile kwaphela uThixo kuSirayeli,  Kwabantliziyo zinyulu.</li>
      <li>Ke mna, beziphantse ukumka iinyawo zam; Gcwizi ukutyibilika ukunyathela kwam;</li>
      <li>Ngokuba bendibamonela abaqhayisayo, Ndakukubona ukuphumelela kwabangendawo.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba abanazintlungu ekufeni kwabo; Baphilile, batyebile umzimba wabo;</li>
      <li>Ebubini babantu abakho bona; Abakhathazwa njengabanye abantu.</li>
      <li>Ngako oko intamo yabo inxitywe ikratshi; Ukugonyamela kubathe wambu ngokwengubo.</li>
      <li>Amehlo abo avelile kukutyeba; Amabhongo eentliziyo zabo aphumela phandle.</li>
      <li>Bahlalela ngentlamba, bathetha ngokubandezela, benobubi;  Bathetha iindumbisa zamazwi.</li>
      <li>Bawubeka ezulwini umlomo wabo, Ulwimi lwabo luhamba emhlabeni wonke.</li>
      <li>Ngako oko abantu babo babuyela apha; Bafinca amanzi amaninzi.</li>
      <li>Bathi, Unokuthini na ukwazi uThixo? Kukho ukwazi na kOsenyangweni?</li>
      <li>Yabona abangendawo abaya Banokuchulumacha ngonaphakade,  bandile ngokutyeba.</li>
      <li>Sifumane sayiqaqambisa intliziyo yethu kanti, Sazihlamba izandla zethu ngokuba msulwa;</li>
      <li>Ndakhathazeka imini yonke, Ukohlwaywa kwethu kwaba kokwemiso yonke.</li>
      <li>Ukuba bendithe, Ndiya kwenjenjalo ukuthetha, Yabona,  ngendinginizile kwisizukulwana soonyana bakho.</li>
      <li>Ndathi ke ndakucinga ukuba ndikwazi oko, Kwayinkohla emehlweni am;</li>
      <li>Ndada ndaya kungena ezingcweleni zikaThixo, Ndakugqala ke ukuphela kwabo.</li>
      <li>Inene, ubamise ezindaweni ezibuthelezi, Wabawisa baba yintshabalala.</li>
      <li>Hayi, ukuphanziswa kwabo ngephanyazo; Baphelile,  bagqityiwe kukukhwankqa.</li>
      <li>Njengephupha ekuqabukeni komntu, Ekuvukeni kwakho, Nkosi,  wowudela umfanekiso wabo.</li>
      <li>Ukuba ndithe ndabindeka intliziyo, Ndahlabeka ezintsweni,</li>
      <li>Ndoba ke ndisisityhakala, ndingenakwazi; Ndoba ke ndisisilo kuwe.</li>
      <li>Mna ke ndihlala ndinawe; Undibambile ngesandla sam sokunene;</li>
      <li>Uya kundikhapha ngecebo lakho. Undithabathe emveni koku,  ndibe nozuko.</li>
      <li>Ndinabani na emazulwini? Ukuba wena ungowam, andilinanze nganto ihlabathi.</li>
      <li>Ingaphela inyama yam nentliziyo yam: Iliwa lentliziyo yam,  nesabelo sam, nguThixo ngonaphakade.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba, yabona, abanyawukileyo kuwe baya kudaka;  Uyababhangisa bonke abahenyuzayo, bemke kuwe.</li>
      <li>Mna ke, ukusondela kuThixo kulungile kum, Ndiyenza ihlathi lam iNkosi uYehova, Ukuze ndiyibalise yonke imisebenzi yakhe.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Eyokuqiqa; eka-Asafu. Yini na Thixo, ukuba uhlale usihlambile, Uqhume umsindo wakho kwizimvu zedlelo lakho?</li>
      <li>Likhumbule ibandla lakho olithengileyo kwakudala,  Olikhululeyo, laba sisizwe selifa lakho; Intaba yaseZiyon,  ohleli kuyo.</li>
      <li>Phakamisa ukunyathela kwakho, ukuya kumanxuwa ahlala ehleli: Utshaba luvive into yonke engcweleni.</li>
      <li>Babharhula ababandezeli bakho endaweni yokuhlangana phakathi; Bamisa eyabo imiqondiso, yaba yiyo eyimiqondiso.</li>
      <li>Kwanga kungenelwe Intshinyela yemithi ngezixengxe.</li>
      <li>Kungoku, uqoqo lwayo lonke Balucanda ngamazembe neengxobonga.</li>
      <li>Bayifaka umlilo ingcwele yakho; Bawuhlambela ngokuwuwisela emhlabeni umnquba wegama lakho.</li>
      <li>Bathi ezintliziyweni zabo, Siya kubanyanzelela phantsi kuphele; Bazitshisile zonke iindawo zikaThixo zokuhlangana ezweni apha.</li>
      <li>Imiqondiso yethu asiyiboni, Akusekho mprofeti; Kuthi akukho waziyo ukuba koda kuse phi na kunjalo.</li>
      <li>Kunini na, Thixo, umbandezeli engcikiva? Utshaba luhleli luligiba igama lakho?</li>
      <li>Usifinyezeleni na isandla sakho, nesokunene sakho? Sirhole esifubeni sakho, ulugqibe.</li>
      <li>Ke uThixo nguKumkani wam kwakumandulo, Ulosebenza usindiso phakathi kwehlabathi lonke.</li>
      <li>Nguwe owahlula ulwandle ngamandla akho, Owaphula iintloko zeengwenya emanzini.</li>
      <li>Nguwe owaxhaxha iintloko zeleviyatan, Wazinika zakukudla kubantu, kubemi bomqwebedu.</li>
      <li>Nguwe owagqobhoza yayimithombo, yayimilanjana; Nguwe owomisa imilambo engomiyo.</li>
      <li>Yeyakho imini, bobakho nobusuku; Nguwe owalungisa ukukhanya nelanga.</li>
      <li>Nguwe owamisa yonke imida yehlabathi; Ihlobo, nobusika,  nguwe owazibumbayo ezo zinto.</li>
      <li>Khumbula oku; utshaba lungcikiva uYehova, Abantu abanobudenge baligibile igama lakho.</li>
      <li>Musa ukuwunikela erhamncweni umphefumlo wehobe lakho;  Ungahlali uwulibele umhlambi wakho oziintsizana.</li>
      <li>Bheka emnqophisweni, Ngokuba iindawo ezimnyama zelizwe zizele zizindlu zogonyamelo.</li>
      <li>Makangabuyi otyumkileyo ehlazisiwe; Makalidumise igama lakho olusizana nolihlwempu.</li>
      <li>Khawusuk ume, Thixo, ubambane nababambene nawe; Khumbula ukukungcikiva kwesidenge yonke imini.</li>
      <li>Musa ukulilibala izwi lababandezeli bakho, Ukungxola kwabasukela phezulu kuwe, okuhlala kunyuka.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli; ngethi, Ungonakalisi. Umhobe ka-Asafu.  Ingoma. Siyabulela kuwe, Thixo, siyabulela; Lisondele igama lakho; Babalisa imisebenzi yakho ebalulekileyo.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba uthi, Ndiya kwenza ngexesha elimisiweyo, Mna ndiya kugweba ngokuthe tye.</li>
      <li>Liyetha amandla ihlabathi, nabemi balo; Ke mna,  ndizizinzisile iintsika zalo. (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Ndithi kubaqhayisi, Musani ukuqhayisa; Nakwabangendawo,  Musani ukuphakamisa uphondo;</li>
      <li>Musani ukuluphakamisela phezulu uphondo lwenu, Ningathethi ngokusa, nolule intamo.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba ugwebo aluveli empumalanga nasentshonalanga,  Nasentlango yeentaba.</li>
      <li>Hayi, nguThixo ogwebayo; Uyamthoba lo, amphakamise lowa.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba indebe isesandleni sikaYehova, Iphuphuma igwebu lewayini, izele yephithikeziweyo. Uthulula kuyo; ewe, iintlenga zayo Ziya kuselwa zifincwe ngabangendawo bonke behlabathi.</li>
      <li>Ke mna ndiya kushumayela ngonaphakade, Ndiya kuvuma kuThixo kaYakobi;</li>
      <li>Zonke iimpondo zabangendawo ndiya kuzixakaxa, Iimpondo zelungisa ziya kuphakanyiswa.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli; eyokubethelwa ngezinto ezineentambo. Umhobe ka-Asafu. Ingoma. Waziwa kwaYuda uThixo, Likhulu kwaSirayeli igama lakhe.</li>
      <li>Umnquba wakhe waba seSalem, Nekhaya lakhe eZiyon.</li>
      <li>Wayaphula apho imibane yesaphetha, Ingweletshetshe,  nekrele, nezixhobo zemfazwe. (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Ukhanyile, uyingangamsha ngaphezu kweentaba zokuqwenga.</li>
      <li>Babhunyulwe abantliziyo iyimbalasane, Balala umlala kanye,  Akazifumana izandla zawo onke amakroti.</li>
      <li>Ekukhalimeni kwakho, Thixo kaYakobi, Kwasindwa bubuthongo iinqwelo zokulwa namahashe.</li>
      <li>Unguwena wena woyikekayo; Ngubani na onokuma phambi kwakho,  wakuba nomsindo?</li>
      <li>Emazulwini usivakalisile isigwebo; Loyika ihlabathi,  lazola,</li>
      <li>Ekusukeni kukaThixo ukuba agwebe, Abasindise bonke abalulamileyo behlabathi. (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Ngokuba ubushushu bomntu buya kuba ngumbulelo kuwe; Uya kuwabhinqa amasalela obushushu.</li>
      <li>Bhambathisani, nisizalise isibhambathiso kuYehova uThixo wenu; Bonke abamngqongileyo mabeze nezithabathaba kofanele kukoyikwa.</li>
      <li>Uya kunqumla ukufutha kweenganga, Uyoyikeka kookumkani behlabathi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli. KuYedutun. Eka-Asafu. Umhobe. Izwi lam lisingisa kuThixo, ndikhala; Izwi lam lisingisa kuThixo, ukuba andibekele indlebe.</li>
      <li>Ngemini yokubandezelwa kwam ndiquqela eNkosini yam; Isandla sam solukile ebusuku, asaqoba; Awavuma ukuthuthuzeleka umphefumlo wam.</li>
      <li>Ndikhumbula uThixo, ndincwine; Ndithelekelele, utyhafe umoya wam. (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Uzibambile iinkophe zamehlo am, Ndikhandiwe, andaba nakuthetha.</li>
      <li>Ndicinga ngemihla yamandulo, Iminyaka yasephakadeni;</li>
      <li>Ndiya kukhumbula ebusuku ukubetha kwam uhadi; Ndithetha nentliziyo yam, uphengulula umoya wam.</li>
      <li>Ndithi, Iya kundihlamba ngonaphakade na iNkosi yam, Ingabi saphinda iphathe ngetarhu na?</li>
      <li>Iphele yaphela na inceba yayo? Sigqibele na isithembiso sayo kwisizukulwana ngesizukulwana?</li>
      <li>UThixo ukulibele na ukubabala? Uyivingcele ngomsindo kusini na imfesane yakhe? (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Ndide ndithi ke, Sisifo sam esi; Yiminyaka yesandla sokunene sOsenyangweni.</li>
      <li>Ndikhankanya izenzo ezincamisayo zikaYehova; Ngokuba ndikhumbula imisebenzi yakho ebalulekileyo yamandulo.</li>
      <li>Ndicamanga ngako konke ukusebenza kwakho, Ndithelekelele ngezenzo zakho zonke ezincamisayo.</li>
      <li>Thixo, isebungcweleni indlela yakho; Ngubani na onguthixo omkhulu njengoThixo wethu?</li>
      <li>UnguloThixo, wenza ngokubalulekileyo; Wawazisa amandla akho ezizweni,</li>
      <li>Wabakhulula ngengalo abantu bakho, Oonyana bakaYakobi noYosefu. (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Akubona amanzi, Thixo, Akubona amanzi, azibhija-bhija,  Ewe, agungqa amanzi enzonzobila;</li>
      <li>Amafu engqingqwa aphalaza amanzi, Isibhakabhaka savakalisa isandi; Ewe, iintolo zakho zahamba-hamba.</li>
      <li>Izwi lendudumo yakho laba sesaqhwithini, Imibane yalikhanyisa elimiweyo, Lagungqa lanyikima ihlabathi.</li>
      <li>Yaba selwandle indlela yakho, Nomendo wakho waba semanzini amaninzi; Awaziwa umkhondo wakho.</li>
      <li>Wabakhokela njengezimvu abantu bakho, Ngesandla sooMoses noAron.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Eyokuqiqa ka-Asafu. Wubekeleni indlebe umyalelo wam,  bantu bakowethu, Wathobeleni indlebe amazwi omlomo wam.</li>
      <li>Ndiya kuwuvula umlomo wam ngomzekeliso; Ndiya kumpompozisa iintsonkotha zamandulo;</li>
      <li>Esakuvayo sakwazi, Abasibaliselayo oobawo.</li>
      <li>Asiyi kukugusha koonyana babo; Sobalisela isizukulwana esizayo iindumiso zikaYehova, Namandla akhe, nemisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo awayenzayo.</li>
      <li>Wamisa isingqiniso kwaYakobi, Wabeka umyalelo kwaSirayeli,  Awawumisela oobawo, Ukuba bawazise oonyana babo;</li>
      <li>Ukuze siwazi isizukulwana esizayo, oonyana abaza kuzalwa,  Basuke babalisele ababo oonyana;</li>
      <li>Bayame ngoThixo, Bangazilibali izenzo ezincamisayo zikaThixo, Bayilondoloze imithetho yakhe:</li>
      <li>Bangabi njengooyise, Isizukulwana esiyinjubaqa,  esineenkani, Isizukulwana esingayilungisanga intliziyo yaso,  Esimoya unganyanisanga kuThixo.</li>
      <li>Oonyana bakaEfrayim, bexhobile, beziintoli ezinezaphetha,  Bajika ngemini yemfazwe.</li>
      <li>Abawugcinanga umnqophiso kaThixo, Abavumanga ukuhamba ngomyalelo wakhe;</li>
      <li>Bazilibala izenzo zakhe ezincamisayo, Nezibalulekileyo zakhe awababonisayo.</li>
      <li>Phambi kooyise wenza ngokubalulekileyo Ezweni lamaYiputa,  emhlabeni waseTsohan.</li>
      <li>Waludabula ulwandle, wabaweza, Wawamisa amanzi njengemfumba.</li>
      <li>Wabakhapha ngelifu emini, Ngokukhanya komlilo ubusuku bonke,</li>
      <li>Walicanda iliwa entlango, Wabaseza amanzi anzongonzongo kakhulu;</li>
      <li>Wavelisa imiqukuqela yamanzi engxondorheni, Wahlisa amanzi njengemilambo.</li>
      <li>Baqokela noko ukona kuye, Nokumphikisa Osenyangweni emqwebedwini.</li>
      <li>Bamlinga uThixo ngentliziyo yabo, Ngokuwubizela umphefumlo wabo ukudla.</li>
      <li>Bathetha ngoThixo, bathi, Unako na uThixo ukulungisa isithebe entlango?</li>
      <li>Yabona, walibetha iliwa, abaleka amanzi, Yakhukula nemilanjana; Woba nako na nokubanika ukutya, Nokubalungiselela inyama abantu bakhe?</li>
      <li>Weva ke uThixo, waphuphuma umsindo wakhe, Watsha umlilo kwaYakobi, Kwenyuka kwaya umsindo kwaSirayeli;</li>
      <li>Ngokuba bengakholwanga kuThixo, Bengakholosanga ngosindiso lwakhe.</li>
      <li>Waziwisela ke umthetho iingqimba zamafu ngaphezulu,  Wazivula iingcango zezulu;</li>
      <li>Wabanisela ngemana ukuze badle, Wabanika ingqolowa yasezulwini.</li>
      <li>Umntu wadla isonka sOnamandla; Wabathumela umphako bada badikwa.</li>
      <li>Wandulula umoya wasempumalanga ezulwini, Wawuqhuba ngamandla akhe umoya wasezantsi;</li>
      <li>Wabanisela inyama njengothuli, Neentaka ezinamaphiko njengentlabathi yolwandle;</li>
      <li>Yawa phakathi kweminquba yabo, Ngeenxa zonke emakhayeni abo.</li>
      <li>Badla, bahlutha kakhulu, Wabazisela ke inkanuko yabo.</li>
      <li>Bengekashenxi enkanukweni yabo, Kusekho ukudla kwabo emlonyeni wabo:</li>
      <li>Kwenyuka umsindo kaThixo waya kubo, Wabulala phakathi kwabatyebileyo babo, Wawawisa amadodana akwaSirayeli.</li>
      <li>Kuyo yonke loo nto bahambisa ngokona, Abakholwa yimisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo.</li>
      <li>Wayiphelisa ke imihla yabo njengomphunga, Neminyaka yabo ngokukhwankqisa.</li>
      <li>Xa wathi wababulala, bamquqela; Babuya bamquqela uThixo ngenyameko,</li>
      <li>Bakhumbula ukuba uThixo uliliwa labo, UThixo Osenyangweni ungumkhululi wabo.</li>
      <li>Ke bamthomalalisa ngomlomo wabo, Bamxokisa ngolwimi lwabo;</li>
      <li>Intliziyo yabo ayaqina kuye, Abanyaniseka emnqophisweni wakhe.</li>
      <li>Ke yena unemfesane, Uxolela ubugwenxa ngocamagushelo,  akonakalisi; Wawubuyisa futhi umsindo wakhe, Akabuxhoxha bonke ubushushu bakhe.</li>
      <li>Wakhumbula ukuba bayinyama, Bangumoya omkayo, ongabuyiyo.</li>
      <li>Kukangaphi bemphikisa entlango, Bemenza buhlungu enkangala!</li>
      <li>Babuya bamlinga uThixo, Bamenzakalisa oyiNgcwele wakwaSirayeli.</li>
      <li>Abasikhumbula isandla sakhe, Imini awabakhulula ngayo embandezelweni;</li>
      <li>Awamisa ngayo imiqondiso yakhe eYiputa, Nezimanga zakhe emhlabeni waseTsohan.</li>
      <li>Wayiguqula imijelo yabo, yaba ligazi, Ababa nakuyisela imiqukuqela yabo yamanzi.</li>
      <li>Wathumela kubo iingcongconi, zabadla; Namasele,  abatshabalalisa.</li>
      <li>Izilimo zabo wazinika iinkumbi ezinqunquthayo, Ukuxelenga kwabo wakunika iinkumbi ezandayo.</li>
      <li>Wawubulala ngesichotho umdiliya wabo, Nemithombe yabo ngomkhenkce.</li>
      <li>Wayinikela kwisichotho imfuyo yabo, Nemihlambi yabo ngemibane.</li>
      <li>Wathumela kubo ukuvutha komsindo wakhe, Ukuphuphuma kwawo,  nokubhavuma, nembandezelo, Ibutho lezithunywa zobubi.</li>
      <li>Wawulungelelanisela umendo umsindo wakhe, Akawunqanda ekufeni umphefumlo wabo, Wabunikela ubomi babo kwindyikitya yokufa.</li>
      <li>Wababulala bonke abamazibulo eYiputa, Iintlahlela zamandla obudoda ezintenteni zakwaHam.</li>
      <li>Abantu bakhe wabafudusa njengezimvu, Wabaqhuba njengomhlambi entlango;</li>
      <li>Wabakhapha bekholosile, bengankwantyi; Ke zona iintshaba zabo lwazigubungela ulwandle</li>
      <li>Wabazisa emdeni wakhe ongcwele, Kule ntaba sayizuzayo isandla sakhe sokunene.</li>
      <li>Wagxotha iintlanga ebusweni babo, Wazenzela amaqashiso zalilifa elicandiweyo; Izizwe zakwaSirayeli wazihlalisa ezintenteni zazo.</li>
      <li>Kodwa bamlinga, bamphikisa uThixo Osenyangweni, Abazigcina izingqiniso zakhe,</li>
      <li>Babuya unuva, banginiza njengooyise. Bajika njengesaphetha esikhohlisayo.</li>
      <li>Bamqumbisa ngeziganga zabo, Bamkhweletisa ngemifanekiso yabo eqingqiweyo.</li>
      <li>Weva uThixo, waphuphuma umsindo, Wawacekisa kakhulu amaSirayeli;</li>
      <li>Wawulahla umnquba waseShilo, Intente abeyimise esintwini;</li>
      <li>Wawanikela ekuthinjweni amandla akhe, Isihombo sakhe esandleni sombandezeli.</li>
      <li>Wabanikela abantu bakhe kwikrele, Umsindo wakhe waphuphumela ilifa lakhe.</li>
      <li>Amadodana abo adliwa ngumlilo, Iintombi zabo azagcotyelwa.</li>
      <li>Ababingeleli babo bawa likrele, Abahlolokazi babo abalila.</li>
      <li>Yaza yavuka njengobelele iNkosi, Njengegorha elimemeleliswa yiwayini.</li>
      <li>Yababetha ngasemva ababandezeli bayo, Yabenza ingcikivo engunaphakade.</li>
      <li>Yayicekisa intente yakwaYosefu, Ayasinyula isizwe sakwaEfrayim.</li>
      <li>Yanyula isizwe sakwaYuda, Intaba yaseZiyon eyayithandayo.</li>
      <li>Yayakha njengokuphakama kwezulu ingcwele yakhe,  Njengomhlaba lo awusekileyo ngonaphakade.</li>
      <li>Yanyula uDavide umkhonzi wayo, Yamthabatha ezibayeni zezimvu;</li>
      <li>Yamthabatha elandela izimvu ezanyisayo, Yamzisa ukuba aluse kwaYakobi abantu bayo, KwaSirayeli ilifa layo.</li>
      <li>Wabalusa ke ngengqibelelo yentliziyo yakhe, Wabakhapha ngokwazi kwezandla zakhe.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Umhobe ka-Asafu. Thixo, iintlanga zingene elifeni lakho,  Ziyenze inqambi itempile yakho engcwele; Ziyenze yayimiwewe iYerusalem.</li>
      <li>Izidumbu zabakhonzi bakho zizinike iintaka zezulu ukuba zizidle, Nenyama yabakho benceba ziyinike amarhamncwa elizwe.</li>
      <li>Ziliphalazile igazi labo njengamanzi ngeenxa zonke eYerusalem; Akwabakho mngcwabi.</li>
      <li>Senziwe ingcikivo kubamelwane bethu, Isigculelo nesicukucezo kwabasingqongileyo.</li>
      <li>Kunini na, Yehova, uhleli uqumbile? Liya kuvutha njengomlilo na ikhwele lakho?</li>
      <li>Phalaza ubushushu bakho ezintlangeni ezingakwaziyo,  Ezikumkanini ezingalinquliyo igama lakho.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba zimdlile uYakobi, Zalenza inxuwa ikhaya lakhe.</li>
      <li>Musa ukubukhumbula kuthi ubugwenxa bamanyange ethu,  Mayingxame isikhawulele imfesane yakho: Ngokuba siswele kakhulu.</li>
      <li>Sincede, Thixo ongumsindisi wethu, ngenxa yozuko lwegama lakho, Usihlangule, uzixolele ngocamagushelo izono zethu ngenxa yegama lakho.</li>
      <li>Yini na ukuba iintlanga zithi kuthi, Uphi na uThixo wabo?  Makwazeke ezintlangeni, emehlweni ethu, Ukuphindezelwa kwegazi labakhonzi bakho eliphalaziweyo.</li>
      <li>Makuze phambi kwakho ukugcuma kwamakhonkxwa; Ngokobukhulu bengalo yakho basalise oonyana bokufa.</li>
      <li>Yibuyisele kubamelwane bethu kasixhenxe esondweni lengubo yabo Ingcikivo yabo, abakungcikive ngayo, Nkosi.</li>
      <li>Ke thina bantu bakho, zimvu zaluswa nguwe, Siya kubulela kuwe ngonaphakade, Sibalise ngendumiso yakho kwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli; ngeyeenyibiba ezingqinisayo. Ka-Asafu.  Umhobe. Ulomalusi kaSirayeli, beka indlebe! Uloqhuba uYosefu njengezimvu, Ulohlala ezikerubhini, bengezela!</li>
      <li>Phambi koEfrayim noBhenjamin noManase, Vusa ubugorha bakho,  Uze kusisindisa.</li>
      <li>Thixo, sibuyise, Ukhanyise ubuso bakho, sisindiswe.</li>
      <li>Yehova, Thixo wemikhosi, Kunini na uqhuma umsindo wakho ekuthandazeni kwabantu bakho?</li>
      <li>Ubadlisa isonka seenyembezi, Wabaseza iinyembezi ngemilinganiso.</li>
      <li>Usenze into abaxabana ngayo abamelwane bethu; Iintshaba zethu ziyasigculela.</li>
      <li>Thixo wemikhosi, sibuyise, Ukhanyise ubuso bakho,  sisindiswe.</li>
      <li>Wanyothula umdiliya eYiputa, Wagxotha iintlanga, wawutyala;</li>
      <li>Wahlahla phambi kwawo, Wendelisa iingcambu, wazalisa ilizwe.</li>
      <li>Zagutyungelwa iintaba ngumthunzi wawo, Nemisedare kaThixo ngamasebe awo.</li>
      <li>Wasa amasebe awo elwandle, Namagatya awo kuwo uMlambo.</li>
      <li>Uzityhobozeleni na iintango zawo, Ukuze bawukhe bonke abadlula ngendlela?</li>
      <li>Ingulube yasehlathini iyawubhuqa, Nento edakasa endle iyawudla.</li>
      <li>Thixo wemikhosi, khawubuye, Uqondele usemazulwini, ubone,  Uwuvelele lo mdiliya.</li>
      <li>Yikhusele into esiyityeleyo isandla sakho sokunene, Unyana lo uzizimaseleyo ngokwakho.</li>
      <li>Utshisiwe ngumlilo, uhlahliwe; Bayadaka ngokusongela kobuso bakho.</li>
      <li>Isandla sakho masibe phezu komfo wesandla sakho sokunene,  Phezu koonyana babantu, ozizimaseleyo ngokwakho.</li>
      <li>Asiyi kumka kuwe; Siphilise, silinqule igama lakho.</li>
      <li>Yehova, Thixo wemikhosi, sibuyise, Ukhanyise ubuso bakho,  sisindiswe.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli; ngolwaseGati. Ka-Asafu. Memelelani kuThixo,  igwiba lethu, Dumani kuThixo kaYakobi.</li>
      <li>Hlabani ingoma, nibethe ingqongqo, Uhadi olumnandi, kunye nomrhubhe.</li>
      <li>Vuthelani isigodlo ukuthwasa kwenyanga, Nokuhlangana kwenyanga, ngemini yomthendeleko wethu.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba ngummiselo lowo kuSirayeli, Lisiko likaThixo kaYakobi.</li>
      <li>Sisingqiniso awasimisayo kwaYosefu, Ekucandeni kwakhe ezweni laseYiputa; Ndeva intetho endingayaziyo.</li>
      <li>Ndawususa umthwalo egxalabeni lakhe; Izandla zakhe zasuka ezingobozini zokuthwala.</li>
      <li>Embandezelweni wadanduluka wena, ndakuhlangula;  Ndakuphendula esitheni leendudumo, Ndakuvavanya emanzini aseMeribha. (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Ndathi, Yivani, bantu bam, ndiqononondise kuni; Sirayeli,  ukuba unokuphulaphula kum!</li>
      <li>Makungabikho thixo wasemzini kuwe; Unganquli thixo wolunye uhlanga.</li>
      <li>Ndim uYehova uThixo wakho, Okunyusileyo elizweni laseYiputa. Yakhamisa, ndiwuzalise umlomo wakho.</li>
      <li>Ke abantu bam abaliva izwi lam, USirayeli akandivumanga.</li>
      <li>Ndabanikela ebungqoleni beentliziyo zabo; Bahamba ngawabo amaqhinga.</li>
      <li>Akwaba abantu bam bebendiva, Akwaba uSirayeli ubehamba ngendlela yam!</li>
      <li>Bendiya kuzithoba kamsinya iintshaba zabo, Ndisibuyisele phezu kwababandezeli babo isandla sam.</li>
      <li>Abamthiyayo uYehova bebeya kuhanahanisa kuye, Libe ngunaphakade ixesha labo.</li>
      <li>Bendiya kubadlisa ingqolowa etyebileyo, Ndibahluthise ngobusi etsilini.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Umhobe ka-Asafu. UThixo umi ebandleni likaThixo, Ugweba phakathi koothixo; uthi,</li>
      <li>Kunini na nigweba ngobugqwetha, Nibanonelela abangendawo?  (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Thethani ityala losweleyo nelenkedama, Gwebelani olusizana nolihlwempu.</li>
      <li>Sizani osweleyo nolihlwempu, Bahlanguleni esandleni sabangendawo.</li>
      <li>Abazi, abaqondi, Bahamba-hamba emnyameni; Ziyashukuma zonke iziseko zehlabathi.</li>
      <li>Ndithe mna, Ningoothixo, Ningoonyana bOsenyangweni nonke niphela.</li>
      <li>Noko niya kufa njengomntu, Niwe njengomnye kubathetheli.</li>
      <li>Khawusuk ume, Thixo, gweba ehlabathini; Ngokuba uya kuzidla ilifa wena zonke iintlanga.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ingoma. Umhobe ka-Asafu. Thixo, musa ukuthi cwaka, Musa ukuthi tu, musa ukuzola, Thixo.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba nanzo iintshaba zakho zixokozela; Abakuthiyayo baphakamisa intloko.</li>
      <li>Bagqugula igqugula elinobuqhophololo ngabantu bakho,  Bacebisane ngabagushiweyo nguwe.</li>
      <li>Bathi, Yizani sibethe bee shwaka, bangabi luhlanga, Lingabi sakhunjulwa igama likaSirayeli.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba bacebisana ngantliziyo-nye, Benza umnqophiso ngawe:</li>
      <li>Iintente zakwaEdom nezakwaIshmayeli, AmaMowabhi namaHagari,</li>
      <li>AmaGebhali nama-Amon nama-Amaleki, AmaFilisti kunye nabemi baseTire;</li>
      <li>Nama-Asiriya athelele kubo, Baba yingalo koonyana bakaLote.  (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Yenza kubo njengoko wenza ngako kumaMidiyan, NakuSisera,  nakuYabhin esihlanjeni seKishon.</li>
      <li>Batshabalala e-Endore, Baba ngumgquba wokugalelwa emhlabeni.</li>
      <li>Benze bona, amanene abo ke, babe njengo-Orebhe nanjengoZebhe; Zonke iinkosi zabo zibe njengoZebha nanjengoTsalimuna;</li>
      <li>Bona bathi, Masiwahluthe abe ngawethu amakhaya kaThixo.</li>
      <li>Thixo wam, benze babe njengesaqhwithi, Njengomququ phambi komoya.</li>
      <li>Njengomlilo odla ihlathi, Njengedangatye lilenya intaba,</li>
      <li>Yenjenjalo ukubasukela ngoqhwithela lwakho, Ubakhwankqise ngomoya wakho ovuthuzayo.</li>
      <li>Buzalise ubuso babo ngehlazo, Balifune igama lakho,  Yehova.</li>
      <li>Mabadane bakhwankqiswe ngonaphakade, Babe neentloni,  badake;</li>
      <li>Bazi ukuba wena, ugama linguYehova, unguwe wedwa Osenyangweni phezu kwehlabathi lonke.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli; ngolwaseGati. Eyoonyana bakaKora. Umhobe.  Hayi, ukuthandeka kweminquba yakho, Yehova wemikhosi!</li>
      <li>Umphefumlo wam ulangazelela, uyaphela kukuzilangazelela,  iintendelezo zikaYehova; Intliziyo yam nenyama yam imemelela kuThixo ophilileyo.</li>
      <li>Intakana le ifumene ikhaya; Inkonjane izifumanele indlu,  Apho izalela khona amathole ayo: Izibingelelo zakho, Yehova wemikhosi, Kumkani wam, Thixo wam.</li>
      <li>Hayi, uyolo lwabahlala endlwini yakho! Basaya kukudumisa.  (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Hayi, uyolo lwabantu abamandla akuwe, Abakhumbula umendo oya eZiyon!</li>
      <li>Bephumela entilini yemithi yeBhaka, Bayenza ibe nemithombo;  Ewe, imvula iyithi wambu ngentsikelelo.</li>
      <li>Baya besomelela ngokomelela; Babonakala phambi koThixo eZiyon, bathi,</li>
      <li>Yehova, Thixo wemikhosi, Wuve umthandazo wam, Wubekele indlebe, Thixo kaYakobi. (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Khangela, Thixo, ngweletshetshe yethu, Ubukhangele ubuso bomthanjiswa wakho.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba imini enye ezintendelezweni zakho ilungile kunewaka; Ndinyule ukuba semnyango endlwini kaThixo wam,  Kunokuhlala ngaphakathi kweentente zokungendawo.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba ulilanga, uyingweletshetshe uYehova uThixo,  UYehova uyababala azukise; Abahamba ngokugqibeleleyo akabavimbi nto ilungileyo.</li>
      <li>Yehova wemikhosi, Hayi, uyolo lomntu okholose ngawe!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli; eyoonyana bakaKora. Umhobe. Yehova, wabe unetarhu kwilizwe lakho. Ububabuyisa abathinjwa bakaYakobi;</li>
      <li>Ububuxolela ubugwenxa babantu bakho, Ubuziselela zonke izono zabo. (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Ubuwufinyeza umsindo wakho ophuphumayo, Ububuya ekuvutheni komsindo wakho.</li>
      <li>Sibuyise, Thixo ongumsindisi wethu, Uyisuse ingqumbo yakho kuthi.</li>
      <li>Uya kusiqumbela ngonaphakade na? Umsindo wakho uya kuwolulela kwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana na?</li>
      <li>Akuyi kubuya usiphilise na, Abantu bakho bavuye ngawe?</li>
      <li>Sibonise inceba yakho, Yehova, Siphe usindiso lwakho.</li>
      <li>Mandive oko aya kukuthetha uThixo, uYehova; Hayi, uthetha uxolo kubantu bakhe nakwabakhe benceba; Mabangabuyeli ke ekunyabeni kwabo.</li>
      <li>Inene, usindiso lwakhe lusondele kwabamoyikayo, Ukuze luhlale uzuko ezweni lakowethu.</li>
      <li>Kuya kuqubisana inceba nenyaniso, Kuya kwangana ubulungisa noxolo.</li>
      <li>Inyaniso iya kuntshula emhlabeni, Ubulungisa buqondele busemazulwini.</li>
      <li>Kananjalo uYehova uya kusinika okulungileyo, Ilizwe lethu lisinike indyebo yalo.</li>
      <li>Ubulungisa buya kuhamba phambi kwakhe, Buyigqale ngentliziyo indlela yokunyathela kwakhe.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Umthandazo kaDavide. Thoba indlebe yakho, Yehova,  ndiphendule, Ngokuba ndilusizana, ndilihlwempu.</li>
      <li>Wugcine umphefumlo wam, ngokuba ndingowenceba; Msindise,  wena Thixo wam, umkhonzi wakho, Lo ukholose ngawe.</li>
      <li>Ndibabale, Nkosi yam, Ngokuba ndidanduluka kuwe yonke imini.</li>
      <li>Wuvuyise umphefumlo womkhonzi wakho, Ngokuba umphefumlo wam ndiwuphakamisela kuwe, Nkosi yam;</li>
      <li>Ngokuba ulungile wena, Nkosi yam, uxolela; Umkhulu ngenceba kubo bonke abakunqulayo.</li>
      <li>Wubekele indlebe umthandazo wam, Yehova, Ulibazele indlebe izwi lokutarhuzisa kwam.</li>
      <li>Ngemini yokubandezelwa kwam ndinqula wena, Ngokuba uya kundiphendula.</li>
      <li>Akukho unjengawe, Nkosi yam, phakathi koothixo; Akukho zenzo zinjengezakho.</li>
      <li>Zonke iintlanga owazenzayo ziya kuza ziqubude phambi kwakho, Nkosi yam, Zizukise igama lakho.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba umkhulu, wenza imisebenzi ebalulekileyo, UnguThixo wena wedwa.</li>
      <li>Ndiyalele, Yehova, indlela yakho, Ndihambe ngenyaniso yakho; Yibandakanye intliziyo yam ukuba ndiloyike igama lakho.</li>
      <li>Ndiya kubulela kuwe, Nkosi yam, Thixo wam, ngentliziyo yonke, Ndilizukise igama lakho ngonaphakade:</li>
      <li>Ngokuba inceba yakho ibe inkulu kum; Wawuhlangula umphefumlo wam kwelingaphantsi labafileyo.</li>
      <li>Thixo, abakhukhumali basukele phezulu kum; Ibandla labanobungqwangangqwili lifuna umphefumlo wam; Abakumisi wena phambi kwabo.</li>
      <li>Ke wena, Nkosi yam, unguThixo onemfesane, onobabalo, Ozeka kade umsindo, omkhulu ngenceba nenyaniso.</li>
      <li>Ndibheke, undibabale; Mphe amandla akho umkhonzi wakho,  Umsindise unyana womkhonzazana wakho.</li>
      <li>Ndenzele umqondiso wokulungileyo, Bawubone abandithiyayo,  badane, Kuba wena, Yehova, undincedile, wandithuthuzela.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Eyoonyana bakaKora. Umhobe. Ingoma. Useko alusekileyo lusezintabeni ezingcwele;</li>
      <li>Amasango eZiyon uYehova uwathanda Ngaphezu kweminquba yonke kaYakobi.</li>
      <li>Kuthethwa iinto ezizukileyo ngawe, Mzi kaThixo.  (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>ORahabhi noBhabheli ndiya kubakhankanyela kwabandaziyo;  Nalo elamaFilisti nelaseTire, kunye nelakwaKushi, Aba bazalelwe khona.</li>
      <li>Ngokusingisele kwiZiyon, kuya kuthiwa, Lo, nalo, uzalelwe kuyo, Abe yena Osenyangweni eyizinzisa.</li>
      <li>UYehova uya kubala, ekuzibhaleni izizwi, athi, Abaya bazalelwe khona: (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Baze, bevuma beqamba, bathi, Yonke imithombo yam ikuwe.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ingoma; umhobe woonyana bakaKora; kumongameli; ngosizi,  ngelidambileyo. Owokuqiqa kaHeman umEzra. Yehova, Thixo ongumsindisi wam, Mhlenikweni ndikhalayo ebusuku phambi kwakho,</li>
      <li>Mawuze phambi kwakho umthandazo wam; Thoba indlebe yakho ekuhlahlambeni kwam.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba umphefumlo wam uhluthi zizinto ezimbi, Ubomi bam bufike kwelabafileyo.</li>
      <li>Ndibalelwe kwabahla baye emhadini, Ndisuke ndanjengomfo ongenamandla</li>
      <li>Ndingumkhululwa phakathi kwabafileyo, Njengababuleweyo,  belele engcwabeni, Ongasabakhumbuliyo; Bona banqunyulweyo esandleni sakho.</li>
      <li>Undibeke emhadini ongaphantsi, Ezindaweni ezimnyama,  ezinzulwini.</li>
      <li>Ubushushu bakho bundishicilele, Undithobele onke amaza akho alwayo. (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Ubashenxisele kude kum abo ndazana nabo, Undenze isikizi kubo; Ndivalelwe, andinakuphuma.</li>
      <li>Iliso lam liyaphela yingcinezelo. Ndidanduluka kuwe,  Yehova, yonke imini, Ndizolulela kuwe izandla zam.</li>
      <li>Uya kuyenzela abafileyo na imisebenzi ebalulekileyo? Kuya kuvuka abangasekhoyo, kusini na, babulele kuwe? (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Ibaliswa engcwabeni na inceba yakho? Enzonzobileni na,  ukunyanisa kwakho?</li>
      <li>Yaziswa emnyameni na imisebenzi yakho ebalulekileyo?  Baziswa ezweni lokulibala na ubulungisa bakho?</li>
      <li>Ke mna, Yehova, ndizibika kuwe, Kwakusasa umthandazo wam wokuhlangabeza.</li>
      <li>Uwuhlambelani na, Yehova, umphefumlo wam? Ubusitheliselani na ubuso bakho kum?</li>
      <li>Ndilusizana, ndiyinto efayo kwasebuncinaneni bam,  Ndithwele izothuso zakho, lindikhohlile.</li>
      <li>Kugqithe phezu kwamukuvutha kwakho, Izidandathekiso zakho zindibhangisile;</li>
      <li>Zindijikelezile njengamanzi imini yonke, Zindizungulezile kwaphela.</li>
      <li>Umsusile kum ondithandayo nonguwethu; Abo ndazana nabo babubumnyama.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Eyokuqiqa kaEtan, umEzra. Iinceba zikaYehova ndiya kuvuma ngazo ngonaphakade, Kwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana ndiya kwazisa ukuthembeka kwakho ngomlomo wam.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba ndithi, Yakheka ngonaphakade inceba; Amazulu, uya kukuzinzisa kuwo ukuthembeka kwakho.</li>
      <li>Wathi, Ndenze umnqophiso nomnyulwa wam, Ndifungile kuDavide umkhonzi wam:</li>
      <li>Ndiya kuyizimasa ngonaphakade imbewu yakho, Ndiyakhe itrone yakho kwisizukulwana ngesizukulwana. (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Amazulu abulela imisebenzi yakho ebalulekileyo, Yehova,  Nokuthembeka kwakho ebandleni labangcwele.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba ngubani na esibhakabhakeni olingana noYehova?  Ngubani na ofana noYehova phakathi koonyana bakaThixo.</li>
      <li>UThixo ongowokungcangcazelelwa ebhungeni elikhulu labangcwele, Ongofanelwe kukoyikwa ngaphezu kwabo bonke abamngqongileyo?</li>
      <li>Yehova, Thixo wemikhosi, Ngubani na onjengawe, oluqilima,  Yehova? Ukuthembeka kwakho kukungqongile.</li>
      <li>Nguwena mlawuli wekratshi lolwandle; Ekuphakameni kwamaza alo uyawadambisa.</li>
      <li>Nguwena mtyumzi kaRahabhi njengongxwelerhiweyo, Wazithi saa iintshaba zakho ngengalo yakho eqinileyo.</li>
      <li>Lelakho izulu, likwalelakho ihlabathi; Elimiweyo nenzaliseko yalo lasekwa nguwe.</li>
      <li>Umntla nomzantsi wadalwa nguwe; ITabhore neHermon zimemelela ngegama lakho.</li>
      <li>Yeyakho ingalo enobugorha; Sithe nkqi isandla sakho,  siphakamile esokunene sakho.</li>
      <li>Ummiso wetrone yakho bubulungisa nokusesikweni; Inceba nenyaniso ilungiselela phambi kwakho.</li>
      <li>Hayi, uyolo lwabantu abakwaziyo ukuduma! Baya kuhamba ekukhanyeni kobuso bakho, Yehova.</li>
      <li>Baya kugcoba egameni lakho imini yonke, Baphakame ngobulungisa bakho.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba isihombo samandla abo nguwe; Ekuthandeni kwakho,  uphondo lwethu luphakamile.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba ikuYehova ingweletshetshe yethu, UkoyiNgcwele kaSirayeli ukumkani wethu.</li>
      <li>Wakha wathetha ngombono kowenceba wakho, wathi, Ndibeke uncedo egorheni, Ndiphakamise indodana ebantwini.</li>
      <li>Ndifumene uDavide umkhonzi wam; Ndimthambisile ngeoli yam engcwele,</li>
      <li>Esiya kuqinisela kuye isandla sam, Nengalo yam imkhaliphise.</li>
      <li>Utshaba aluyi kumqubula; Nonyana wobugqwetha akayi kumcinezela.</li>
      <li>Ndiya kubaqoba phambi kwakhe ababandezeli bakhe,  Ndibaxabele abamthiyayo.</li>
      <li>Inyaniso yam nenceba yam inaye; Luya kuphakama uphondo lwakhe egameni lam.</li>
      <li>Ndiya kusisa elwandle isandla sakhe, EMilanjeni esokunene sakhe.</li>
      <li>Yena ukundibiza wothi, UnguBawo, UnguThixo wam, neliwa lokundisindisa.</li>
      <li>Kananjalo mna ndiya kumenza owamazibulo, Osenyangweni kookumkani behlabathi.</li>
      <li>Ndiya kumgcinela inceba yam ngonaphakade, Umnqophiso wam unyanise kuye;</li>
      <li>Ndiyimise ngonaphakade imbewu yakhe, Netrone yakhe ibe njengemihla yamazulu.</li>
      <li>Ukuba bathe oonyana bakhe bawulahla umyalelo wam, Abahamba ngamasiko am;</li>
      <li>Ukuba bathe bayihlambela imimiselo yam, Abayigcina imithetho yam:</li>
      <li>Ndoluvelela ukreqo lwabo ngentonga, Nobugwenxa babo ngemivumbo.</li>
      <li>Ke yona inceba yam andiyi kuyaphula kuye, Ndingaxoki ekuthembekeni kwam.</li>
      <li>Andiyi kuwuhlambela umnqophiso wam, Ndiyijike into ephume emlonyeni wam.</li>
      <li>Ndibufunge kwakanye ubungcwele bam, ndathi, Inene, andiyi kumxokisa uDavide;</li>
      <li>Imbewu yakhe iya kubakho ngonaphakade, Netrone yakhe njengelanga phambi kwam.</li>
      <li>Iya kuqiniseka njengenyanga ngonaphakade; Ingqina lasesibhakabhakeni lithembekile. (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Kwawena umhlambile, umcekisile, Umphuphumele ngomsindo umthanjiswa wakho;</li>
      <li>Uthe nethe ngumnqophiso womkhonzi wakho; Usidyobhile emhlabeni isithsaba sakhe.</li>
      <li>Uzityhobozile zonke iintango zakhe, Uzenze inxuwa iinqaba zakhe.</li>
      <li>Bayamphanga bonke abadlula ngendlela, Waba yingcikivo kubamelwane bakhe.</li>
      <li>Usiphakamisile isandla sokunene sabambandezelayo,  Uzivuyisile zonke iintshaba zakhe.</li>
      <li>Wabuyisa nokubuyisa uhlangothi lwekrele lakhe, Akwammisa emfazweni.</li>
      <li>Umsusile enkazimlweni yakhe, Uyikhahlele emhlabeni itrone yakhe,</li>
      <li>Uyinqumle imihla yobutsha bakhe, Wamthi wambu ngokudana.  (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Kunini na, Yehova, uhleli uzisithelisile, Busitsha njengomlilo ubushushu bakho?</li>
      <li>Khumbula ukunqamka kwam, into okuyiyo! Ubadaleleni na,  baba yinto engento bonke oonyana babantu?</li>
      <li>Yiyiphi na indoda ehleliyo, engayi kukubona ukufa,  Enokuwusindisa umphefumlo wayo esandleni selabafileyo?  (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Ziphi na iinceba zakho zangaphambili, Nkosi yam,  Owamfungela zona uDavide ngokuthembeka kwakho?</li>
      <li>Khumbula, Nkosi yam, ukungcikiveka kwabakhonzi bakho;  Ndithwele esifubeni sam zonke izizwe ezininzi,</li>
      <li>Ezingcikivayo, ziziintshaba zakho, Yehova; Ezingcikiva amanyathela omthanjiswa wakho.</li>
      <li>Makabongwe uYehova ngonaphakade. Amen, amen.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Umthandazo kaMoses, umfo wakwaThixo. Nkosi yam, ulikhaya wena kuthi, Isizukulwana ngesizukulwana.</li>
      <li>Kungekazalwa zintaba, Ungekavelisi mhlaba, nazwe limiweyo,  Kususela kwaphakade kude kuse ephakadeni, wena unguThixo.</li>
      <li>Umbuyisela umntu eluthulini, Uthi, Buyani, nyana babantu.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba iwaka leminyaka emehlweni akho Linjengemini yezolo,  xa idluleyo, Linjengomlindo wasebusuku.</li>
      <li>Uyabakhukulisa, balale; Ngengomso babuya bahlume njengotyani.</li>
      <li>Ngomso butyatyamba, bubuye buhlume; Ngokuhlwa buyasikwa bome.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba siyaphela ngumsindo wakho, Sikhwankqiswe bubushushu bakho.</li>
      <li>Ububeke ubugwenxa bethu phambi kwakho, Nesibufihlileyo ububeka ekukhanyiseleni kobuso bakho.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba yonke imihla yethu isangene ngokuphuphuma komsindo wakho, Siyiphelisile iminyaka yethu njengentsebezo.</li>
      <li>Imihla yeminyaka yethu iseminyakeni engamashumi asixhenxe;  Ukuba ithe yaba mininzi kakhulu, iba yiminyaka emashumi asibhozo, Libe ke iqhayiya layo likukwaphuka nokungabi nto yanto, Ngokuba ithe phe yakhawuleza, saphaphazela semka.</li>
      <li>Ngubani na owaziyo amandla omsindo wakho, Nokuphuphuma kwawo, ngoko ufanele ukoyikwa ngako?</li>
      <li>Sazise kanye ukuyibala imihla yethu, Ukuze sizuze intliziyo elumkileyo.</li>
      <li>Buya, Yehova, kunini na? Uzohlwaye ngenxa yabakhonzi bakho.</li>
      <li>Sihluthise kwakusasa ngenceba yakho, Simemelele, sivuye yonke imihla yethu.</li>
      <li>Sivuyise ngangemihla owasicinezela ngayo. Ngangeminyaka esabona ububi ngayo.</li>
      <li>Mayibonakale kubakhonzi bakho imisebenzi yakho,  Nobungangamela bakho koonyana babo.</li>
      <li>Ubumnandi bukaYehova mabube phezu kwethu. Zimasa isenzo sezandla zethu phezu kwethu, Isenzo sezandla zethu usizimase sona.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ohleli esitheni lOsenyangweni, Azilalise emthunzini kaSomandla,</li>
      <li>Uthi kuYehova, Hlathi lam, Mboniselo yam, Thixo wam,  endikholose ngaye!</li>
      <li>Ngokuba ngokwakhe uya kukuhlangula emgibeni womthiyeli,  Endyikityeni yokufa eyeyelisayo.</li>
      <li>Wokugubungela ngeentsiba zakhe, Uzimele phantsi kwamaphiko akhe. Likhaka, yingweletshetshe inyaniso yakhe.</li>
      <li>Akuyi koyikiswa zizothuso ebusuku, Nalutolo lubaleka emini;</li>
      <li>Nandyikitya yakufa ihamba esithokothokweni, Nasifo sibhubhisayo, sibhuqa emini enkulu.</li>
      <li>Kungawa iwaka ecaleni kwakho, Isigidi ngasekunene kwakho,  Kodwa kungasondeli nto kuwe.</li>
      <li>Wokhangela ngamehlo akho odwa, Ukubonele ukubuyekezwa kwabangendawo.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba nguwe, Yehova, ihlathi lam. Umenze Osenyangweni ikhaya lakho.</li>
      <li>Akuyi kuqubisana bubi nawe. Kungafiki sibetho ententeni yakho.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba izithunywa zakhe uziwisele umthetho ngawe, Ukuba zikugcine ezindleleni zakho zonke.</li>
      <li>Zokuthwala wena ngezandla zozibini, Hleze ubetheke ngonyawo lwakho etyeni.</li>
      <li>Wonyathela phezu kwengonyama nephimpi, Uyinyashe ingonyama entsha nenamba ngeenyawo.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba enamathele kum, ndomsiza; Ndimse engxondeni,  ngokuba elazi igama lam.</li>
      <li>Wondibiza, ndiphendule, Ndoba naye embandezelweni;  Ndomhlangula, ndimzukise;</li>
      <li>Ndimanelise ngemihla emide, Ndimbonise ukusindisa kwam.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Umhobe; ingoma, ngemini yesabatha. Kulungile ukubulela kuYehova, Nokulibethela uhadi igama lakho, Wena usenyangweni;</li>
      <li>Ukuyixela kwakusasa inceba yakho, Nokunyanisa kwakho ebusuku,</li>
      <li>Ngoweentambo ezilishumi nangomrhubhe, Ngokulubetha uhadi ngofefe.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba uyandivuyisa, Yehova, ngomsebenzi wakho, Ngezenzo zezandla zakho ndinokumemelela.</li>
      <li>Azizikhulu izenzo zakho, Yehova! Zinzulu kakhulu iingcinga zakho.</li>
      <li>Isityhakala asinakwazi; Isinyabi asikuqondi oko.</li>
      <li>Ekudubuleni kongendawo njengomfuno, Ekutyatyambeni kwabasebenzi bonke bobutshinga, Kukuze batshabalale ngonaphakade.</li>
      <li>Ke wena, Yehova, ungophezulu ngonaphakade.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba uyabona, iintshaba zakho, Yehova, Ngokuba uyabona,  iintshaba zakho ziva kutshabalala; Baya kuchithwa-chithwa bonke abasebenzi bobutshinga.</li>
      <li>Uyaluphakamisa uphondo lwam njengolwenqu; Ndigalelwe ioli entsha.</li>
      <li>Iliso lam liyababonela abandilalelayo, Indlebe yam iyabeva abasukela phezulu kum benobubi.</li>
      <li>Amalungisa aya kudubula njengesundu, Aya kukhula njengomsedare weLebhanon.</li>
      <li>Etyelwe nje endlwini kaYehova, Aya kutyatyamba ezintendelezweni zoThixo wethu.</li>
      <li>Aya kuhluma eselenezimvi, Aya kuba etyebile, eluhlaza;</li>
      <li>Ukuze axele ukuba uthe tye uYehova, Uliwa lam, kungekho bugqwetha kuye.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
