      <li>UYehova ungukumkani, uzambathise ubungangamsha; UYehova uzambathise, ubhinqe, amandla; Lizinzile ke elimiweyo,  alinakushukunyiswa.</li>
      <li>Kususela koko, izinzile itrone yakho; Kususela kwaphakade,  ukho wena.</li>
      <li>Imilambo iphakamisile, Yehova, Imilambo iphakamise isandi sayo, Imilambo iphakamise ingxolo yayo.</li>
      <li>Ngaphezu kwezandi zamanzi amaninzi Angangamsha, ngaphezu kwamaza alwayo olwandle, Unobungangamsha phezulu uYehova.</li>
      <li>Izingqiniso zakho zinyanise kunene, Ubungcwele buyifanele indlu yakho, Yehova, imihla emide.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Thixo wempindezelo, Yehova, Thixo wempindezelo, bengezela!</li>
      <li>Phakama, Mgwebi wehlabathi! Babuyisele impatho yabo abanekratshi.</li>
      <li>Kunini na abangendawo, Yehova, Kunini na abangendawo bevuyelela?</li>
      <li>Balephuza amagwebu, bathetha ngokusa, Bayandolosa bonke abasebenzi bobutshinga.</li>
      <li>Batyumza abantu bakho, Yehova, Bacinezela ilifa lakho.</li>
      <li>Babulala umhlolokazi nowasemzini, Bancinitha inkedama.</li>
      <li>Bathi ke, Akaboni uYehova, Akagqali uThixo kaYakobi.</li>
      <li>Qondani, nina bazizityhakala ebantwini; Nina zinyabi, niya kuqiqa nini na?</li>
      <li>Omilisele indlebe, akayi kuva na? Obumbe iliso, akayi kukhangela na?</li>
      <li>Umthethisi weentlanga akayi kohlwaya na, Ulofundisa abantu ukwazi?</li>
      <li>UYehova ngumazi weengcinga zabantu, Ukuba zingumphunga.</li>
      <li>Hayi, uyolo lwendoda oyithethisayo, Yehova, Oyifundisayo ngomyalelo wakho;</li>
      <li>Ukuba uyizolise eziminini zobubi, Ade ambelwe isihogo ongendawo.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba uYehova akabalahli abantu bakhe, Akalishiyi ilifa lakhe.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba isiko liya kubuyela ebulungiseni, Balilandele bonke abantliziyo zithe tye.</li>
      <li>Ngubani na oya kusukela phezulu kubo abanobubi, ngenxa yam? Ngubani na oya kumelana nabasebenzi bobutshinga, ngenxa yam?</li>
      <li>Koko uYehova abe luncedo lwam, Umphefumlo wam unge uhle msinya, waya apho kuthiwa cwaka khona.</li>
      <li>Ukuba ndithi, Lwatyibilika unyawo lwam, Isuka inceba yakho, Yehova, indixhase.</li>
      <li>Ebuninzini beengcinga-ngcinga zam ngaphakathi kwam,  Iintuthuzelo zakho ziyawuyolisa umphefumlo wam.</li>
      <li>Ingaqhelana nawe na itrone yolweyeliselo, Ebumba ububi ngommiselo?</li>
      <li>Bahlanganyela umphefumlo welungisa, Baligwebe igazi elimsulwa.</li>
      <li>Kanti ke uYehova uyingxonde kum, UThixo wam liliwa endizimela ngalo.</li>
      <li>Ububuyisela phezu kwabo ubutshinga babo, Uba bhangisa ngobubi babo; Uya kubabhangisa uYehova, uThixo wethu.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Yizani simemelele kuYehova, Sidume kwiliwa lokusindiswa kwethu.</li>
      <li>Masize phambi kobuso bakhe sinombulelo, Masidume kuye ngeengoma.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba uThixo omkhulu nguYehova, NguKumkani omkhulu ngaphezu koothixo bonke.</li>
      <li>Uzisesandleni sakhe iingontsingontsi zehlabathi, Neencopho zeentaba zezakhe.</li>
      <li>Ulolwakhe ulwandle, nguyena walwenzayo; Nomhlaba owomileyo zawubumba izandla zakhe.</li>
      <li>Yizani, masiqubude, siguqe, Sithobe phambi koYehova umenzi wethu.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba nguThixo wethu yena, Thina ke singabantu bokwaluswa nguye, nezimvu zesandla sakhe. Namhla, ukuba ninokuliva izwi lakhe,</li>
      <li>Musani ukuyenza lukhuni intliziyo yenu, njengaseMeribha,  Njengemini yaseMasa entlango;</li>
      <li>Oko bandilingayo ooyihlo. Bandicikida, bewubona umsebenzi wam.</li>
      <li>Iminyaka yaba ngamashumi amane ndikruqukile sesi sizukulwana, Ndathi, Ngabantu abantliziyo zindwendwayo, Abazazi iindlela zam bona;</li>
      <li>Endada ndafunga ndinomsindo, ukuthi, Inene, abasayi kungena ekuphumleni kwam.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Vumani kuYehova ingoma entsha, Vumani kuYehova, nonke hlabathi.</li>
      <li>Vumani kuYehova, bongani igama lakhe, Shumayelani iimini ngeemini iindaba ezilungileyo zosindiso lwakhe.</li>
      <li>Balisani ezintlangeni uzuko lwakhe, Balisani ezizweni zonke imisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo;</li>
      <li>Ngokuba mkhulu uYehova, engowokudunyiswa kunene; Uyoyikeka yena ngaphezu koothixo bonke.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba bonke oothixo bezizwe abanto zanto; UYehova yena wenza amazulu.</li>
      <li>Yindili nobungangamela phambi kwakhe, Ngamandla nokuhomba engcweleni yakhe.</li>
      <li>Mnikeni uYehova, nina mizalwane yezizwe, Mnikeni uYehova uzuko namandla;</li>
      <li>Mnikeni uYehova uzuko lwegama lakhe; Thwalani umnikelo,  nize ezintendelezweni zakhe.</li>
      <li>Mnquleni uYehova, nivethe ezingcwele, Thuthumelani phambi kwakhe, nonke hlabathi.</li>
      <li>Yithini ezintlangeni, UYehova ngukumkani, Liya kuzinza ngoko elimiweyo, lingashukumi, Uya kugweba phakathi kwezizwe ngokuthe tye.</li>
      <li>Liya kuvuya izulu, Ligcobe ihlabathi; Luya kugquma ulwandle, nenzaliseko yalo.</li>
      <li>Liya kudlamka ilizwe, nento yonke ekulo, Ize imemelele yonke imithi yehlathi</li>
      <li>Phambi koYehova, ngokuba esiza, Ngokuba esiza kugweba ihlabathi. Uya kuligweba elimiweyo ngobulungisa, Nezizwe ngokunyanisa kwakhe.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>UYehova ngukumkani; liyagcoba ihlabathi, Ziyavuya iziqithi ezininzi.</li>
      <li>Ngamafu nesithokothoko ngeenxa zonke kuye, Bubulungisa nokusesikweni ummiso wetrone yakhe.</li>
      <li>Kuhamba umlilo phambi kwakhe; Ulenya ababandezeli bakhe ngeenxa zonke.</li>
      <li>Ikhanyisa elimiweyo imibane yakhe; Uyabona umhlaba,  uzibhija-bhije.</li>
      <li>Iintaba zinyibilika njengomthwebeba phambi koYehova, Phambi kweNkosi yehlabathi lonke.</li>
      <li>Izulu lixela ubulungisa bakhe, Zilubone uzuko lwakhe zonke izizwe.</li>
      <li>Badanile bonke abakhonza umfanekiso oqingqiweyo, Abaqhayisa ngeento ezingento; Bayamnqula bonke oothixo.</li>
      <li>Iyeva, iyavuya iZiyon, Ziyagcoba iintombi zakwaYuda, Ngenxa yemigwebo yakho, Yehova.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba nguwe, Yehova, Osenyangweni phezu kwehlabathi lonke; Unyukile kunene ngaphezu koothixo bonke.</li>
      <li>Bathandi bakaYehova, kuthiyeni okubi. Umgcini wemiphefumlo yabenceba bakhe Uya kubahlangula esandleni sabangendawo.</li>
      <li>Ukukhanya likuhlwayelelwe ilungisa, Novuyo baluhlwayelelwe abantliziyo zithe tye.</li>
      <li>Vuyani ngoYehova, malungisa, Nibulele isikhumbuzo sakhe esingcwele.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Umhobe. Vumani kuYehova ingoma entsha, Ngokuba wenze imisebenzi ebalulekileyo; Simzuzele uloyiso isandla sakhe sokunene, nengalo yakhe engcwele.</li>
      <li>Ulwazisile uYehova usindiso lwakhe, Ubutyhilile emehlweni eentlanga ubulungisa bakhe.</li>
      <li>Ukhumbule inceba yakhe nokunyanisa kwakhe kwindlu kaSirayeli; Zilubonile zonke iziphelo zehlabathi usindiso loThixo wethu.</li>
      <li>Dumani kuYehova, nonke hlabathi, Gqobhokelani ekumemeleleni, nibethe uhadi.</li>
      <li>Mbetheleni uhadi uYehova, Uhadi nelizwi lengoma;</li>
      <li>Ngamaxilongo nezwi lesigodlo Dumani phambi koKumkani uYehova.</li>
      <li>Malugqume ulwandle nenzaliseko yalo, Elimiweyo nabemi balo.</li>
      <li>Imilambo mayibethe izandla, Zimemelele kunye iintaba</li>
      <li>Phambi koYehova, ngokuba esiza kugweba ihlabathi. Uya kuligweba elimiweyo ngobulungisa, Izizwe ngokuthe tye.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>UYehova nguKumkani, ziyagungqa izizwe; Ulohlala ekerubhini,  liyashukuma ihlabathi.</li>
      <li>UYehova mkhulu eZiyon; Uphakamile ngaphezu kwezizwe zonke.</li>
      <li>Baya kulibulela igama lakho elikhulu eloyikekayo; Ngokuba ungcwele yena.</li>
      <li>Amandla okumkani athanda okusesikweni; Uwazimasile wena ngokuthe tye; Wenze okusesikweni nobulungisa kwaYakobi wena.</li>
      <li>Mphakamiseni uYehova, uThixo wethu, Niqubude esitulweni seenyawo zakhe; Ngokuba ungcwele yena.</li>
      <li>OoMoses noAron phakathi kwababingeleli bakhe, NoSamuweli phakathi kwabalinqulayo igama lakhe, Baye bebiza kuYehova,  wabaphendula yena.</li>
      <li>Wathetha kubo esemqulwini welifu; Bazigcina izingqino zakhe, Nommiselo awabanika wona.</li>
      <li>Yehova, Thixo wethu, wabaphendula wena, Waba nguThixo oxolelayo kubo, Ongoziphindezelayo iintlondi zabo.</li>
      <li>Mphakamiseni uYehova, uThixo wethu, Niqubude entabeni yakhe engcwele; Ngokuba ungcwele uYehova uThixo wethu.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Umhobe wombingelelo wokubulela. Dumani kuYehova, nonke hlabathi.</li>
      <li>Mkhonzeni uYehova nivuya; Yizani phambi kwakhe nimemelela.</li>
      <li>Yazini ukuba uYehova nguThixo yena; Wasenza yena,  asisithi; Singabantu bakhe nezimvu ezaluswa nguye.</li>
      <li>Ngenani emasangweni akhe nibulela, Ezintendelezweni zakhe nidumisa; Bulelani kuye, bongani igama lakhe.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba uYehova ulungile, Inceba yakhe ingunaphakade,  Ukunyaniseka kwakhe kukwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>EkaDavide. Umhobe. Ndiya kuvuma ngenceba nangomgwebo;  Ndiya kukubethela uhadi, Yehova.</li>
      <li>Ndiya kuqiqa indlela yengqibelelo; Uya kuza nini na kum?  Ndiya kuhamba ngengqibelelo yentliziyo yam Phakathi kwendlu yam.</li>
      <li>Andiyi kubeka phambi kwamehlo am Nto inobutshijolo.  Ukwenza ngokunxaxha ndikuthiyile, Akuyi kunamathela kum.</li>
      <li>Intliziyo ejibilizayo iya kukhwelela kude kum; Into embi andiyi kuyazi.</li>
      <li>Omhlebayo ummelwane wakhe ngasese, Lowo ndiya kumbhangisa.  Omehlo aqwayingileyo, ontliziyo igungubeleyo, Lowo andinakumthwala.</li>
      <li>Amehlo am akwabanyanisayo ezweni, Ukuba bandiphahle;  Ohamba ngendlela yengqibelelo, Lowo makandilungiselele.</li>
      <li>Akayi kuhlala phakathi kwendlu yam Owenza inkohliso;  Othetha ubuxoki akayi kuqina Phambi kwamehlo am.</li>
      <li>Imiso ngemiso, ndiya kubabhangisa Bonke abangendawo belizwe, Ukuze ndibanqumle emzini kaYehova Bonke abasebenzi bobutshinga.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Umthandazo wolusizana xa atyhafileyo, ephalaza iinkalazo zakhe phambi koYehova. Yehova, wuve umthandazo wam, Kufike kuwe ukuzibika kwam.</li>
      <li>Musa ukubusithelisa ubuso bakho kum ngemini yokubandezelwa kwam, Ndithobele indlebe yakho; Ngemini endidanduluka ngayo khawuleza undiphendule.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba iyaphela imihla yam njengomsi; Amathambo am avutha njengeziko.</li>
      <li>Ibethwe yoma njengomfuno intliziyo yam, Ngokuba ndilibele nokudla ukudla kwam.</li>
      <li>Ngenxa yezwi lokugcuma kwam Amathambo am atshele enyameni yam.</li>
      <li>Ndifana nengcwangube yentlango, Ndinjengesikhova sasemanxoweni.</li>
      <li>Andilali; Ndinjengentaka eyodwa phezu kwendlu.</li>
      <li>Imini yonke ziyandingcikiva iintshaba zam, Abandigezelayo bathuka ngam.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba ndidle uthuthu njengesonka, Into endiyiselayo ndiyiphithikeze nezililo,</li>
      <li>Ngenxa yokubhabhama kwakho noburhalarhume bakho; Ngokuba undifunqule wandilahla.</li>
      <li>Imihla yam injengokoluka kwamathunzi; Mna ndomile njengomfuno.</li>
      <li>Ke wena, Yehova, uhleli ngonaphakade, Inkumbuzo yakho ikwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana.</li>
      <li>Uya kusuk ume, uyiphathe iZiyon ngemfesane; Ngokuba lixesha lokuyibabala eli, ngokuba lifikile ixesha elimisiweyo.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba abakhonzi bakho bakholiswe ngamatye ayo, Uthuli lwayo banofefe ngalo.</li>
      <li>Ziya kuloyika iintlanga igama likaYehova, Nookumkani bonke behlabathi ubuqaqawuli bakho;</li>
      <li>Ngokuba eyakhile iZiyon uYehova, Wabonakala ebuqaqawulini bakhe.</li>
      <li>Uwubhekile umthandazo wabachushuluzayo, Akawudela umthandazo wabo.</li>
      <li>Oko kuya kubhalelwa isizukulwana esizayo, Abantu abaza kudalwa badumise uYehova.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba uqondele, esendaweni yakhe ephezulu engcwele;  Wondela ehlabathini esemazulwini uYehova,</li>
      <li>Ukuba akuve ukugcuma kwabakhonkxiweyo, Abakhulule oonyana bokufa;</li>
      <li>Bancokole eZiyon ngegama likaYehova, Ngendumiso yakhe eYerusalem;</li>
      <li>Ekubuthelaneni kwezizwe ndawonye, Nezikumkani, ukuba zikhonze uYehova.</li>
      <li>Uwathobile endleleni amandla am, Uyinqamle imihla yam.</li>
      <li>Ndithi, Thixo wam, musa ukundisusa phakathi kwemihla yam.  Ikwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana iminyaka yakho.</li>
      <li>Waliseka kudala ihlabathi; Lisisenzo sezandla zakho izulu.</li>
      <li>Ezo zinto ziya kudaka, wena ke ume; Zona zonke ziya konakala njengengubo, Wozigugisa njengesambatho, ziguge;</li>
      <li>Ke wena uhleli unguwe, Iminyaka yakho ayinakuphela.</li>
      <li>Oonyana babakhonzi bakho baya kuhlala, Imbewu yabo izimaseke phambi kwakho.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>EkaDavide. Mbonge uYehova, mphefumlo wam, Ilibonge igama lakhe elingcwele into yonke engaphakathi kwam.</li>
      <li>Mbonge uYehova, mphefumlo wam, Ungayilibali yonke impatho yakhe entle:</li>
      <li>Uloxolela bonke ubugwenxa bakho; Ulophilisa zonke izifo zakho;</li>
      <li>Ulokhulula ubomi bakho esihogweni, Akuthi jize ngenceba nemfesane;</li>
      <li>Lo uwuzalisayo umlomo wakho ngento elungileyo, Buhlaziyeke ubutsha bakho njengobokhozi.</li>
      <li>NguYehova umenzi wemisebenzi yobulungisa, Nezigwebo ngenxa yabacudisiweyo bonke;</li>
      <li>Umazisi weendlela zakhe kuMoses, Wezenzo zakhe ezincamisayo koonyana bakaSirayeli.</li>
      <li>Unemfesane enobabalo uYehova, Uzeka kade umsindo, mkhulu ngenceba.</li>
      <li>Akaphiki kuphele, Akawugcini umsindo ngonaphakade.</li>
      <li>Akenzi kuthi ngokwezono zethu, Akasiphathi ngokobugwenxa bethu;</li>
      <li>Ngokuba injengokuphakama kwezulu phezu komhlaba, Ukuba namandla, inceba yakhe kwabamoyikayo;</li>
      <li>Kunjengokuba kude kwempumalanga entshonalanga,  Ukulukhwelelisa kwakhe kuthi ukreqo lwethu;</li>
      <li>Kunjengokusikwa yimfesane koyise kubantwana, Ukusikwa yimfesane kukaYehova kwabamoyikayo.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba uyakwazi yena ukubunjwa kwethu, Ekhumbula ukuba siluthuli.</li>
      <li>Hayi, umntu! Injengotyani imihla yakhe; Njengentyantyambo yasendle, kunjalo ukutyatyamba kwakhe.</li>
      <li>Xa uthe umoya wadlula kuyo, ayibikho, Ingabi sazana nayo indawo yayo.</li>
      <li>Ke yona inceba kaYehova ikwabamoyikayo, kususela kwaphakade kude kuse ephakadeni, Nobulungisa bakhe bukoonyana boonyana;</li>
      <li>Kwabawugcinileyo umnqophiso wakhe, Kwabazikhumbulayo iziyalezo zakhe ukuba bazenze.</li>
      <li>UYehova uyizinzisile emazulwini itrone yakhe, Ubukumkani bakhe bulawula into yonke.</li>
      <li>Mbongeni uYehova, nina zithunywa zakhe, Magorha omeleleyo, alenzayo ilizwi lakhe, Ephulaphula isandi selizwi lakhe.</li>
      <li>Mbongeni uYehova, nonke mikhosi yakhe, Balungiseleli bakhe, benzi bokuthanda kwakhe.</li>
      <li>Mbongeni uYehova, nonke zenzo zakhe, Ezindaweni zonke zobukumkani bakhe. Mbonge uYehova, mphefumlo wam.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Mbonge uYehova, mphefumlo wam. Yehova, Thixo wam, umkhulu kakhulu; Wambethe indili nobungangamela.</li>
      <li>Ulothi wambu ukukhanya njengengubo. Ulolaneka izulu njengelengalenga lentente;</li>
      <li>Ulohlanganisa emanzini imiqadi yamagumbi akhe aphezulu;  Ulowenza amafu inqwelo yakhe, Ulohamba ngamaphiko omoya;</li>
      <li>Ulowenza izithunywa zakhe imimoya, Abalungiseleli bakhe umlilo olenyayo.</li>
      <li>Waliseka ihlabathi phezu kwemimiso yalo, Ukuba lingashukunyiswa naphakade kanaphakade.</li>
      <li>Waligubungela ngamanzi anzongonzongo njengesambatho, Ema amanzi phezu kweentaba.</li>
      <li>Ekukhalimeni kwakho asaba, Ezwini lendudumo yakho abaleka buphuthuphuthu;</li>
      <li>Kwenyuka iintaba, kwehla izihlambo, Aya kuloo ndawo ubuwasekele yona.</li>
      <li>Wamisa umda ukuba angegqithi, Angabuye awugubungele umhlaba.</li>
      <li>Ulothuma imithombo iye ezihlanjeni; Ihamba phakathi kweentaba;</li>
      <li>Iseza zonke iinyamakazi zasendle; Amaesile asendle aqabula inxano lawo.</li>
      <li>Kuhlala phezu kwayo iintaka zezulu, Zitsholoza phakathi kwamasebe;</li>
      <li>Uloseza iintaba kumagumbi akhe aphezulu; Uyahlutha umhlaba ziziqhamo zezenzo zakho.</li>
      <li>Ulontshulisela iinkomo utyani, Nomfuno wokunceda umntu;  Ukuze kuphume isonka emhlabeni.</li>
      <li>Iwayini iyivuyise intliziyo yomntu; Bukhazimle ubuso ngeoli, Isonka siyixhase intliziyo yomntu.</li>
      <li>Iyahlutha imithi kaYehova, Imisedare yaseLebhanon awayityalayo,</li>
      <li>Apho zakhela khona iintaka; Ingwamza, isemisipresini indlu yayo.</li>
      <li>Iintaba zona ezo ziphakamileyo zezamagogo, Amawa azimela iimbila.</li>
      <li>Inyanga wayenzela amaxesha ayo, Ilanga liyakwazi ukutshona kwalo.</li>
      <li>Wenza ubumnyama wena, kube sebusuku, Ashukume ngabo onke amarhamncwa ehlathi.</li>
      <li>Iingonyama ezintsha zigqumela ukuqwenga, Zifuna ukudla kwazo kuThixo.</li>
      <li>Lakuthi chapha ilanga, ziyahlanganisana, Zibuthume ezikhundleni zazo.</li>
      <li>Uyaphuma umntu aye emsebenzini wakhe Nasenkonzweni yakhe,  ahlwise.</li>
      <li>Hayi, ukuba zininzi izenzo zakho, Yehova! Zonke ziphela uzenze ngobululumko; Uzele umhlaba zizidalwa zakho.</li>
      <li>Nalo ulwandle lulukhulu, lubanzi ngeenxa zombini; Kulapho kuzinambuzane zingenakubalwa, Ezincinane kwanezikhulu izinto eziphilileyo.</li>
      <li>Kulapho kuhamba iinqanawa; Nango umnenga owawubumbela ukudlala kulo.</li>
      <li>Zonke ezo nto ziphela zikhangele kuwe, Ukuba uzinike ukudla kwazo ngexesha elililo.</li>
      <li>Uyazinika, ziyachola; Uyasivula isandla sakho, ziyahlutha kokulungileyo.</li>
      <li>Uyabusithelisa ubuso bakho, ziyakhwankqiswa;  Uyawuhlanganisa umoya wazo, ziphume umphefumlo, Zibuyele eluthulini lwazo.</li>
      <li>Uthuma umoya wakho, ziyadalwa, Ubuhlaziye ubuso bomhlaba.</li>
      <li>Ubuqaqawuli bukaYehova mabube ngunaphakade; UYehova makavuye ngezenzo zakhe;</li>
      <li>Ulobheka emhlabeni, uzamazame; Uchukumisa iintaba,  ziqhume.</li>
      <li>Ndiya kuvuma kuYehova lo gama ndidla ubomi, Ndiya kumbethela uhadi uThixo wam ekubeni ndingokhoyo.</li>
      <li>Makube nencasa kuye ukucamngca kwam; Mna ndiya kuvuya ngoYehova.</li>
      <li>Mabagqitywe ehlabathini aboni, Bangabi sabakho abangendawo. Mbonge uYehova, mphefumlo wam, Haleluya!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Bulelani kuYehova, nqulani igama lakhe; Yazisani ezizweni izenzo zakhe ezincamisileyo.</li>
      <li>Vumani kuye, mbetheleni uhadi; Xoxani ngemisebenzi yakhe yonke ebalulekileyo.</li>
      <li>Qhayisani ngegama lakhe elingcwele; Mayivuye intliziyo yabamquqelayo uYehova.</li>
      <li>Ngxamelani uYehova namandla akhe; Funani ubuso bakhe ngamaxesha onke.</li>
      <li>Khumbulani imisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo awayenzayo,  Izimanga zakhe, nezigwebo zomlomo wakhe,</li>
      <li>Mbewu ka-Abraham, yomkhonzi wakhe, Nyana bakaYakobi,  banyulwa bakhe.</li>
      <li>NguYehova uThixo wethu yena; Zisehlabathini lonke izigwebo zakhe.</li>
      <li>Uwukhumbula ngonaphakade umnqophiso wakhe, Ilizwi awalimisela iwaka lezizukulwana;</li>
      <li>Awanqophisana ngalo noAbraham, Awalifungela uIsake;</li>
      <li>Awalimisayo ukuba libe ngummiselo kuYakobi, Libe ngumnqophiso ongunaphakade kuSirayeli;</li>
      <li>Esithi, Ndikunika ilizwe lakwaKanan, Libe licandelo lelifa lenu;</li>
      <li>Besengamadoda ambalwa, Bebancinane, bengabaphambukeli kulo.</li>
      <li>Babehamba besuka kolunye uhlanga, baye kolunye uhlanga,  Besuka kobunye ubukumkani, baye kwabanye abantu.</li>
      <li>Akavumelanga mntu ukuba abacudise, Wohlwaya ookumkani ngenxa yabo;</li>
      <li>Esithi, Musani ukubachukumisa abathanjiswa bam, Musani ukubaphatha kakubi abaprofeti bam.</li>
      <li>Wabiza indlala, yeza phezu kwelizwe, Wawaphula wonke umsimelelo osisonka.</li>
      <li>Wathuma indoda phambi kwabo; Kwathengiswa ngoYosefu, waba likhoboka.</li>
      <li>Bazicinezela iinyawo zakhe ngamakhamandela, Wafika umphefumlo wakhe esinyithini;</li>
      <li>Kwada kwalixesha lokufika kwelizwi lakhe, Intetho kaYehova yamnyibilikisa.</li>
      <li>Ukumkani wathuma, wamkhulula, Umlawuli wezizwe wamvulela;</li>
      <li>Wamenza inkosi yendlu yakhe, Umlawuli wemfuyo yakhe yonke,</li>
      <li>Ukuba abakhonkxe abathetheli bakhe ngokuzithandela kwakhe, Amadoda akhe amakhulu awafundise ubulumko.</li>
      <li>Waza uSirayeli waya eYiputa, UYakobi waphambukela ezweni lakwaHam.</li>
      <li>Wabaqhamisa kakhulu abantu bakhe, Wabomeleza ngaphezu kwababandezeli babo.</li>
      <li>Wazijika iintliziyo zabo, ukuba babathiye abantu bakhe,  Babaqhathanisele abakhonzi bakhe.</li>
      <li>Wathuma uMoses, umkhonzi wakhe, NoAron awamnyulayo.</li>
      <li>Bazenza kubo iindawo zemiqondiso yakhe, Nezimanga zakhe ezweni lakwaHam.</li>
      <li>Wathumela ubumnyama, kwaba mnyama; Ababa nakuwaphikisa amazwi akhe.</li>
      <li>Wawaguqula amanzi abo, aba ligazi, Wazibulala iintlanzi zabo.</li>
      <li>Ilizwe labo lanyakazela amasele Ezingontsini zookumkani babo.</li>
      <li>Wathetha, zafika izibawu, Iingcongconi, emideni yabo yonke.</li>
      <li>Wabanika isichotho, saba yimvula; Umlilo walenya ezweni labo.</li>
      <li>Wayibetha imidiliya yabo nemikhiwane yabo, Wayishwaqa imithi yemida yabo.</li>
      <li>Wathetha, kwafika iinkumbi ezandayo, Nezikhothululayo,  into engenakubalwa;</li>
      <li>Zayidla imifuno yonke ezweni labo, Zazidla iziqhamo zomhlaba wabo.</li>
      <li>Waza wababulala bonke abamazibulo ezweni labo, Intlahlela yamandla abo onke.</li>
      <li>Wabakhupha ke abakhe benesilivere negolide, Akwabakho ukhubekayo ezizweni zakhe.</li>
      <li>Lavuya iYiputa ekuphumeni kwabo, Ngokuba lifikelwe kukunkwantyisa kwabo.</li>
      <li>Waneka ilifu lokubasitha, Nomlilo wokukhanyisa ebusuku.</li>
      <li>Babiza, wazisa izagwityi, Wabahluthisa nangesonka sasezulwini.</li>
      <li>Wavula iliwa, abaleka amanzi, Ahamba engumlambo emqwebedwini.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba wakhumbula ilizwi lakhe elingcwele, Wakhumbula uAbraham umkhonzi wakhe.</li>
      <li>Wabakhupha abantu bakhe benemihlali, Abanyulwa bakhe bememelela.</li>
      <li>Wabanika amazwe eentlanga, Bayihlutha inzuzo yokwaphuka kwezizwe,</li>
      <li>Ukuze bayigcine imimiselo yakhe, Bayibambe imiyalelo yakhe. Haleluya!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Haleluya! Bulelani kuYehova, ngokuba elungile, Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</li>
      <li>Ngubani na onokuzixela izenzo zobugorha bukaYehova,  Onokuyivakalisa yonke indumiso yakhe?</li>
      <li>Hayi, uyolo lwabaligcinayo isiko, Lwabenza ubulungisa ngamaxesha onke!</li>
      <li>Ndikhumbule, Yehova, ekwenzeni kwakho isisa kubantu bakho;  Ndiyelele ngosindiso lwakho,</li>
      <li>Ukuze ndibone inyhweba yabanyulwa bakho, Ndivuye ekuvuyeni kohlanga lwakho, Ndiqhayise kunye nelifa lakho.</li>
      <li>Sonile, thina noobawo; Senze ubugwenxa, senze okungendawo.</li>
      <li>Oobawo abayiqiqanga eYiputa imisebenzi yakho ebalulekileyo; Ababukhumbulanga ubuninzi beenceba zakho;  Baphika elwandle, eLwandle oluBomvu.</li>
      <li>Wabasindisa ngenxa yegama lakhe, Ukuze abazise ubugorha bakhe.</li>
      <li>Walukhalimela uLwandle oluBomvu, loma, Wabahambisa emanzini anzongonzongo kwanga kusentlango.</li>
      <li>Wabasindisa esandleni sobathiyayo, Wabakhulula esandleni sotshaba.</li>
      <li>Amanzi abagubungela ababandezeli babo, Akwasala namnye kubo.</li>
      <li>Bakholwa ke ngamazwi akhe, Bayivuma indumiso yakhe.</li>
      <li>Kanti bahle bazilibala izenzo zakhe, Abalilinda icebo lakhe.</li>
      <li>Bakhanukile entlango, Bamlinga uThixo enkangala.</li>
      <li>Wabanika abakubizayo; Wathumela ukungcumbeka emphefumlweni wabo.</li>
      <li>Bamenzela umona uMoses eminqubeni, NoAron ongcwele kaYehova.</li>
      <li>Wavuleka umhlaba, wamginya uDatan, Waliselela ibandla lika-Abhiram;</li>
      <li>Umlilo walitshisa ibandla labo, Amalangatye abalenya abangendawo.</li>
      <li>Benza ithole eHorebhe, Baqubuda emfanekisweni otyhidiweyo.</li>
      <li>Balwananisa uzuko lwabo Ngento emilise okwenkomo edla utyani.</li>
      <li>Bamlibala uThixo, umsindisi wabo, Owenza imisebenzi emikhulu eYiputa;</li>
      <li>Imisebenzi ebalulekileyo ezweni lakwaHam, Imisebenzi eyoyikekayo eLwandle oluBomvu.</li>
      <li>Wathi uya kubatshabalalisa, Koko wesukayo uMoses,  umnyulwa wakhe, Wema ethubeni phambi kwakhe, Ebuyisa ubushushu bakhe, ukuba angatshabalalisi.</li>
      <li>Balicekisa ilizwe elinqwenelekayo, Abakholwa lilizwi lakhe,</li>
      <li>Bakrokra ezintenteni zabo, Abaliphulaphula izwi likaYehova.</li>
      <li>Wabaphakamisela isandla sakhe, Wafungela ukuba abawise entlango;</li>
      <li>Ayiwise imbewu yabo phakathi kweentlanga, Abachithachithe emazweni.</li>
      <li>Bazibandakanya noBhahali-pehore, Badla imibingelelo yabafileyo,</li>
      <li>Bamqumbisa ngeentlondi zabo; Sagaleleka phakathi kwabo isibetho.</li>
      <li>Wesuka wema uPinehasi, walamla; Sathintelwa isibetho.</li>
      <li>Oko kwabalelwa kuye ekuthini bubulungisa Izizukulwana ngezizukulwana kude kuse ephakadeni.</li>
      <li>Bamqumbisa emanzini aseMeribha, Kwehla ububi kuMoses ngenxa yabo;</li>
      <li>Ngokuba bawuphikisa umoya wakhe, Waphololoza ke ngomlomo wakhe.</li>
      <li>Abazitshabalalisa izizwe, Awayethethe ngazo kubo uYehova;</li>
      <li>Baxubana neentlanga ezo, Bafunda izenzo zazo;</li>
      <li>Bakhonza izithixo zazo, Yaba sisirhintyelo kubo.</li>
      <li>Babingelela ngoonyana babo nangeentombi zabo kwiidemon;</li>
      <li>Baphalaza igazi elimsulwa, Igazi loonyana babo neleentombi zabo, Ababingelela ngabo kwizithixo zakwaKanan;  Lahlanjelwa ilizwe ngamagazi.</li>
      <li>Baba ziinqambi ngezenzo zabo, Bahenyuza ngeentlondi zabo.</li>
      <li>Wavutha ke umsindo kaYehova kubantu bakhe, Laba lisikizi kuye ilifa lakhe.</li>
      <li>Wabanikela ezandleni zeentlanga, Balawulwa ngababathiyileyo.</li>
      <li>Zabaxina iintshaba zabo, Bathotyelwa phantsi kwezandla zazo.</li>
      <li>Zibe zininzi izihlandlo ebahlangula; Ke bona bamphikisa ngamaqhinga abo, Bonakala bubugwenxa babo.</li>
      <li>Noko ke wakunonelela ukubandezelwa kwabo, Akuva ukuhlahlamba kwabo.</li>
      <li>Wawukhumbula ngenxa yabo umnqophiso wakhe, Wazohlwaya ngenxa yobuninzi beenceba zakhe.</li>
      <li>Wabafumanisa imfesane Phambi kwabo bonke abaye bebathimbile.</li>
      <li>Sisindise, Yehova, Thixo wethu, Sibuthe ezintlangeni,  Ukuze sibulele kwigama lakho elingcwele, Sizingce ngendumiso yakho.</li>
      <li>Makabongwe uYehova, uThixo kaSirayeli, Kususela kwaphakade kude kuse ephakadeni. Mabathi bonke abantu, Amen.  Haleluya!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Bulelani kuYehova, ngokuba elungile, Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</li>
      <li>Mabatsho abakhululwa bakaYehova, Awabakhululayo esandleni sombandezeli;</li>
      <li>Wababutha emazweni, Empumalanga nasentshonalanga, Entla naselwandle.</li>
      <li>Badinga entlango, endleleni esenkanga, la, Abafumana mzi wakuhlala.</li>
      <li>Belambile, benxaniwe, Watyhafa phakathi kwabo umphefumlo wabo.</li>
      <li>Bakhala ke kuYehova embandezelweni yabo, Wabahlangula ekucuthekeni kwabo;</li>
      <li>Wabanyathelisa endleleni ethe tye, Ukuba baye kumzi wokuhlala.</li>
      <li>Mabayibulele kuYehova inceba yakhe, Nemisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo koonyana babantu!</li>
      <li>Kuba ewuhluthisile umphefumlo otshobayo, Wawuzalisa ngokulungileyo umphefumlo olambileyo.</li>
      <li>Behleli emnyameni nasethunzini lokufa, Bekhonkxwe yimbandezelo nasisinyithi,</li>
      <li>Ngokuba bephikise amazwi kaThixo, Belitshitshisa icebo lOsenyangweni:</li>
      <li>Wayithoba intliziyo yabo ngokubasebenzisa kanzima;  Bakhubeka, akwabakho mncedi.</li>
      <li>Bakhala ke kuYehova embandezelweni yabo; Wabasindisa ekucuthekeni kwabo.</li>
      <li>Wabakhupha emnyameni nasethunzini lokufa, Waziqhawula iimbophelelo zabo.</li>
      <li>Mabayibulele kuYehova inceba yakhe, Nemisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo koonyana babantu!</li>
      <li>Kuba ezaphule iingcango zobhedu, Wayixakaxa imivalo yesinyithi.</li>
      <li>Abamathileyo, ngenxa yendlela yokukreqa kwabo, Nangenxa yobugwenxa babo, bacinezelwa;</li>
      <li>Konke ukudla kwaba lisikizi kumphefumlo wabo, Bafika emasangweni okufa.</li>
      <li>Bakhala ke kuYehova embandezelweni yabo, Wabasindisa ekucuthekeni kwabo.</li>
      <li>Wathumela ilizwi lakhe, wabaphilisa, Wabasiza ezihogweni zabo.</li>
      <li>Mabayibulele kuYehova inceba yakhe, Nemisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo koonyana babantu!</li>
      <li>Mababingelele imibingelelo yombulelo, Bancokole ngezenzo zakhe bememelela.</li>
      <li>Abaya elwandle ngeenqanawa, Benze ishishini emanzini amaninzi,</li>
      <li>Bazibona bona izenzo zikaYehova, Nemisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo enzulwini.</li>
      <li>Watsho, wavusa umoya ovuthuzayo, Waphakamisa amaza ayo.</li>
      <li>Banyuka basinga ezulwini, behla basinga emanzini enzonzobila; Umphefumlo wabo uthe amandla bububi.</li>
      <li>Bathendeleka, bahexa njengenxila, Butshone bonke ubulumko babo.</li>
      <li>Bakhala ke kuYehova embandezelweni yabo Wabakhupha ekucuthekeni kwabo.</li>
      <li>Ukumisile ukuvuthuza, kwathi cwaka, Amaza ayo azola;</li>
      <li>Bavuya ke, kuba edambile; Wabafikisa echwebeni abalilangazelelayo.</li>
      <li>Mabayibulele kuYehova inceba yakhe, Nemisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo koonyana babantu!</li>
      <li>Mabamphakamise ebandleni labantu, Bamdumise embuthweni yamadoda amakhulu.</li>
      <li>Uyenze imilambo yaba yintlango, Namathende amanzi aba ngumhlaba onxaniweyo;</li>
      <li>Ilizwe elineziqhamo laba leletyuwa, Ngenxa yezinto ezimbi zabemi balo.</li>
      <li>Uyenze intlango yaba lidike elinamanzi, Ilizwe elingumqwebedu laba ngamathende amanzi.</li>
      <li>Wabahlalisa khona abalambileyo, Bamisa umzi wokuhlala.</li>
      <li>Bahlwayela amasimi, batyala izidiliya, Bavelisa iziqhamo,  baba nongeniselo.</li>
      <li>Wabasikelela, banda kunene, Iinkomo zabo akazinciphisa.</li>
      <li>Bancipha, basibekeka Ngokukhanyangwa bububi nesingqala.</li>
      <li>Uwagalele ngendelo amanene, Wawadingisa enyanyeni,  kungekho ndlela.</li>
      <li>Walisa engxondeni ihlwempu, kude nengcinezelo, Walenzela imizalwana yanjengomhlambi.</li>
      <li>Baya kubona abathe tye, bavuye, Bonke ubugqwetha buvale umlomo.</li>
      <li>Lowo ulumkileyo makazigcine ezi ndawo, Azigqale iinceba zikaYehova.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ingoma. Umhobe kaDavide. Izimasekile intliziyo yam,  Thixo, Ndiya kuvuma, ndibethe uhadi, Kwanozuko lwam.</li>
      <li>Vukani, mrhubhe nohadi; Ndiya kusiphangela isifingo.</li>
      <li>Ndiya kubulela kuwe phakathi kwezizwe, Yehova,  Ndikubethele uhadi phakathi kwezizwe.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba inkulu ngaphezu kwezulu inceba yakho, Yada yesa esibhakabhakeni inyaniso yakho.</li>
      <li>Ziphakamise ngaphezu kwezulu, Thixo, Bube phezu kwehlabathi lonke ubuqaqawuli bakho.</li>
      <li>Ukuze zihlangulwe iintanda zakho, Sindisa ngesandla sakho sokunene, undiphendule.</li>
      <li>UThixo uthethe engcwele; mandivuyelele, Ndimabe uShekem,  ndiyilinganisele intili yaseSukoti.</li>
      <li>Ngowam uGiliyadi, ngowam uManase, UEfrayim sisigcina-ntloko sam, UYuda yintonga yam yommiselo;</li>
      <li>UMowabhi sisitya sam sokuhlambela, Ndiyiphosa kuEdom imbadada yam; Ndiduma ngelamaFilisti.</li>
      <li>Ngubani na owondisa emzini onqatyisiweyo, Ngubani na owondikhaphela kwaEdom?</li>
      <li>Asinguwe na, Thixo, lo usihlambileyo? Akwaphuma, Thixo,  nemikhosi yethu.</li>
      <li>Sincede kumbandezeli wethu; Alunto yanto usindiso lomntu.</li>
      <li>NgoThixo siya kweyisa, Abagqushe yena ababandezeli bethu.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli; ekaDavide. Umhobe. Thixo wendumiso yam,  musa ukuthi tu;</li>
      <li>Ngokuba bandakhamisele umlomo ongendawo, nomlomo onenkohliso; Bathetha ngam ngolwimi lobuxoki.</li>
      <li>Bandijikele ngeentetho zentiyo; Balwa nam ngelize.</li>
      <li>Ekubeni mna ndibathanda, bona bayandichasa, Ndibe mna ndithandaza.</li>
      <li>Endaweni yobulungisa bandibuyekeza ngobubi; Ekubeni mna ndibathanda, bona bayandithiya.</li>
      <li>Misa ongendawo, abe ngumveleli wakhe, Eme uSathana ngasekunene kwakhe.</li>
      <li>Ekuthethweni kwetyala makaphume engongendawo, Nomthandazo wakhe ube sisono.</li>
      <li>Imihla yakhe mayibe mbalwa, Mabuthatyathwe ngomnye ubuveleli bakhe.</li>
      <li>Oonyana bakhe mababe ziinkedama, Nomkakhe abe ngumhlolokazi;</li>
      <li>Babhadule bebhadula oonyana bakhe, becela, Bengqiba,  bekude namanxuwa akowabo.</li>
      <li>Umboleki-mali makakushwankathele konke anako, Abasemzini baphange ukuxelenga kwakhe.</li>
      <li>Makungabikho wolulela nceba kuye, Kungabikho uzibabalayo iinkedama zakhe.</li>
      <li>Izivela-mva zakhe mazibe zezokunqunyulwa, Igama lazo licinywe esizukulwaneni esizayo.</li>
      <li>Mabukhunjulwe nguYehova ubugwenxa booyise, Singacinywa isono sonina.</li>
      <li>Masibe phambi koYehova ngamaxesha onke, Akunqumle ehlabathini ukukhunjulwa kwabo;</li>
      <li>Ngenxa enokuba engakukhumbulanga ukwenza inceba,  Etshutshise indoda elusizana, Elihlwempu, enentliziyo eyothukileyo, ukuba ayibulale.</li>
      <li>Ewe, wathanda ukuqalekisa, kwamfikela; Akakufuna ukusikelela, kwakhwelela kude kuye.</li>
      <li>Wambatha ukuqalekisa kwanga yingubo yakhe, Kwangena embilinini wakhe njengamanzi, Nanjengeoli emathanjeni akhe.</li>
      <li>Makube njengengubo kuye, azithe wambu ngayo, Kube luqhwemesha, alunxibe amaxesha onke.</li>
      <li>Nguwo lowo umvuzo wabandichasayo, ophuma kuYehova,  Wabathetha okubi ngomphefumlo wam.</li>
      <li>Ke wena Yehova, Nkosi, ndenzele ngenxa yegama lakho;  Ngokokuba ilungile inceba yakho; ndihlangule.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba ndilusizana, ndilihlwempu, Intliziyo yam ihlatyiwe phakathi kwam.</li>
      <li>Ndinjengethunzi xa lolukayo, ndiyemka; Ndiphetshethwa njengenkumbi.</li>
      <li>Amadolo am ayagexa kukuzila ukudla, Nenyama yam ibhityile, tu ukutyeba.</li>
      <li>Ndithe ndasisingcikivo kubo; Bendibona, bahlunguzela intloko.</li>
      <li>Ndincede, Yehova, Thixo wam, Ndisindise ngokwenceba yakho;</li>
      <li>Bazi ukuba sisandla sakho eso, Ukuba kukwenza kwakho,  Yehova.</li>
      <li>Bayaqalekisa aba, uyasikelela wena; Besukile bema, baya kudana; uya kubuya yena umkhonzi wakho.</li>
      <li>Abandichasayo baya kwambatha ihlazo, Bazithi wambu ukudana njengengubo yokwaleka.</li>
      <li>Ndiya kubulela kakhulu kuYehova ngomlomo wam, Ndimdumise phakathi kwabaninzi;</li>
      <li>Kuba emi ekunene kolihlwempu, Ukuba amsindise kwabawugwebayo umphefumlo wakhe.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>EkaDavide. Umhobe. Utsho uYehova eNkosini yam ukuthi,  Hlala ngasekunene kwam, Ndide iintshaba zakho ndizenze Isitulo seenyawo zakho.</li>
      <li>Intonga yamandla akho uya kuyithumela uYehova, ivela eZiyon, esithi, Yiba nobukhosi phakathi kweentshaba zakho.</li>
      <li>Abantu bakho baya kuzinikela ngeentliziyo, ngemini yakho yokuphuma umkhosi; Bebethe ezingcwele, ekuphumeni kwesifingo,  Uza kuwe umbethe womlisela wakho.</li>
      <li>Ufungile uYehova, akayi kuzohlwaya; uthe, Ungumbingeleli ngonaphakade wena Ngokohlobo lukaMelkitsedeke.</li>
      <li>INkosi ngasekunene kwakho Iya kuphalusa ookumkani ngemini yomsindo wayo.</li>
      <li>Iya kugweba phakathi kweentlanga, kuzale zizidumbu;  Iphaluse intloko ezweni elibanzi.</li>
      <li>Endleleni iya kusela emlanjaneni; Ngenxa yoko iya kuphakamisa intloko.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Haleluya! Ndiya kubulela kuYehova ngentliziyo yonke,  Elucweyweni lwabathe tye nasebandleni.</li>
      <li>Zikhulu izenzo zikaYehova, Zezokungxokwa iintsingiselo zazo zonke.</li>
      <li>Unendili nobungangamela umsebenzi wakhe, Ubulungisa bakhe bumi ngonaphakade.</li>
      <li>Uyenzele ukuze ikhunjulwe imisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo;  Unobabalo nemfesane uYehova.</li>
      <li>Ubaphe ukudla abamoyikayo; Uwukhumbule ngonaphakade umnqophiso wakhe.</li>
      <li>Ubabonise abantu bakhe amandla ezenzo zakhe, Ebanika ilifa leentlanga.</li>
      <li>Izenzo zezandla zakhe ziyinyaniso nesiko; Zithembekile zonke iziyalezo zakhe.</li>
      <li>Zizimasekile nanini nangonaphakade; Zenziwe ngenyaniso,  zithe tye.</li>
      <li>Ubathumele abantu bakhe inkululeko; Uwumisele ngonaphakade umnqophiso wakhe; Lingcwele, liyoyikeka, igama lakhe.</li>
      <li>Ingqalo yobulumko kukoyika uYehova, Banengqiqo elungileyo bonke abenza ngako; Indumiso yakhe ihlala imi.</li>

  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Haleluya! Hayi, uyolo lomntu omoyikayo uYehova,  Oyinoneleleyo kunene imithetho yakhe!</li>

      <li>Bubuncwane nobutyebi endlwini yakhe; Ubulungisa bakhe buhlala bumi.</li>
      <li>Baphunyelwa kukukhanya ebumnyameni abathe tye, Benobabalo,  nemfesane, nobulungisa.</li>
      <li>Unoyolo umntu obabalayo, aboleke; Uya kuyimisa intetho yakhe ematyaleni.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba akayi kushukunyiswa naphakade; Uya kuba lilungisa elikhunjulwa ngonaphakade.</li>
      <li>Akoyikiswa ziindaba ezimbi; Iqinisekile intliziyo yakhe,  ikholose ngoYehova.</li>
      <li>Izimasekile intliziyo yakhe, akoyiki; Uya kuda ababonele ababandezeli bakhe.</li>
      <li>Uyahlakaza, upha amahlwempu; Ubulungisa bakhe buhlala bumi, Uphondo lwakhe luphakamile, lunozuko.</li>
      <li>Ongendawo yena uya kukubona, aqumbe, Atshixize amazinyo,  anyibilike; Umnqweno wongendawo uyadaka.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Haleluya! Dumisani, bakhonzi bakaYehova, Dumisani igama likaYehova.</li>

  <li>

      <li>Ekuphumeni kukaSirayeli eYiputa, Kwendlu kaYakobi ebantwini abantetho ingaziwayo,</li>

      <li>Iintaba zadloba njengeenkunzi zeegusha; Iinduli,  njengamatakane omhlambi.</li>

      <li>Ngumgcini wabazizidenge uYehova; Ndandiswele,  wandisindisa.</li>

      <li>Ndingumphambukeli ehlabathini, Musa ukuyisithelisa kum imithetho yakho.</li>

      <li>Ubakhalimele abakhukhumali, Abaqalekiswa abo,  balahlekeneyo nemithetho yakho.</li>
