      <li>Izingqiniso zakho ziziyoliso zam noko, Zingamaphakathi am.</li>
      <li>Umphefumlo wam unamathele eluthulini: Ndiphilise ngokwelizwi lakho.</li>
      <li>Ndizicacisile iindlela zam, wandiphendula; Ndifundise imimisela yakho.</li>
      <li>Ndiqondise iindlela zeziyalezo zakho, Ndicamngce ngemisebenzi yakho ebalulekileyo.</li>
      <li>Umphefumlo wam uvuza iinyembezi sisingqala, Ndimise ngokwelizwi lakho.</li>
      <li>Indlela yobuxoki yisuse kum; Ndibabale umyalelo wakho.</li>
      <li>Ndiyinyule indlela yokuthembeka; Amasiko akho ndijolise kuwo.</li>
      <li>Ndinamathele ezingqinisweni zakho; Musa ukundidanisa,  Yehova.</li>
      <li>Ndigidima ngendlela yemithetho yakho, Ngokuba uyenze banzi intliziyo yam.</li>
      <li>Ndiyalele, Yehova, indlela yemimiselo yakho, Ndiyibambe kuphele.</li>
      <li>Ndiqondise, ndibambe umyalelo wakho, Ndiwugcine ngentliziyo yonke.</li>
      <li>Ndinyathelise endleleni yemithetho yakho, Ngokuba ndiyithandile.</li>
      <li>Intliziyo yam yithobele ezingqinisweni zakho,  Ungayithobeli ekubaweni.</li>
      <li>Dlulisa amehlo am angakhangeli inkohlakalo, Ndiphilise ngeendlela zakho.</li>
      <li>Zalisa kumkhonzi wakho intetho yakho, Eyokuba bakoyike.</li>
      <li>Yidlulise ingcikivo yam endinxunguphala yiyo, Ngokuba amasiko akho alungile.</li>
      <li>Nanku ndilangazelela iziyalezo zakho, Ndiphilise ngobulungisa bakho.</li>
      <li>Mazize kum iinceba zakho, Yehova, Nosindiso lwakho ngokwentetho yakho;</li>
      <li>Ndimphendule ngelizwi ondingcikivayo, Ngokuba ndikholose ngelizwi lakho.</li>
      <li>Musa ukuda ulihluthe emlonyeni wam ilizwi lenyaniso,  Ngokuba ndilindele izigwebo zakho;</li>
      <li>Ndowugcina umyalelo wakho ngamaxesha onke, Ngonaphakade kanaphakade;</li>
      <li>Ndihamba-hambe endaweni ebanzi, Ngokuba ndifuna iziyalezo zakho.</li>
      <li>Ndothetha ngezingqiniso zakho phambi kokumkani, Ndingabi nakudana.</li>
      <li>Ndoziyolisa ngemithetho yakho Endiyithandayo;</li>
      <li>Ndiziphakamise izandla zam emithethweni yakho endiyithandayo, Ndicamngce ngemimiselo yakho.</li>
      <li>Khumbula ilizwi lakho kumkhonzi wakho, Ngenxa enokuba undithembise lona.</li>
      <li>Yiyo le intuthuzelo yam ekucinezelekeni kwam, Yokuba intetho yakho indiphilisile.</li>
      <li>Abakhukhumali bada bandigxeka kakhulu; Kanti andithi gu bucala emyalelweni wakho.</li>
      <li>Ndawakhumbula amasiko akho kususela kwanaphakade, Yehova,  Ndathuthuzeleka.</li>
      <li>Ndingenwe ngumsindo oshushu, Ndisenziwa ngabangendawo abalahla umyalelo wakho.</li>
      <li>Iziingoma kum imimiselo yakho, Endlwini yokuphambukela kwam.</li>
      <li>Ndilikhumbule ebusuku igama lakho, Yehova, Ndawugcina umyalelo wakho.</li>
      <li>Ndinikwe oku, Ukuba ndibambe iziyalezo zakho.</li>
      <li>Isabelo sam, Yehova, ndithi, Sesokuba ndigcine amazwi akho.</li>
      <li>Ndiya kubongoza ngentliziyo yonke, Ndibabale ngokwentetho yakho.</li>
      <li>Ndazicingela iindlela zam, Ndazibuyisela iinyawo zam ezingqinisweni zakho.</li>
      <li>Ndikhawulezile andazila-zila Ukugcina imithetho yakho.</li>
      <li>Izintya zabangendawo zindithandele, Andiwulibele umyalelo wakhe noko.</li>
      <li>Ndivuka phakathi kobusuku, ndibulele kuwe, Ngenxa yezigwebo zobulungisa bakho.</li>
      <li>Ndilidlelane labo bonke abakoyikayo, Nelabazigcinayo iziyalezo zakho.</li>
      <li>Inceba yakho, Yehova, izalise ihlabathi; Ndifundise imimiselo yakho.</li>
      <li>Umenzele okulungileyo umkhonzi wakho, Yehova, ngokwelizwi lakho.</li>
      <li>Ndifundise, ndibe nemvo nokwazi okulungileyo, Ngokuba ndikholwa yimithetho yakho.</li>
      <li>Ndingekacinezelwa, ndaye ndilahleka; Kungoku ndiyigcinile intetho yakho.</li>
      <li>Ulungile wena, ulungisa; Ndifundise imimiselo yakho.</li>
      <li>Abakhukhumali bathungele ubuxoki ngam; Mna ndizibamba ngentliziyo yonke iziyalezo zakho.</li>
      <li>Ithe fithi kukutyeba intliziyo yabo; Ke mna ndiziyolisa ngomyalelo wakho.</li>
      <li>Kundilungele okokuba ndacinezelwayo, Ukuze ndiyifunde imimiselo yakho.</li>
      <li>Ulungile kum umyalelo womlomo wakho, Ngaphezu kwamawaka egolide nesilivere.</li>
      <li>Izandla zakho zindenzile, zandilungisa; Ndiqondise,  ndifunde imithetho yakho.</li>
      <li>Abakoyikayo bondibona, bavuye, Ngokuba ndilindele elizwini lakho.</li>
      <li>Ndiyazi, Yehova, ukuba zinobulungisa izigwebo zakho;  Undicinezele, phofu uthembekile.</li>
      <li>Ngamana inceba yakho yaba yeyokundithuthuzela,  Njengokwentetho yakho kumkhonzi wakho.</li>
      <li>Mazize kum iimfesane zakho, ndiphile, Ngokuba umyalelo wakho undiyolisa.</li>
      <li>Mabadane abakhukhumali, ngokuba bendigobele phantsi ngobuxoki, Mna ndicamngca ngeziyalezo zakho.</li>
      <li>Mabandibuyele abakoyikayo, Nabazaziyo izingqiniso zakho.</li>
      <li>Mayigqibelele intliziyo yam emimiselweni yakho, Ukuze ndingadani.</li>
      <li>Umphefumlo wam uyaphela kukululangazelela usindiso lwakho, Ndilindele elizwini lakho.</li>
      <li>Amehlo am ayaphela kukulangazelela intetho yakho,  Ndisithi, Uya kundithuthuzela nini na?</li>
      <li>Noko ndithe ndaba njengentsuba emsini; Andiyilibali imimiselo yakho.</li>
      <li>Zingaphi na iintsuku zomkhonzi wakho? Uya kuda ubagwebe nini na abandisukelayo?</li>
      <li>Abakhukhumali bandimbele izihogo, Abangenamyalelo wakho.</li>
      <li>Yonke imithetho yakho ithembekile: Bandisukela ngobuxoki;  ndincede.</li>
      <li>Baphantse ukundigqibela emhlabeni, Ke mna andizilahli iziyalezo zakho.</li>
      <li>Ndiphilise ngokwenceba yakho, Ndizigcine izingqiniso zomlomo wakho.</li>
      <li>Lingunaphakade, Yehova, Limi emazulwini ilizwi lakho.</li>
      <li>Ukuthembeka kwakho kukwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana;  Ulizinzisile ihlabathi, lema.</li>
      <li>Ezo zinto zimele izigwebo zakho nanamhla, Ngokuba iinto zonke zingabakhonzi bakho.</li>
      <li>Koko umyalelo wakho wandiyolisayo, Ndinge ndaphelayo ekucinezelekeni kwam.</li>
      <li>Andiyi kuzilibala naphakade iziyalezo zakho, Ngokuba undiphilisile ngazo.</li>
      <li>Ndingowakho mna, ndisindise, Kuba ndicamanga ngeziyalezo zakho.</li>
      <li>Abangendawo bandilindile ukuze banditshabalalise; Mna ndigqale izingqiniso zakho.</li>
      <li>Yonke inzaliseko ndiyibonile apho iphela khona; Ke wona umthetho wakho ngumphangalala omkhulu.</li>
      <li>Hayi, ukuwuthanda kwam umyalelo wakho! Imini le yonke ndiyacamngca ngawo.</li>
      <li>Indifundisa ubulumko ngaphezu kweentshaba zam imithetho yakho, Ngokuba yeyam ngonaphakade.</li>
      <li>Ndinokuqiqa ngaphezu kwabafundisi bam bonke, Ngokuba ngezingqiniso zakho ndiyacamngca.</li>
      <li>Ndinokuqonda ngaphezu kwamadoda amakhulu, Ngokuba ndizibamba iziyalezo zakho.</li>
      <li>Ndizinqandile iinyawo zam kwiindlela zonke ezimbi, Ukuze ndiligcine ilizwi lakho.</li>
      <li>Andisuki emasikweni akho, Ngokuba undiyalile wena.</li>
      <li>Hayi, ukuba mnandi kwentetho yakho ekhuhlangubeni lam!  Igqithe nobusi emlonyeni wam.</li>
      <li>Ngeziyalezo zakho ndinokuqonda, Ngenxa yoko ndiwuthiyile wonke umendo wobuxoki.</li>
      <li>Lisisibane seenyawo zam ilizwi lakho, Likukukhanya emendweni wam.</li>
      <li>Ndikufungele, ndikumisile, Ukuzigcina izigwebo zobulungisa bakho.</li>
      <li>Ndide ndacinezeleka kakhulu; Yehova, ndiphilise ngokwelizwi lakho.</li>
      <li>Ngamana wakholeka kuwe, Yehova, umbingelelo wesisa womlomo wam; Ndifundise amasiko akho.</li>
      <li>Umphefumlo wam uhlala usesandleni sam, Ndingawulibali umyalelo wakho.</li>
      <li>Abangendawo bandenzele umgibe, Andiphambukanga eziyalezweni zakho.</li>
      <li>Ndizidle ilifa izingqiniso zakho ngonaphakade, Ngokuba ziyimihlali yentliziyo yam;</li>
      <li>Intliziyo yam ndiyithobele ekwenzeni imimiselo yakho Ngonaphakade, kuphele.</li>
      <li>Abambaxa ndiyabathiya, Wona umyalelo wakho ndiyawuthanda.</li>
      <li>Isithe lam nengweletshetshe yam nguwe, Ndilindele elizwini lakho.</li>
      <li>Sukani kum, nina benzi beento ezimbi, Ndibambe imithetho yoThixo wam.</li>
      <li>Ndizimase ngokwelizwi lakho, ndiphile, Ungandidanisi ekulindeni kwam.</li>
      <li>Ndixhase ndisinde, Ndihlale ndibheke emimiselweni yakho.</li>
      <li>Ubacukucezile bonke abalahlekana nemimiselo yakho,  Ngokuba inkohliso yabo ibubuxoki.</li>
      <li>Wena ususa bonke abangendawo behlabathi njengentlenga,  Ngoko ndiyazithanda izingqiniso zakho.</li>
      <li>Inyama yam isuka ihambe kukunkwantyiswa nguwe, Ndizoyike izigwebo zakho.</li>
      <li>Ndenza ngesiko nangobulungisa, Ungandinikeli kwabandicudisayo.</li>
      <li>Mmele umkhonzi wakho, kulunge; Mabangandicudisi abakhukhumali.</li>
      <li>Amehlo am ayaphela kukululangazelela usindiso lwakho,  Nentetho yobulungisa bakho.</li>
      <li>Umkhonzi wakho menzele ngokwenceba yakho Undifundise imimiselo yakho.</li>
      <li>Ndingumkhonzi wakho, ndiqondise, Ndizazi izingqiniso zakho.</li>
      <li>Lilixa lokuba uYehova enze, Kuba bawaphule umyalelo wakho.</li>
      <li>Ngenxa yoko ndiyithanda imithetho yakho Ngaphezu kwegolide, nakwengcwengiweyo.</li>
      <li>Ngenxa yoko ndithi, Zonke iziyalezo zakho zithe tye ngezinto zonke; Wonke umendo wobuxoki ndiwuthiyile.</li>
      <li>Ziyimisebenzi ebalulekileyo izingqiniso zakho, Ngenxa yoko uzibambile umphefumlo wam.</li>
      <li>Ukutyhila kwamazwi akho kuyakhanyisa, Kuqondisa abazizidenge.</li>
      <li>Ndakhamisa umlomo wam, ndakhefuza, Ngokuba ndiyilangazelela imithetho yakho.</li>
      <li>Ndibheke, undibabale, Ngokwesiko lakho kubathandi begama lakho.</li>
      <li>Qinisa ukunyathela kwam ngentetho yakho, Mabungabi nagunya kum ubutshinga, nabuphi na.</li>
      <li>Ndikhulule ekucudiseni komntu, Ndizigcine iziyalezo zakho.</li>
      <li>Khanyisa ubuso bakho kumkhonzi wakho, Undifundise imimiselo yakho.</li>
      <li>Ahla imijelo yamanzi amehlo am, Ngenxa yokuba bengawugcini umyalelo wakho.</li>
      <li>Ulilungisa wena, Yehova, Zithe tye izigwebo zakho.</li>
      <li>Uzimisile izingqiniso zakho, zanobulungisa, Zaba nokuthembeka kakhulu.</li>
      <li>Ikhwele lam lindibhangisile, Ngokuba abandibandezelayo bewalibele amazwi akho.</li>
      <li>Ilizwi lakho linyibilikisiwe njengegolide kunene,  Umkhonzi wakho uyalithanda.</li>
      <li>Ndimncinane, ndideliwe, Noko andizilibali iziyalezo zakho.</li>
      <li>Ubulungisa bakho bubulungisa obungunaphakade, Umyalelo wakho uyinyaniso.</li>
      <li>Imbandezelo nengcutheko indifumene, Imithetho yakho iyandiyolisa.</li>
      <li>Zinobulungisa ngonaphakade izingqiniso zakho,  Ndiqondise, ndiphile.</li>
      <li>Ndikhala ngentliziyo yonke, ndiphendule; Yehova,  imimiselo yakho ndiya kuyibamba.</li>
      <li>Ndikhala kuwe, ndisindise, Ndigcine izingqiniso zakho.</li>
      <li>Ndakuphangela ukusa, ndazibika, Ndalindela emazwini akho.</li>
      <li>Amehlo am aphengela imilindo yasebusuku, Ukuze ndicamngce ngentetho yakho.</li>
      <li>Live ilizwi lam ngokwenceba yakho, Yehova, ndiphilise ngokwamasiko akho.</li>
      <li>Bayasondela abaphuthuma amanyala, Banyawuka emyalelweni wakho;</li>
      <li>Usondele wena, Yehova, Yonke imithetho yakho iyinyaniso.</li>
      <li>Kudala ndisazi ngokwezingqiniso zakho, Ukuba uzisekile ngonaphakade.</li>
      <li>Khangela ukucinezeleka kwam, undihlangule, Ngokuba ndingawulibali umyalelo wakho.</li>
      <li>Bambana nobambene nam, undikhulule, Ndiphilise ngokwelizwi lakho.</li>
      <li>Lunyawukile kwabangendawo usindiso, Ngokuba abayifuni imimiselo yakho.</li>
      <li>Iimfesane zakho zininzi, Yehova; Ndiphilise ngokwamasiko akho.</li>
      <li>Baninzi abandisukelayo nabandibandezelayo; Andithi gu bucala ezingqinisweni zakho.</li>
      <li>Ndababona abatshinizi, ndakruquka, Abo bangayigciniyo intetho yakho.</li>
      <li>Bona ukuthanda kwam iziyalezo zakho, Yehova, ndiphilise ngokwenceba yakho.</li>
      <li>Isimbuku selizwi lakho siyinyaniso iphela,  Zingunaphakade zonke izigwebo zobulungisa bakho.</li>
      <li>Abathetheli bandisukela ngelize, Intliziyo yam iyankwantyiswa ngamazwi akho.</li>
      <li>Ndinemihlali ngentetho yakho, Njengofumene ixhoba elininzi.</li>
      <li>Ndikuthiyile ukuxoka, lisikizi kum; Ndiyawuthanda umyalelo wakho.</li>
      <li>Ndikudumisa kasixhenxe ngemini, Ngenxa yezigwebo zobulungisa bakho.</li>
      <li>Banoxolo olukhulu abawuthandayo umyalelo wakho; Akukho sikhubekiso kubo.</li>
      <li>Ndikhangela usindiso lwakho, Yehova; Ndenza imithetho yakho.</li>
      <li>Umphefumlo wam uyazigcina izingqiniso zakho, Ndizithanda kunene.</li>
      <li>Ndiyazigcina iziyalezo zakho nezingqiniso zakho, Ngokuba zonke iindlela zam ziphambi kwakho.</li>
      <li>Makusondele phambi kwakho ukuhlahlamba kwam; Yehova,  ndiqondise ngokwelizwi lakho.</li>
      <li>Masifike isikhungo sam phambi kwakho; Ndihlangule ngokwentetho yakho.</li>
      <li>Umlomo wam mawumpompoze indumiso, Kuba undifundisile imimiselo yakho.</li>
      <li>Ulwimi lwam luya kuyiphendula intetho yakho, Ngokuba yonke imithetho yakho inobulungisa.</li>
      <li>Isandla sakho masibe sesokundinceda, Ngokuba ndizinyulele iziyalezo zakho.</li>
      <li>Ndilangazelela usindiso lwakho, Yehova; Umyalelo wakho uyandiyolisa.</li>
      <li>Mawuphile umphefumlo wam, ukudumise, Andincede amasiko akho.</li>
      <li>Ndiya ndimka njengemvu elahlekileyo; mfune umkhonzi wakho, Ngokuba andiyilibali imithetho yakho.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ingoma yezinyuko. Engxingongweni yam ndakhala kuYehova,  Wandiphendula.</li>
      <li>Ndathi, Wuhlangule, Yehova, umphefumlo wam emlonyeni oxokayo, Elulwimini olunenkohliso.</li>
      <li>Makakunike ntoni na, akongeze ntoni na, Lulwimindini lunenkohliso?</li>
      <li>Iintolo zegorha ezitsolo, Kunye namalahle avuthayo onwele.</li>
      <li>Athi ke mna! Kuba ndingumphambukeli kwaMesheki, Ndihleli ngasezintenteni zakwaKedare.</li>
      <li>Umphefumlo wam kade uhleli Nabaluthiyileyo uxolo.</li>
      <li>Mna ndingowoxolo; Ke ndithi ndakuthetha, bona babe yimfazwe.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ingoma yezinyuko. Ndiwaphakamisele ezintabeni na amehlo am? Luya kuvela phi na uncedo lwam?</li>
      <li>Uncedo lwam luvela kuYehova, UMenzi wezulu nehlabathi.</li>
      <li>Akayi kukha alunikele unyawo lwakho ekutyibilikeni; Akayi kukha ozele umgcini wakho.</li>
      <li>Uyabona, akozeli, akalali, UMgcini kaSirayeli.</li>
      <li>NguYehova umgcini wakho, NguYehova umthunzi wakho ekunene kwakho.</li>
      <li>Emini ilanga aliyi kukwenzakalisa, Nenyanga ebusuku.</li>
      <li>UYehova uya kukugcina ebubini bonke, Uya kuwugcina umphefumlo wakho.</li>
      <li>UYehova uya kukugcina ukuphuma kwakho nokungena kwakho,  Kususela ngoku kude kuse ephakadeni.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ingoma yezinyuko. KaDavide. Ndavuya bakuthi kum, Masiye endlwini kaYehova.</li>
      <li>Iinyawo zethu zifike zema Emasangweni akho, Yerusalem;</li>
      <li>Yerusalem, wena wakhiweyo Ngokomzi ohlangeneyo wamnye;</li>
      <li>Apho zinyuka ziye khona izizwe, Izizwe zikaYehova;  Ibubungqina ke loo nto kwaSirayeli, Ukuba kubulelwe kwigama likaYehova.</li>
      <li>Kuba khona apho kumiswe iitrone zokugweba, Iitrone zendlu kaDavide.</li>
      <li>Celelani iYerusalem uxolo; Mababe nokuchulumacha abakuthandayo,</li>
      <li>Malube luxolo eludongeni lwakho olurhaqileyo,  Nokuchulumacha ezingxandeni zakho ezinde.</li>
      <li>Ngenxa yabazalwana bam nowethu, Makhe ndithethe uxolo ngawe.</li>
      <li>Ngenxa yendlu kaYehova, uThixo wethu, Ndiya kufuna okukulungeleyo.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ingoma yezinyuko. Ulohlala emazulwini, Ndiwaphakamisela kuwe amehlo am.</li>
      <li>Uyabona, njengokuba amehlo abakhonzi Emi kwisandla seenkosi zabo; Njengokuba amehlo omkhonzazana Emi kwisandla senkosikazi yakhe: Ngokunjalo amehlo ethu akuYehova, uThixo wethu, Ade asibabale.</li>
      <li>Sibabale, Yehova, sibabale, Ngokuba sanele kakhulu kukudelwa.</li>
      <li>Umphefumlo wethu wanele kakhulu Kukugculela kwabangakhathalele bani, Nokudela kwabanekratshi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ingoma yezinyuko. KaDavide. Koko uYehova ebengakuthi,  Makatsho uSirayeli,</li>
      <li>Koko uYehova ebengakuthi Ekusukeleni kwabantu phezulu kuthi,</li>
      <li>Bange beba basiginya sihleli, Ekuvutheni komsindo wabo kuthi;</li>
      <li>Ange esintywilisele amanzi, Wadlula phezu komphefumlo wethu umsinga;</li>
      <li>Ange edlule phezu komphefumlo wethu Amanzi akhukumeleyo.</li>
      <li>Ungowokubongwa uYehova, Ongasinikelanga emazinyweni abo,  ukuba siqwengwe.</li>
      <li>Umphefumlo wethu usindile, njengentaka emgibeni wababambisi; Umgibe uqhawukile, sasinda ke thina.</li>
      <li>Uncedo lwethu lusegameni likaYehova, UMenzi wezulu nehlabathi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ingoma yezinyuko. Abo bakholosa ngoYehova banjengentaba yaseZiyon: Ayishukumi, ihleli ngonaphakade.</li>
      <li>IYerusalem ijikelezwe ziintaba; Ke uYehova ubajikelezile naye abantu bakhe, Kususela ngoku kude kuse ephakadeni.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba ayiyi kuhlala intonga yokungendawo elifeni lamalungisa, Ukuze amalungisa angazisi ebugqwetheni izandla zawo.</li>
      <li>Yehova, yenza okulungileyo kwabalungileyo, Kwabathe tye ezintliziyweni zabo.</li>
      <li>Ke bona abathi gu bucala ngeendlela zabo ezimagoso-goso,  UYehova makabemkise, kunye nabasebenzi bobutshinga. Malube luxolo kuSirayeli.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ingoma yezinyuko. Ekubabuyiseni kukaYehova ababuyayo baseZiyon, Saba njengabaphuphayo;</li>
      <li>Waza wazala kukuhleka umlomo wethu, Lwazala kukumemelela ulwimi lwethu. Baza bathi phakathi kweentlanga, UYehova ubenzele izinto ezinkulu aba.</li>
      <li>UYehova usenzele izinto ezinkulu, Saba ngabavuyayo.</li>
      <li>Buyisa, Yehova, abathinjiweyo bakuthi, Njengemilambo yamanzi yelasezantsi.</li>
      <li>Abahlwayelayo beneenyembezi Baya kuvuna benokumemelela.</li>
      <li>Ohamba ahambe elila, Ephethe intlwayelelo, Uyabuya eze ememelela, Ethwele izithungu zakhe.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ingoma yezinyuko. KaSolomon. Ukuba akayakhi uYehova indlu, Bafumana besaphuka yiyo abakhi bayo. Ukuba umzi akawugcini uYehova, Ufumana ephaphama owugcinayo.</li>
      <li>Nifumana nivuka kusasa, Nihlale nisebenza kude kube sebusuku, Nikudla ukudla kokubulaleka; Uyipha intanda yakhe,  ilele ubuthongo.</li>
      <li>Uyabona, ilifa likaYehova ngoonyana, Umvuzo sisiqhamo sesizalo.</li>
      <li>Njengeentolo esandleni segorha, Banjalo oonyana bobutsha.</li>
      <li>Hayi, uyolo lomfo ozalise umphongolo wakhe ngabo! Abayi kudana, Xa bathetha neentshaba esangweni.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ingoma yezinyuko. Hayi, uyolo lwabantu bonke abamoyikayo uYehova, Abahamba ngeendlela zakhe!</li>
      <li>Ukuxelenga kwezandla zakho inene uya kukudla, Uya kuba noyolo wena, kulunge kuwe.</li>
      <li>Umkakho woba njengomdiliya oqhamayo Endlwini yakho ngaphakathi; Oonyana bakho babe njengezithole zomnquma Ngeenxa zonke esithebeni sakho.</li>
      <li>Yabona, unjalo ukusikelelwa umfo Omoyikayo uYehova.</li>
      <li>Makakusikelele uYehova eZiyon. Uyibone iYerusalem inenyhweba Yonke imihla yobomi bakho;</li>
      <li>Ubone abantwana babantwana bakho. Malube luxolo kuSirayeli.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ingoma yezinyuko. Kukaninzi bendibandezela kwasebuncinaneni bam, Makatsho uSirayeli;</li>
      <li>Kukaninzi bendibandezela kwasebuncinaneni bam: Ababanga nakundithini noko.</li>
      <li>Abalimi balima emhlana kum, Bayolula indima yabo.</li>
      <li>UYehova ulilungisa, Uzinqumle izintya zabangendawo.</li>
      <li>Mabadane babuye umva Bonke abayithiyayo iZiyon.</li>
      <li>Mababe njengengca ephuma phezu kwezindlu, Eyomayo ingekahlumi,</li>
      <li>Engekasizalisi nesandla sakhe umvuni, Engekalizalisi nesondo lengubo yakhe umbophi wezithungu;</li>
      <li>Bengekathi nabadlulayo, Intsikelelo kaYehova mayibe kuni;  Siyanisikelela egameni likaYehova.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ingoma yezinyuko. Ezinzulwini ndinqula wena, Yehova,</li>
      <li>Nkosi, yiva ilizwi lam. Iindlebe zakho mazilibazele Ilizwi lokutarhuzisa kwam.</li>
      <li>Ukuba uthe wabunqala ubugwenxa, Yehova, Ngubani na ongaba nokuma, Nkosi?</li>
      <li>Ngokuba kunawe ukuxolela, Ukuze woyikwe.</li>
      <li>Ndithembele kuYehova, uthembile umphefumlo wam; Ndilinde ilizwi lakhe.</li>
      <li>Umphefumlo wam ulindele eNkosini Ngaphezu kwabalinde ukusa, Ewe, abalinde ukusa.</li>
      <li>Lindela kuYehova, Sirayeli, Ngokuba inceba ikuYehova;  Ikuye inkululeko eninzi.</li>
      <li>Yena ke wowakhulula amaSirayeli Ebugwenxeni bawo bonke.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ingoma yezinyuko; kaDavide. Yehova, intliziyo yam ayiphakamile, amehlo am akaqwayingile; Andihambi ezintweni ezinkulu, Eziyimisebenzi ebalulekileyo kum.</li>
      <li>Inene, ndiwuzolise ndawuthozamisa umphefumlo wam;  Unjengomntwana olunyulweyo, ehleli kunina; Unjengomntwana olunyulweyo umphefumlo wam kum.</li>
      <li>Wena Sirayeli, lindela kuYehova Kususela ngoku kude kuse ephakadeni.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ingoma yezinyuko. Yehova, mkhumbulele uDavide Ukucinezeleka kwakhe konke;</li>
      <li>Yena wamfungelayo uYehova, Wabhambathisa kwimbalasane enguThixo kaYakobi,</li>
      <li>Esithi, Andiyi kungena ententeni eyindlu yam, Andiyi kunyuka ndiye esililini, emandlalweni wam;</li>
      <li>Andiyi kuwanika amehlo am ubuthongo, Neenkophe zam ukozela:</li>
      <li>Ndide ndimfumanele indawo uYehova, Ndiyifumanele umnquba imbalasane kaYakobi.</li>
      <li>Khangela, sawuva e-Efrata, Sawufumana ezintilini zaseKiriyati-yeharim.</li>
      <li>Masingene emnqubeni wakhe, Siqubude esihlalweni seenyawo zakhe.</li>
      <li>Khawusuk ume, Yehova, uze ekuphumleni kwakho, Wena netyeya yamandla akho.</li>
      <li>Ababingeleli bakho mabambathe ubulungisa, Bamemelele abakho benceba.</li>
      <li>Ngenxa kaDavide umkhonzi wakho, Musa ukubutyhala ubuso bomthanjiswa wakho.</li>
      <li>UYehova wamfungela uDavide; Inyaniso, akayi kubuya kuloo nto, Esithi, Esiqhameni sezibilini zakho Ndimisa oya kuba setroneni yakho.</li>
      <li>Ukuba bathe oonyana bakho bawugcina umnqophiso wam,  Nesingqiniso sam endibafundisayo: Oonyana babo bothi nabo bahlale Etroneni yakho nanini.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba uYehova uyinyule iZiyon, Uyinqwenele ukuba ibe likhaya lakhe;</li>
      <li>Esithi, Nantsi indawo yam yokuphumla kwam nanini; Ndiya kuhlala apha, ngokuba oko ndikunqwenele.</li>
      <li>Umphako wayo ndiya kuwusikelela kunene; Amahlwempu ayo ndiya kuwahluthisa ngesonka,</li>
      <li>Ndibambathise ngosindiso ababingeleli bayo, Abenceba bayo bamemelele bememelela.</li>
      <li>Apho ndiya kumhlumisela uphondo uDavide, Ndiya kumlungisela isibane umthanjiswa wam.</li>
      <li>Iintshaba zakhe ndiya kuzambathisa udano; Ke phezu kwakhe yena siya kutyatyamba isithsaba sakhe.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ingoma yezinyuko; kaDavide. Yabonani, ukuba kuhle, ukuba mnandi, Ukuthi abazalwana bahlale bemxhelo mnye!</li>
      <li>Kunjengeoli elungileyo entloko, Isihla ezindevini,  Ezindevini zika-Aron, Isihla iye emqukumbelweni weengubo zakhe.</li>
      <li>Kunjengombethe waseHermon, Ohla phezu kweentaba zaseZiyon;  Ngokuba uYehova wayimisela khona apho intsikelelo, Ubomi, kude kuse ephakadeni.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Ingoma yezinyuko. Yabonani, mbongeni uYehova, nonke bakhonzi bakaYehova, Nimiyo endlwini kaYehova ebusuku.</li>
      <li>Phakamiselani engcweleni izandla zenu, Nimbonge uYehova.</li>
      <li>Makakusikelele eZiyon uYehova, UMenzi wezulu nehlabathi.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Haleluya. Dumisani igama likaYehova; Dumisani, nina bakhonzi bakaYehova,</li>
      <li>Nimiyo endlwini kaYehova, Ezintendelezweni zendlu yoThixo wethu.</li>
      <li>Dumisani uYehova, ngokuba elungile uYehova; Libetheleni uhadi igama lakhe, ngokuba kumnandi.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba uYehova unyule uYakobi ukuba abe ngowakhe, Wanyula uSirayeli ukuba abe yinqobo kuye.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba ndiyazi mna ukuba mkhulu uYehova, INkosi yethu ingaphezu koothixo bonke.</li>
      <li>Konke akuthandileyo uYehova uya kwenza, Ezulwini nasemhlabeni, Ezilwandle nasemanzini onke enzonzobila.</li>
      <li>Ulonyusa amafu eziphelweni zehlabathi, Imvula wayenzela imibane; Ulorhola umoya koovimba bakhe.</li>
      <li>Owawabulalayo amazibulo aseYiputa, Ethabathele ebantwini wesa ezinkomeni;</li>
      <li>Wathumela imiqondiso nezimanga Phakathi kwakho, Yiputa,  KuFaro nakubakhonzi bakhe bonke;</li>
      <li>Owabulala iintlanga ezinkulu, Wabulala ookumkani abanamandla;</li>
      <li>OoSihon, ukumkani wama-Amori, No-Ogi, ukumkani waseBhashan, Nezikumkani zonke zakwaKanan;</li>
      <li>Walinikela ilizwe labo lalilifa, Lalilifa kumaSirayeli,  abantu bakhe,</li>
      <li>Yehova, igama lakho lingunaphakade, Inkumbuzo yakho,  Yehova, ikwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba uYehova uya kugweba phakathi kwabantu bakhe,  Azohlwaye ngenxa yabakhonzi bakhe.</li>
      <li>Izithixo zeentlanga yisilivere negolide, Umsebenzi wezandla zabantu.</li>
      <li>Zinomlomo nje, azithethi; Zinamehlo nje, aziboni;</li>
      <li>Zineendlebe nje, aziva; Akukho nento engumoya emlonyeni wazo.</li>
      <li>Baya kuba njengazo abenzi bazo, Bonke abasukuba bekholose ngazo.</li>
      <li>Nina ndlu kaSirayeli, bongani uYehova; Nani ndlu ka-Aron,  bongani uYehova.</li>
      <li>Nina ndlu kaLevi, bongani uYehova; Nani boyika uYehova,  bongani uYehova.</li>
      <li>Ngowokubongwa uYehova eZiyon, Ulohlala eYerusalem.  Haleluya!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Bulelani kuYehova, ngokuba elungile: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</li>
      <li>Bulelani kuThixo woothixo: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</li>
      <li>Bulelani kuNkosi kankosi: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</li>
      <li>KuloMenzi wemisebenzi ebalulekileyo emikhulu yedwa:  Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</li>
      <li>KuloMenzi wezulu ngengqondo: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</li>
      <li>KuloMtwabululi wehlabathi phezu kwamanzi: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</li>
      <li>KuloMenzi wezikhanyiso ezikhulu: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe;</li>
      <li>Ilanga lilawule emini: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe;</li>
      <li>Inyanga neenkwenkwezi zilawule ebusuku: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</li>
      <li>Kulowabulala amaYiputa kumazibulo awo: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</li>
      <li>Wawakhupha amaSirayeli phakathi kwawo: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</li>
      <li>Ngesandla esithe nkqi, nangengalo eyolukileyo: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</li>
      <li>KuloMgabuli woLwandle oluBomvu, lwagabuka: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</li>
      <li>Wawaweza amaSirayeli esazulwini salo: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</li>
      <li>Wamvuthululela uFaro nempi yakhe eLwandle oluBomvu:  Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</li>
      <li>Kulohambisa abantu bakhe entlango: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</li>
      <li>Kulowaxabela ookumkani abakhulu: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</li>
      <li>Wabulala ookumkani abaziingangamsha: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe;</li>
      <li>USihon, ukumkani wama-Amori: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe;</li>
      <li>No-Ogi, ukumkani waseBhashan: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</li>
      <li>Walinikela ilizwe labo laba lilifa: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe,</li>
      <li>Laba lilifa kuSirayeli umkhonzi wakhe: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</li>
      <li>Owasikhumbulayo ebuphantsini bethu: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</li>
      <li>Wasihlangula kwabasibandezelayo: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</li>
      <li>Ulonika into yonke ephilileyo ukudla: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</li>
      <li>Bulelani kuThixo wamazulu: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>NgaseMilanjeni yaseBhabheli Sahlala phantsi khona, salila,  Sakuyikhumbula iZiyon.</li>
      <li>Emingculubeni phakathi kwayo Sazixhoma khona iihadi zethu.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba khona apho abathimbi bethu basibiza Izango zengoma; Abathuthumbisi bethu basibiza uvuyo, Besithi,  Sivumeleni ingoma yaseZiyon.</li>
      <li>Singathini na ukuvuma ingoma kaYehova Emhlabeni wolunye uhlanga?</li>
      <li>Ukuba ndithe ndakulibala, Yerusalem, Masinyele isandla sam sokunene.</li>
      <li>Ulwimi lwam malunamathele ekhuhlangubeni lam, Ukuba andithanga ndikukhumbule; Ukuba andithanga ndiyinyuse iYerusalem Ngaphezu kwemivuyo yam yonke.</li>
      <li>Bakhumbule, Yehova, oonyana bakaEdom, Umhla weYerusalem,  Abo bathi, Yidilizeni, yidilizeni Kuse elusekweni lwayo.</li>
      <li>Ntombi inguBhabheli, wena unyashiweyo; Hayi, uyolo lwalowo ukubuyekezayo ukuphatha kwakho Osiphethe ngako!</li>
      <li>Hayi, uyolo lwalowo ubabambayo abahlekeze abantwana bakho Engxondorheni!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>EkaDavide. Ndiya kubulela kuwe ngentliziyo yam yonke;  Phambi koothixo ndiya kukubethela uhadi.</li>
      <li>Ndiya kuqubuda ndibhekise etempileni yakho engcwele,  Ndibulele kwigama lakho, ngenxa yenceba yakho, nangenxa yenyaniso yakho; Kuba ulikhulisile ilizwi lakho ngaphezu kwegama lakho lonke.</li>
      <li>Ngomhla wokubiza kwam wandiphendula, Wandikhaliphisa,  yangamandla emphefumlweni wam.</li>
      <li>Baya kubulela kuwe, Yehova, bonke ookumkani behlabathi,  Bakuweva amazwi omlomo wakho;</li>
      <li>Bavume ngeendlela zikaYehova, Ukuba lukhulu uzuko lukaYehova:</li>
      <li>Ngokuba noko uYehova aphakamileyo, uyambona othobekileyo;  Ke yena oziphakamisayo umazi nakude.</li>
      <li>Ukuba ndithe ndahamba-hamba phakathi kweembandezelo,  uyandiphilisa; Wosolulela emsindweni weentshaba zam isandla sakho, Sindisindise isandla sakho sokunene.</li>
      <li>UYehova uya kundifezela. Yehova, inceba yakho ingunaphakade, Izenzo zezandla zakho musa ukuziyekela.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli; ekaDavide. Umhobe. Yehova, undigocagocile,  wandazi.</li>
      <li>Wena uyakwazi ukuhlala kwam nokusuka kwam; Uyaziqonda izicamango zam nakude.</li>
      <li>Ukuhamba kwam nokulala kwam, uyakwela; Uqhelene neendlela zam zonke.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba akukho lizwi elulwimini lwam Ongalaziyo ke,  Yehova, kanye.</li>
      <li>Ngasemva nangaphambili undingqingile, Wasibeka phezu kwam isandla sakho.</li>
      <li>Kubalulekile kum oko kwazi, Kuphezulu, kundinqabele.</li>
      <li>Ndingahambela phi na ukumka emoyeni wakho? Ndingabalekela phi na ukumka ebusweni bakho?</li>
      <li>Ukuba ndithe ndenyuka ndaya emazulwini, ulapho wena; Ukuba ndithe ndazandlalela kwelabafileyo, nanko ukho.</li>
      <li>Ukuba ndithe ndaphakamisa amaphiko esifingo, Ndaya ndahlala ekupheleni kolwandle,</li>
      <li>Besingandikhaphayo kwanalapho isandla sakho, Sindibambe isandla sakho sokunene.</li>
      <li>Ukuba ndithe, Mabundisongele ubumnyama bona bodwa,  Nokukhanya kube bubusuku ngeenxa zonke kum:</li>
      <li>Kwanobumnyama obo abungebi bubumnyama kuwe; Ubusuku bungaba mhlophe njengemini, Ubumnyama bungaba njengokukhanya</li>
      <li>Ngokuba wena wazibumba izintso zam, Wandibiyela esizalweni sikama.</li>
      <li>Ndiyabulela kuwe ngenxa enokuba ndenziwe ngokoyikekayo,  ngokubalulekileyo; Zibalulekile izenzo zakho, Umphefumlo wam uyazi kakuhle.</li>
      <li>Ayengagushekile kuwe amathambo am, Mna ndenzelwayo entsithelweni, Ndalukwa ndayimfakamfele ezinzulwini zomhlaba.</li>
      <li>Amehlo akho andibona ndiseyimbumba, Zazibhalwe encwadini yakho iimini zonke ziphela; Ziyiliwe ngenxa engaphambili,  Kungekabikho ke nanye kuzo.</li>
      <li>Kum ke zinjani na ukunqaba izicamango zakho, Thixo!  Asingangani isimbuku sazo!</li>
      <li>Zingathi, ndizibalile, zibe ninzi ngaphezu kwentlabathi;  Ndakuvuka ndoba ndisenawe.</li>
      <li>Ngamana wambulala ongendawo, Thixo! Nina madoda amagazi,  sukani kum.</li>
      <li>Abo bakukhankanyela amayelenqe, Balibizela inkohlakalo igama lakho abazondi bakho.</li>
      <li>Andinakubathiya na abakuthiyayo, Yehova, Ndikruquke ngabasukela phezulu kuwe?</li>
      <li>Ndibathiya ngentiyo ephelelisileyo, Kum mna baziintshaba.</li>
      <li>Ndigocagoce, Thixo, uyazi intliziyo yam; Ndicikide, uzazi iingcinga-ngcinga zam;</li>
      <li>Ubone ukuba kukho ndlela yobubi na kum, Undikhaphele kwindlela engunaphakade.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide. Ndihlangule, Yehova,  esintwini esinobubi, Ndilondoloze emntwini ogonyamelayo,</li>
      <li>Abacinga okubi entliziyweni. Imihla yonke baxhaya imfazwe.</li>
      <li>Balola ulwimi lwabo njengenyoka; Ubuhlungu berhamba busemlonyeni wabo (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Ndigcine, Yehova, ezandleni zongendawo, Ndilondoloze emntwini ogonyamelayo, Abacinga ukuzikhubekisa iinyawo zam.</li>
      <li>Abanekratshi bandiqhushekele isibatha nezintya, Baneke umnatha ecaleni kwendlela, Bandithiyele ngemigibe.  (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Ndithi kuYehova, UnguThixo wam; Beka indlebe, Yehova,  elizwini lesikhungo sam.</li>
      <li>Yehova, Nkosi yam, nqaba endisindisayo, Uyigqubuthele intloko yam ngemini yeduli.</li>
      <li>Musa ukumnika, Yehova, ongendawo iminqweno yakhe; Musa ukuwuphumelelisa umnkqangiyelo wakhe, Hleze aziphakamise.  (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Yona intloko yabandingqingayo, Ububi bomlomo wabo mabubagubungele.</li>
      <li>Mabathotyelwe amalahle avuthayo; Makabawise emlilweni,  emimbithini, bangabi saphuma.</li>
      <li>Indoda enolwimi mayingazinzi ehlabathini; Indoda enokugonyamela, ububi mabuyizingele ngembembetshane.</li>
      <li>Ndiyazi ukuba uYehova uya kulifeza Ityala losizana,  ibango lamahlwempu.</li>
      <li>Inene, amalungisa aya kubulela kwigama lakho; Baya kuhlala ebusweni bakho abathe tye.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Umhobe kaDavide. Yehova, ndiyakunqula, khawuleza uze kum; Libekele indlebe izwi lam ekudandulukeni kwam kuwe.</li>
      <li>Umthandazo wam mawuhlale uhleli phambi kwakho usisiqhumiso, Nokuphakamisa kwam izandla kube ngumnikelo wangokuhlwa.</li>
      <li>Umlomo wam wumisele umlindi, Yehova; Misa umgcini emnyango womlomo wam.</li>
      <li>Intliziyo yam musa ukuyithobela entweni embi, Ukuba isebenze intlondi yokungendawo Namadoda asebenza ubutshinga;  Mandingazidli izimnandi zawo.</li>
      <li>Malindibethe ilungisa linenceba, lindohlwaye; Ioli enjalo yentloko ayingeyali intloko yam: Ngokuba usekho nomthandazo wam ebubini bawo.</li>
      <li>Bakhahlelwa emacaleni engxondorha abagwebi bawo, Beve amazwi am ukuba amnandi.</li>
      <li>Njengolimayo enqika umhlaba, Anjalo ukuthi saa amathambo ethu emlonyeni wengcwaba.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba akuwe, Yehova, Nkosi yam, amehlo am; Ndizimela ngawe; musa ukuwuphalaza umphefumlo wam.</li>
      <li>Ndigcine esangweni lomgibe wabandithiyelayo,  Nasezirhintyelweni zabasebenza ubutshinga.</li>
      <li>Mabeyele ezintanjeni zabo abangendawo, Ndide ndidlule mna okukanye.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Eyokuqiqa kaDavide; oko ebesemqolombeni. Umthandazo.  Ndikhala kuYehova ngezwi lam, Ndikhunga uYehova ngezwi lam,</li>
      <li>Ndiphalaza inkalazo yam phambi kwakhe, Ndixela imbandezelo yam phambi kwakhe.</li>
      <li>Ekutyhafeni komoya phakathi kwam, Uyayazi wena ingqushu yam. Emendweni endihamba ngawo Bandiqhushekela isibatha.</li>
      <li>Bheka ngasekunene ubone, Akukho undibukayo; Andinandawo ndingasabela kuyo, Akukho uwukhathaleleyo umphefumlo wam.</li>
      <li>Ndikhala kuwe, Yehova, Ndithi, Nguwe ihlathi lam, Isabelo sam ezweni labahleliyo.</li>
      <li>Kubazele indlebe ukuhlahlamba kwam, Ngokuba ndiswele kakhulu: Ndihlangule kwabandisukelayo, Ngokuba bomelele kunam.</li>
      <li>Wukhuphe entolongweni umphefumlo wam, Ndibulele kwigama lakho. Amalungisa aya kuzithi jize ngesithsaba ngenxa yam,  Ngokuba undiphethe kakuhle.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Umhobe kaDavide. Yehova, yiva umthandazo wam, kubekele indlebe ukutarhuzisa kwam; Ndiphendule ngokunyaniseka kwakho,  ngobulungisa bakho.</li>
      <li>Musa ukumsa ematyaleni umkhonzi wakho: Ngokuba phambi kwakho akukho namnye uhleliyo olilungisa.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba utshaba luwusukele umphefumlo wam, Lubutyumzele emhlabeni ubomi bam; Lundihlalise ezindaweni ezimnyama,  njengabafe ngonaphakade.</li>
      <li>Utyhafile phakathi kwam umoya wam; Imangalisiwe phakathi kwam intliziyo yam.</li>
      <li>Ndikhumbula imihla yamandulo; Ndicamngca ngemisebenzi yakho yonke, Ndicamngca ngesenzo sezandla zakho.</li>
      <li>Ndizolulela kuwe izandla zam, Umphefumlo wam ukungxamele njengelizwe elibharhileyo. (Phakamisani.)</li>
      <li>Khawuleza undiphendule, Yehova; uyaphela umoya wam. Musa ukubusithelisa kum ubuso bakho, Ndifane nabahla baye emhadini.</li>
      <li>Ndivise kwakusasa inceba yakho, Ngokuba ndikholose ngawe.  Ndazise indlela endiya kuhamba ngayo: Ngokuba ndiwuphakamisela kuwe umphefumlo wam.</li>
      <li>Ndihlangule ezintshabeni zam, Yehova. Ndizimela ngawe.</li>
      <li>Ndifundise ukwenza ikholo lakho, ngokuba unguThixo wam.  UMoya wakho olungileyo makandikhaphele ezweni elisithabazi.</li>
      <li>Ngenxa yegama lakho, Yehova, ndiphilise; Wukhuphe embandezelweni umphefumlo wam ngobulungisa bakho.</li>
      <li>Ngenceba yakho zibhangise iintshaba zam, Ubatshabalalise bonke abawubandezelayo umphefumlo wam, Ngokuba ndingumkhonzi wakho.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>EkaDavide. Makabongwe uYehova, uliwa lam, Ulofundisa izandla zam ukulwa, Iminwe yam imfazwe.</li>
      <li>Unceba yam, umboniselo yam, Ungxonde yam, umsindisi wam,  mna lo; Ungweletshetshe yam, undizimela ngaye; Ulonyathelela abantu bam phantsi kwam.</li>
      <li>Yehova, uyintoni na umntu, le nto umaziyo? Unyana womfo,  le nto umnyamekelayo?</li>
      <li>Umntu lo ufana nomphunga, Imihla yakhe injengethunzi elidlulayo.</li>
      <li>Yehova, thoba amazulu akho, uhle; Phatha ezintabeni,  ziqhume.</li>
      <li>Banekisa imibane, uziphangalalise; Thuma iintolo zakho,  uziduba-dube.</li>
      <li>Thuma izandla zakho, zivele phezulu; Ndirhole, ndihlangule emanzini amakhulu. Esandleni soonyana bolunye uhlanga;</li>
      <li>Abamlomo uthetha inkohlakalo, Abasandla sokunene sisesokunene sobuxoki.</li>
      <li>Thixo, ndokuvumela ingoma entsha, Ndikubethele umrhubhe ontambo zilishumi;</li>
      <li>Ulonika ookumkani usindiso, Ulohlangula uDavide umkhonzi wakhe ekreleni elinobubi.</li>
      <li>Ndirhole, ndihlangule esandleni soonyana bolunye uhlanga,  Abamlomo uthetha inkohlakalo, Abasandla sokunene sisesokunene sobuxoki;</li>
      <li>Baze oonyana bethu babe njengezityalo ezikhulileyo ebutsheni babo; Iintombi zethu zibe njengeembombo ezivathisiweyo ngeemfakamfele ngokokwakhiwa kwebhotwe;</li>
      <li>Oovimba bethu bazale, bavelise iintlobo ngeentlobo;  Iigusha zethu zizale amawaka, zande ngezigidi emaphandleni ethu;</li>
      <li>Iinkomo zethu zizale, Kungabikho kungenelwa, kungabikho kuthinjwa, Kungabikho kuhlahlamba ezitratweni zethu.</li>
      <li>Hayi, uyolo lwabantu ekunjalo kubo! Hayi, uyolo lwabantu abaThixo unguYehova!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Eyokudumisa kaDavide. Ndiya kukuphakamisa, Thixo wam,  wena Kumkani, Ndilibonge igama lakho ngonaphakade kanaphakade.</li>
      <li>Imihla yonke ndiya kukubonga, Ndilidumise igama lakho ngonaphakade kanaphakade.</li>
      <li>Mkhulu uYehova, ngowokudunyiswa kakhulu; Ubukhulu bakhe abunakugocwagocwa.</li>
      <li>Izizukulwana ngezizukulwana, kunconywa izenzo zakho,  Kuxelwe ubugorha bakho.</li>
      <li>Bunobungangamela ubuqaqawuli bendili yakho; Ngeendawo zakho ezibalulekileyo ndiya kucamngca.</li>
      <li>Bothetha ngamandla ezenzo zakho ezoyikekayo, Ndibalise ngobukhulu bakho.</li>
      <li>Bompompoza isikhumbuzo sokulunga kwakho okukhulu,  Bamemelele ngobulungisa bakho.</li>
      <li>Unobabalo nemfesane uYehova, Uzeka kade umsindo, mkhulu ngenceba.</li>
      <li>Ulungile uYehova kubo bonke, Imfesane yakhe ikuzo zonke izenzo zakhe.</li>
      <li>Ziyabulela kuwe, Yehova, zonke izenzo zakho, Bakubonge abakho benceba;</li>
      <li>Uzuko lobukumkani bakho balutsho, Bathethe ngobugorha bakho.</li>
      <li>Ukuba babazise oonyana babantu ubugorha bakhe,  Ubuqaqawuli obuhle bobukumkani bakhe.</li>
      <li>Ubukumkani bakho bubukumkani bamaphakade onke, Nolawulo lwakho lukwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana.</li>
      <li>UYehova ungumxhasi wabo bonke abawayo, Ngumphakamisi wabo bonke abagobileyo.</li>
      <li>Amehlo eento zonke akhangele kuwe, Wena ke uzinika ukudla kwazo ngexesha elililo;</li>
      <li>Uyasivula isandla sakho, Uzihluthise iinto zonke eziphilileyo ngeento ezikholekileyo.</li>
      <li>Ulilungisa uYehova ngeendlela zakhe zonke, Unenceba ngezenzo zakhe zonke.</li>
      <li>Usondele uYehova kubo bonke abamnqulayo, Kubo bonke abamnqulayo ngenyaniso.</li>
      <li>Uyayenza into ekholekileyo kwabamoyikayo, Akuve ukuzibika kwabo, abasindise.</li>
      <li>UYehova ungumgcini wabo bonke abamthandayo,  Abatshabalalise bonke abangendawo.</li>
      <li>Umlomo wam mawuthethe indumiso kaYehova, Inyama yonke ilibonge igama lakhe elingcwele ngonaphakade kanaphakade.</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Haleluya! Mdumise uYehova, mphefumlo wam.</li>
      <li>Ndiya kumdumisa uYehova lo gama ndidla ubomi; Ndiya kumbethela uhadi uThixo wam ekubeni ndingosekhoyo.</li>
      <li>Musani ukukholosa ngamanene, Ngonyana womntu, yena ungenalo usindiso.</li>
      <li>Uyaphuma umoya wakhe, abuyele yena emhlabeni wakhe; Ngaloo mini ayatshitsha amabhongo akhe.</li>
      <li>Hayi, uyolo lwalowo uluncedo lunguThixo kaYakobi, Lwalowo ulinde kuYehova uThixo wakhe:</li>
      <li>KuMenzi wezulu nomhlaba, Nolwandle neento zonke ezikulo;  Kulogcina inyaniso ngonaphakade;</li>
      <li>Kogweba ityala labacudiswayo; Kopha abalambileyo ukudla;  KuYehova okhulula ababanjwa;</li>
      <li>KuYehova ovula amehlo eemfama; KuYehova ophakamisa abagobileyo; KuYehova othanda amalungisa;</li>
      <li>KuYehova ogcina abaphambukeli; Kulophakamisa inkedama nomhlolokazi, Ayiphethule indlela yabangendawo.</li>
      <li>UYehova ungukumkani ngonaphakade, UThixo wakho, Ziyon,  kwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana. Haleluya!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Haleluya! Ngokuba kulungile ukuvuma ngoThixo wethu;  Ngokuba kumnandi, ifanelekile indumiso.</li>
      <li>Umakhi weYerusalem nguYehova; Abagxothwa bakwaSirayeli ubabuthela khona.</li>
      <li>Ulophilisa abaphuke intliziyo, Abophe amanxeba abo;</li>
      <li>Ulobala inani leenkwenkwezi, Ezibiza zonke ngamagama.</li>
      <li>Inkulu iNkosi yethu, inamandla amakhulu; Ingqondo yayo ayiphele ndawo.</li>
      <li>Ulophakamisa abalulamileyo nguYehova, Uthobela abangendawo emhlabeni.</li>
      <li>Hlabelani kuYehova eyokubulela, Mbetheleni uhadi uThixo wethu.</li>
      <li>Ulosibekelisa izulu ngamafu, Ulolungisela umhlaba imvula;  Ulontshulisa utyani ezintabeni;</li>
      <li>Ulonika inkomo ukudla, Namathole ehlungulu alilayo.</li>
      <li>Akabunanze nganto ubugorha behashe, Akakholiswa zizitho zendoda;</li>
      <li>UYehova ukholiswa ngabamoyikayo, Abalinde inceba yakhe.</li>
      <li>Mncome uYehova, Yerusalem. Mdumise uThixo wakho, Ziyon:</li>
      <li>Ngokuba eyomelezile imivalo yamasango akho, Ebasikelele abantwana bakho phakathi kwakho.</li>
      <li>Ngulomisa uxolo emideni yakho, Wakuhluthisa ngengqolowa etyebileyo.</li>
      <li>Ulothumela intetho yakhe ehlabathini, Ilizwi lakhe ligidima ngokukhawuleza;</li>
      <li>Ulonika ikhephu njengoboya bezimvu, Ugcwayela iqabaka njengothuthu,</li>
      <li>Ephosa umkhenkce wakhe njengamaqhekeza; Ngubani na onokuma phambi kwengqele yakhe?</li>
      <li>Uthumela ilizwi lakhe, ezo nto azinyibilikise; Uvuthuzisa umoya wakhe, aqukuqele amanzi.</li>
      <li>Uloxelela uYakobi ilizwi lakhe, USirayeli imimiselo yakhe namasiko akhe.</li>
      <li>Akenjanga ngalo kolunye uhlanga, Namasiko aluwazi.  Haleluya!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Haleluya! Dumisani uYehova emazulwini; Mdumiseni ezindaweni eziphezulu.</li>
      <li>Mdumiseni, nonke zithunywa zakhe; Mdumiseni, nonke mikhosi yakhe;</li>
      <li>Mdumiseni, wena langa, nawe nyanga; Mdumiseni, nonke zinkwenkwezi zinokukhanya;</li>
      <li>Mdumiseni, mazulu awo amazulu, Nani, manzi angaphezu kwezulu.</li>
      <li>Mazilidumise ezo nto igama likaYehova; Ngokuba wawisa umthetho, zadalwa.</li>
      <li>Wazimisa ngonaphakade kanaphakade, Wazimisela ummiselo ezingayi kuwugqitha.</li>
      <li>Dumisani uYehova ehlabathini, Nina bominenga, nani nonke,  manzi enzonzobila:</li>
      <li>Wena mlilo, nawe sichotho; wena khephu, nawe msi; Moya uvuthuzayo, ulenzayo ilizwi lakhe;</li>
      <li>Nina zintaba, nani zinduli nonke, Nina mithi eneziqhamo,  nani misedare nonke;</li>
      <li>Nina marhamncwa, nani zinkomo nonke, Nina zinambuzane,  nani zintaka zinamaphiko;</li>
      <li>Ookumkani behlabathi, nezizwe zonke, Abathetheli nabagwebi behlabathi lonke;</li>
      <li>Umlisela kwanomthinjana, Amadoda amakhulu kunye nabafana:</li>
      <li>Mabalidumise igama likaYehova, Ngokuba liyingxonde igama lakhe yena yedwa; Indili yakhe ingaphezu komhlaba nezulu.</li>
      <li>Wabaphakamisela abantu bakhe uphondo, Lwayindumiso kwabakhe benceba bonke, Koonyana bakaSirayeli, abantu abasondeleyo kuye. Haleluya!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Haleluya! Mvumeleni uYehova ingoma entsha, Indumiso yakhe ebandleni labenceba.</li>
      <li>USirayeli makavuye ngoMenzi wakhe; Usapho lwaseZiyon malugcobe ngoKumkani walo.</li>
      <li>Mabalidumise igama lakhe beqamba, Bembethela ingqongqo nohadi.</li>
      <li>Ngokuba uYehova uyakholiswa ngabantu bakhe, Uyabahombisa abalulamileyo ngoloyiso.</li>
      <li>Mabadlamke benozuko abenceba, Mabamemelele besezililini zabo.</li>
      <li>Yimibongo kaThixo emqaleni wabo, Likrele elintlangothi mbini esandleni sabo;</li>
      <li>Ukuze benze impindezelo ezintlangeni, Izohlwayo ezizweni;</li>
      <li>Bakhonkxe ookumkani bazo ngemixokelelwane, Nabazukileyo kuzo ngamakhamandela esinyithi;</li>
      <li>Benze kubo isiko elibhaliweyo. Luzuko olo lwabakhe benceba bonke. Haleluya!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
  <li>
    <ol>
      <li>Haleluya! Dumisani uThixo engcweleni yakhe, Mdumiseni esibhakabhakeni samandla akhe.</li>
      <li>Mdumiseni ngenxa yobugorha bakhe, Mdumiseni ngokobuninzi bobukhulu bakhe.</li>
      <li>Mdumiseni ngokuvuthela isigodlo, Mdumiseni ngomrhubhe nohadi.</li>
      <li>Mdumiseni ngengqongqo nengqungqo, Mdumiseni ngeento ezineentambo nogwali.</li>
      <li>Mdumiseni ngamacangci akhenkcezayo, Mdumiseni ngamacangci adumayo.</li>
      <li>Yonke into ephefumlayo mayimdumise uYehova. Haleluya!</li>
    </ol>
  </li>
</ol>
